yt speke brute shall shewed ye lode englod wos fyrst namd albio ccheso vos namit nobull land sirrie ther wos nobull kyng myghty gret renoe wos called dieclisian yt wel wortheli gou er ned ruled thurgh noble chiualri quered landes hym almost kynges world hym entedat hit fell th dioclisian spoused getill damisell wos wod er fair emes dought er labana loued hym reson wold gat vpo xxxiij doughtres wich eldest wos called albine thees damiselles whan come vn age bicomen fair wos voder wher dioclisian anoe let make asompnyng comaunded lettres kynges helden hym shold cum certain day lett er coteyned make riall fest pat wich day thider coen brought hem amirallis prince duke nobull chiualrie fest wos rialy arayed ther leued ioye myrthe ynough wos wond er wit befeell thus dioclisian thought marie doughtres among altho kynges tho solempnite spakene ded albine eldest doughter hir sustres richely maried vn xxxiij kynges lordes gret honour pouer solempnyte solempnite wos done eu er kyng toke wyf lad ther cotre ther maad hem quenes befell thus afterward dame albine bicome stoute sterne told lytell pris lord hym scorne desspyt wolde nat done butt wold haue hir owne dyuerse matres hir sustres euerychone bere euel ayenst ther lordes wondyr wytt moch thought ther husbondes nought hy age comen ther fadre tho kynges ther lordes wold haue chastized fair maner vpon loue frendshipp shold amend ther lith er dycions wos nought diden ther wyll thyng liked poer wher tho xxxiij kyng vpon tyme often time beten ther wyfes wened wold amended ther tatches ther wilkednes bot soche codicions fair speche warnyng didden wors betynges eft sone mochel wers wher kyng wedded albine wrot tach dicions wyf albin letter sent dioclision hir fadre whe kyng herd albines lord sent lett er dioclisian anone sent lettres enseled ther seales dicions tach ther wyfes pwhen kyng dioclisian saw herd many playntes doughtres wos sore ashamed become wond er angre wroth toward doughtres thought bothe nyght day yf tho myght mend misded anone sent lettres vn xxxiij kynges shold cu hym bring hem wyfes eu er ychone certane day wold ther chastise hem ther wikkednesse yf myght maner wise kyng comen tyme day tho wos sette bitwene hym kyng dioclisian vnd er song moche honour maad solepne feste al vnd er lordshipp thrid day aft er solepnite kyng dioclisian sent aft er xxxiij doughtres shold cum speke hym hys chambre war come spake vn ther wikkednes ther cruelte spituesly hem reued vndernam hem said yf wold nat chastised shold loue lese eu er lady herden come abasshed gretli aschamed ther fadre said wold make amendes deted ther fadres chambre dame albine wos eldest suster lad hem hir chambre tho made void wer theryn lefe wos among hem hir sustres yfere tho sayd albine faire sustres wel know kyng fadre v hath reproued shamed despyseed enchesone make v obedient vn owr housbandes certes shall neu er while leue sith come hier kyng blod myn housbond whan th said hir sustres said tho saied albine full well wot fair sustres owr housbandes plened vn fader vpo v wherfor hath v th soule reproued despised wherfor sustres counsell nyght housbandes bene bedde one assent cutten hir throtes may bene pee hem better moo doo thing vnder fadres power ower ell anone ladis consented grated thys cosell nyght wos coyn lordd lady went bedde anone ther lordes slepe cutte heir housbondes throtes flow dioclisian kyng fadre herd thing bicome hugeli wroth ayenst doughtres anoe wold hem haue brenet pbut al baron lordes sirrie couceilled doo suche stretnes owne doughtres bot onli shold voyde lond eu er neu er shuld com ayene dyde pand dioclisian wos ther fadre anoe co maunded gone shypp deliu er ed hem vitailles half yere whan wos done sustren went ship sailed forth see bitoke ther frendes appolyn wos ther god long thee sailed see till last come arreued yle wos wyldernesse dame albion wos come lond hir sustres thys albine went frest forth shypp saied hir sustres moche oldest suster copany fyrst land haue take moche o nam albine lond called albio aft er myn name anoe al hir sustres grated hir good wyll tho vet al ye sustres ye ship toke lond albion hir suster cald ther went vp downe fonde nether ne woma ne child wyld bestes diuerse kyndes ther vitalles war dispended thei failled fedde wyth herbes frutes seson yere leued best myght aftee token flessh dyuerse bestes bycame wonder fat desired mannys compane manys kynde hem failled hete woxen wonder coragious kynd desired manys companie eny othyr solace myrthe whan deuel ceuyd went dyuerse contreys nome bodi eir likyng nature shad men come lande albion lay thoo wyme shad tho nature vpon consaued broght forth geantys wich one wos called gogmagog langherigan wer named diuerse name nad maner come forth wer borne horrible geantes albion duelled caues hylles ther wyll londe albion lyked vn tyme brut arriued come totnes wos yle albion ther brute conquered skomfited thes geantes aboue sayd phere geneth brut goten slewe fyrst moder fader conquered albion named bretan owne name called englond name engist saxonie thys brute cam bretan bowte xviij yeer hely knaw nobull cite greet troy theer wos nobull knyght man grete pouer wos called eneas cite troy lost destroed thurgh grece eneas al meyne fled then comei lumbardy tho wos lord gou er nour lond kyng wos called latyne nother kyng ther wos wos called turocelyne strongli wered vpo kyng latyne often tymes hym moche harme whe kyng latyne herd eneas comen vnd er feng hym wyth mochel honour hym helde moche herd hym wist well wos nobull knyght worthy hys body hiy dedes eneas helpet kyng latyne shortly tell well worthely slew turocelyne discomfited hym pepull al wos done kyng latyne yaf lond wos turocelinis thys noble man eneas mariage lauyne doughter faire creature man wist lyued geder ioye myrthe dayes theyr lyfes tyme asconyus son eneas wedded wyfe vpo hyr begat son wos called silueyn silueyn whan colde sum resun man vn wittyng fadre yenst wyll acquentyd hym damysell wos cosyn lauyne wos kyng latynes dougter quene wos eneas wyfe brought damysell wyth chylde whon ascanius fad er wist anone let enquere wisest master grettest klerkes chyld damisey shold bring forth ansuered sayed shold bring ofrth son shold kyll bothe fadre also modre moder dyed beryng hym whan chyld wos borne fad er let calle hym brute master siyd shold doo moche harme sorow mony dyuerse place shold come gret honour worshyp kyng ascanius dyed god wold silueyn son resaued lond made hym wonderly well beloued amonges pepull whan brute thatt wos siluenus son wos xv yere olde went vpon day wythe fadre play solace brute shold shote vn hert hys harew myshapped glaced ther brutkel led fad er phow brute wos dreuen lond helde hym grece myschance befell pepull lond made sorow ynowgh war sore angreyd encheson therof driuen brute oute lond wold suffer hym amonges saugh myght ther bide went then grece ther fond vijm men lynage kynred troy wor come gret blode stori telleth men wome child wich wer holden thraldom bondage kyng pandras grece deth achilles wos bitrayed slayn troy thys brute wos wonder fayr man strong huge age glad cheyr sembland also worthy body wos wellbeloued emonges pepule kyng pandras herde speke goodnes condicions anone made hym duell hym brute bicome wond er priue moch beloued kyng long tyme brute duelled kyng last troy brute spakyn gedre kynred lynage acquantance ther plened vn brute ther sorow ther bondage mony sh me ye kyng pandros done brute sayn vpon tyme ye ben lord linage strong man myghty ye ou captayn lord gou er nour wyll cume commandmentes done maner thinges bryng ye v oute wrecchitnes bandage wil fyght wyth kyng trouth wt ye grace gret god shall hym ouercome shall make kyng lond done homage shall holde euermore brute tho gret pite ther bondage brought yn preuely went hem kynges court tho troy put wodis montaygens helde sent vn kyng pandros shuld yeue leu sauely wend lond wold longer duelle bondage kyng pandras wax tho sore annoyd tho swore wold slae eu er ychone ordeneyd grett pouer went towardes feght brute men manli defended fersly foughten kylled al kynges men none ascaped token kyng hym helde prison ordeyned counsell bi tweyn mygth done su said shuld put deth su said shuld exiled lond su said shuld brent pand tho spake wyse knyght called mempris said brute tho troy yf kyng padras wold yelde hym haue lyfe councell yeue vn brute duke soferayne doughter gennogen wyfe mariage hyr hondreth shippes wel araied hys tresour gold siluer corne wyne moch o nedeth haue thyng go oute lond ordayn v land elles ne none kynred comen v shall neuer haue pee lond amonges grece haue slayn mony ther kynghtes frendes euermore contake shold amonges v brut tho folke consented well counsell thyng tolden kyng padras hee haue lyfe graunted moch axid none yaf vn brute gennogen douter wyfe hudreth shippes o myche o neded vitalles o befor wos ordenyd brute tho toke wife men soke lond grece went vn see wynd wedre ther wyll com thrid day ile wos called lorgres brute anone sent lond aspye man er contre found nold cite al wasted forlet na therynne nether ne woman ne thyng duelling mydell cite founden old tempull feier lady yt wos called diane goddesse come ayene vn brut told hym seyn found coselled hym gone doo sacrifice vn dame dian woned yef ansuer thyng yt eu er men prayed hir namli vn yt hir honoured wt sacrifice brut wet yt ymage sayd diane noble goddest lady yt thyng hast myght thy pouer wyndes water wodes feldes al thyng world man er bestes yt ther ben make prayer yt ye cocell tell wher place shall haue counabull duellyng pepull ther shall make honor welfaier tempyll nobull wher ye shall eu er honoured done praer diane ansuerd man er brute go eue forth thy wey ou er see fraunce toward west ther ye shall find ile yt called albion yt ile bicompassed ye see may cu theri bot bene shippes yt lond wer woed geantes bot bot wyldernes lond destenyed ordant yow pepull phow coryn becoe brute kig goffar wos discofid brute hade ansuere diane goddesse anoe let ancres wynd vp sayled high see whe men sailed xx dayes mo fond fast beside cost see thousand lynage kynred troy ther souerayne ther mast er called corin whan brute wist whennes weer tho toke moch ioye shippis led forth hym corin ther becoe brute hym dyd homage long sailled forth yt se till come gascoyne anoe arriued hauen liegers ther duellid viij dayes rest ther sayles amende ther wos nede tydyng sone come kig goffar lord lond yt moch pepill strange lond arreuid lond hauen liegers wherfor hee sore angreyd anoyde come arriued lond lysens leue anone ordeyned hym gret pouer dryue brute shend pepull bout kyng goffar wos discomfited pepull hym self flede fraunce ther seke helpe socour pand tyme regned fraunce xij kynges xi assemaled gret pouer help goffar fight ayenes brute goffar duelle fraunce halfe yere mene tyme goffar fraunce brute hys companye destruyed lond gascoyne let take tresour kyng goffar ther let bryng shippes brute founden lond fair place couenabull theyr brute made faire castell strong pwhen wos done kyng goffar come fro fraunce xi kynges hym brought xx men fyght wt brute compani brute vijm iijc men neuerthelees ij hostes mett gedre brute folke thorgh help hym selfe turyn cosyn corin well manly hym defended fought tell lytell tym kylled fraunshemen ijm mo anon tho alyue fled way pand batell turin brute cosyn slayn brute let enteer hym worthely whan space leyser castell made tho let call castell tour cause name turin ther wos entyred yet day ther nobull cite c lled tour kyng goffar wist turin wos deyd co ayene men yaf strong batell vn brute bot brute hys men wery fighttyng myght longer endure bot meegre hym brute went castell men made yates fast saue take consell amonges brute corin yaf counsell ordeyned corin priualy shold goo oute bussh hym wod til morne mornyng whan brute shold fight enymys corin shold cum folke one side sla harme myght amornyng dauyng day brute went castell faught enmys fersly defendid bot litell tyme brute folke slew viijc gofears men come corin busshement smot ground compani wold stond byed kyng goffar comp nye war descomfited fast gun fle brute corin ther companye fersly persoed gogmagog master geantes wos stronger heyr ony brute keped hym encheson shold wrestyll corin brute wos gretter hyer ony brute men thee gredyl sted vpward pgogmagog corin vndir toke ther wrestyll gedre went wrestilled long tyme last gogmagog held corin fast brake ij ribbbes side wherfor corin wos sore angri ther toke gogmagog betwix armes kest hym doune vpon roche gogmagog brak peces died euell deth therfor place called yit vn day faut gogmagog brute yaf cuntre vn corin ther corin called name cornwalle men called cornwailles shuld men contre called eu er contre duelled corin thee made tounes sonny one slew haue heritage ydoyne ther modre killed thatt wherfor land destruied gorbodian deid ij sonys yt become stout proude eu er wered ged er ye land one called ferres porres ferres wold haue small peces herd eu er suche cursed mod er yt kyllid hir owne handes hir son long tyme aft er last reproue shame mod er yt enchesun one son murdred lost bothe phow iiij kynges courtasly held breten ther name ye shall heyr ij brethern war deid nad left behynd nother son ne dought er ne noe kynred yt myght haue ye heritage moch ye strangest driue scomfited ye feblest toke ther londes eu er cotre gret strife vnd er emong thynges ther amoges ye contre ou er come tho thurgh ther myght strenght tuke ye londes eu er tok c er tayn cotre contre let call hi kyng con cald scater wos kig scotland yt wos called dawaliere kig loegers land wos lotrins thatt wos brute son thrid called rudac kyng walis iiij called cloten kig cornewaill cloten shold haue land reson cause thar wos wist noe right heir o butt strongest set litell bi hem wer lesse estate therfor clote nomore lad amog hem cornwaill pof kyng donebant clotens son wone lond cloten son yt called doneband deth fadre come hardy man fair curteys passed king fairnes worthenesse none knyght wist well fader lyued rightfull heir lod shold haue reson kynges moch strength toke hym lond pand aft er ward doneband ordeyned gret pouer conquered fyrst land logeris aft er wold haue conquered land scotland wailles scat came yaf batell rudac come ayene walys men help hym fell rudac wos kylled also scater playn bataill doneband victorie conquerid land well maintined pee quiete neuir befor well mayntined phow doneband frist kyng euer bore croune gold bretan thys doneband let make hym croune gold wered croune vpon hede neu er kig bifore ordyened statut man done neu er moch harme myght come tempull ther shold man hym mysdo gone ther safete pee aft er goin lond cutre hym plesed owt ony harme ony man sett hond vpon hym shold lese life doneband made toun malmesberi toune also vise regned well worthely xl yere died lyeth new troy phow bronne belin deted bitweyn lond deth doneband ther fadre twix aft er yt doneband wos deid sonys yt deted land bitweyn ther fad er ordeyned yt belyn eldest son ye land bretan humbar southward brotherbrenne land humber scotlad moch beli better part brenne therfor waxed wroth wold haue lond belyn brother wold greunte hym nomore wherfor cotake roso betweyn two brenne yonger brother myght ne strenght yen belyn therfor brenne thurgh cosell hys folke wet fro then norwey kyng olsinges prayd help socour coquer brenne shold hir haue hir lede hym eu er shold lese hir myght sake brenne whan gutlagh herd tydig lay aspy brenne mony shippis myght haue two fletes metten gedre long tyme faught brenne turned ayene wer discomfited kyng gutlagh toke samye put hir shyppe brenne sham fulli fled then man discomfitied pand kyng gutlagh wold haue went owne contre ther come vpon hi sych gret tempest v dayes lasted thurgh tempast wos driuen breten iij shippis mo tho keped costes see toke gutlagh samye folke presented belyn belyn put preson phow belyn drofe land kyng gutlagh de marke samye hit long brenne come son foor saied come vn ladyes howse absent hir howsbond logig wer slepe rose suerde hond wt strengthe feir rauychid woma whe wos go ye nexte day aft er send vn hir fadre hir housbond gret kynne thus saied vn pthis kyng son come heder o freynd mystrist thus defilyt chastyte lost name eu er hir frendys se hyr wepe petuysly coplayn coforthid hir o cold saied wos velany vn hir wos ayenes hir answered rose exiled kig eu er geny th see sit thes kynges rome neu er wos none pof gou er nan rome till emours gan aftyr tyrant wos deid roman ordeyned yt ther shuld neu er kyng rome bot wold bi gou er ned fro yt forth bi consules whe tho kiges regned cc yere xl made statute yt ij consules shuld chosen shuld goueren cite peepull cause thes tow wor chosen yf wold make excesse thee shuld gou er ne ther wos thyng obeyed bot yf cosented also shuld stond ther dignite passyng yere cause dominacio long tyme shuld vsurpe vpo wos righfull tyme empyre rome dilatid passyng xij myell ne lordshipp passing xij myell fyrst consules yt wer made called luciu brutu thes two gret thig ther tyme yet pepull bare heuy ther dominacion wher foor chose man wich shuld haue auctorite thei clepeed hym dictator pin tym lix et ante cristi natitate vc xl zorobobell comandment god founded tempil made fite bot wos long vt p patet esdre aftir pepull ierusale come fro babulon thes ij ruyled ihesus hee prest o gou er nour zorobobell duke thys maner gydyng kepid vn herodes tyme hee prestis shuld principall dukis vnd er bot duke wos eu er tribe iuda prophesi iacob vnd er good gydyng prestis rede pepull haue recedit fro varay truthe faythe afoor tyme iues kyngis mony tymes ran ydolatry esdras prest kynrad aron tyme excedid holynes throgh who gret wisdo iues stait holpin cambises son ciri regned kyngdom persa rum wich commaunded myghtili tempull ierusalem shold bildid ayene fadre comandid shold byldid cambises made cursed iuge fleid hilt lyue mad son sit fad er skyn thurgh drede shold drid falshed iuge rightwisli pthis cambises mony namys holx scriptur boke esdri artharxerses assuorus historia iudith yt wasdoon vnd er hi called nabogodonosor olifernes prince cheualry subdued mony landes lord last come vn bethelem ther wos slayn iudit woman vt p patet iuddith et ereneides regned persis half yere darius regned perses wich bi mocion zorobobell comaundid thee werke ye tepull take ayene maunded prince wise shuld let bot shuld help yt could vide plra esdre ho de ho tepore abiguu pp diu er sitate docto rum circa annu mudi iiijm vijc xxxiiij et xpi nati iiijc lxv abiuth son zorobobell ye lyne crist wos macha man v sone loue vn god wos bishop israel bot iij sone wer iudas machabe wos bishop iij yere wos son mathathias macabe named yt eu er wos israell wich neu er none like hym foor ne aft er wos fre ei libro macha antioch epiphanes son antioch myghty tyme kyng syrry heed vn fort wt cursed therfor figured antecrist moy mart er cruelly made falsly disposid hym entyr egipt fad er bot obtened tribute thurgh strength haue kyng kyng gynder armager brether assembled gedired gret host yfere briton yaf bataell emprour claudius kylled roman gret plente emprour afterward one wos called hamon saw ther pepull theer whaerfast slayn preuali kest way armes toke armes ed breton armed armuro come batell kyng sayed maner syr ye good hert goddis loue roman enmys anone shall slayn discumfited euerychon kyng yaf kepe vn wordes ne speche armes yt vpon hym wened briton tratour eu er held hym next kyng preualy vnder shulders armes smot kyng wherfor deid fell doune erthe whan armag er saw brother deid caste away armes toke hym brother armes come botaill among briton bad hertely fight fast lay doune roman armes wened kyng gynd afore wos slayn wyst begone britans fersly fight kyld roman last emprour soke felde flede fast o myght folke wynchestre fals traitour hamon slayn kyng fast anone gan fle hast myght armager kynges brother pursued full fersly fers hert drofe hym vn water ther toke hym anone smot bothe hand hede foot hewed body peces tho let cast water wherfor water called hamanus hauen afterward ther made fayr toune yet standeth yt called southamton afterward armager went wynchestre seke claudius cesar emprour rome ther armager hym toke claudius emprour thurgh concel roman left lyue made pee armager maner ye shall say claudius emprour shuld yeue vn armager gennen fair doughter haue wife land fro tyme forward shuld empreurs poer rome uppon suche conueant neuer afterward emprour rome shuld take none tribute land bot feaulte wer acorded vpon conand claudius cesar sent reme doughter gennen wos comen claudi cesar yaf hir armager wife armag er spoused hir london mych solempnite myrth tho armager crouned made kig britan pof kyng armager whose tyme sent petre preched antiochie apostoles diu er se cuntreis armager regned well worthely lond gou er ned claudius cesar remembrans acord reu er ence honour dought er made lond fair toune castell let call toune name claucestren called gloucestre wos done emprour toke leue tho went rome armager tho kyng gou er ned lond well nobely life tyme armag er gat son wife thatt wos called westmer while armager regned sent petre preched antioche ther made nobull chyrche wich sat fyrst chair ther dwelled vij yere aft er went rome made pope till nero emprour let martir tho preched opanly apposteles diu er se landes right fayeth armager regned xxiiij yere died lieth london phow kyng westmer yaf berynger yland forlet ther berynger made toun berewike armager regned son westmer wos good man worthy body well gou er ned land hit befell tydyng come day king rodrik gascoine come land houge host pepull wos duellyng staynsmore kyng westmer herd tho tydynges let assemble houge host britans come kyng rodrik yaf hym batall kyng westmer kylled rodrik hondes playn batall whe kyng rodrikes men saw ther lord wos deid yolden kyng westmer bicome men eu er yaf cotre wos forleten wher myght duell thed er wet duelled ther ther life tyme ixc men ther mo left batell ther gou er ner prince wos called beringer began toun yt myght ther duell haue resoorte let call toune birewyke vpo twede ther duelled become riche woman amonges breton wold yef ther doughtres thestrangers wherfor went ower see irland brought woman ther spoused men koud nat vnd er stond ther langage ne speche thes woman therfor spoken geder scottes aft er ward thurgh changyng tber lanhages fraunce war called tho scottet shulde folke cuntre called euer phow kyng westmer let arere stone entring westmerland ther slew rodrik ther begon fyrst housing aft er bataill aboue saied whe rodrik wos deid kyng westmer remebrance victorie let arere ther sydes way gret stone hygh yet hit standeth eu er shall stand let graue stone lettres yt th saied kyng westmer britonne killed place rodrik hys emmny pand westmer fyrst bylded house toune westmerland yt stone begieth westmerlond yt westmer let call aft er name pand whe westmer done duelled lyfes tyme contre westmerlod loued cutre ony cotre regned xxv yere died lieth carleill pof kyng coill wos westmer son held lond pee life tyme kyng westmer regned son coill good worthi good codicios well gou er ned lod loue pee tyme wos neu er cotake debate britan regned wos kig pee life tym whe bene kyng xi ere died lieth yorke claudi wos emour rome next aft er gay regned xiiij yere viij dayes come gret bretan called englod chalage tribut wich thei deni vn roman aft er gret batels ther wos twix ye emour claudi armag er kig britan aft er cordmet made yt armag er shuld wed claudi doughter thes ij shuld eu er life pee toke wher claudi named cite wer wer weddid hi called claudicestre call gloucestre pthis claudi iij wife petiua fyrst wyf gat doughter yt heyght antoia first wife decessed weddit messalina gat son yt height britanic octauia dought thrid wedit agrippma hauig son yt height nero claudi wedit doughter octauia nero wife son claudi luf yt agrippma last wife killed messalina fyrst wife lest shuld haue holp britanic hir son empyre yet agrippma last wife claudius dred lest hir housband wold haue proferred britanicus haue deposed nero son therfor poysunied hir housband claudius nero motit empire nero yaf mother sich reward yene poysunied britanicu kyld motber wife octauia iamys apostil time slai herod agrippa petre wos presid vt p patet actuu pthe body sent iamys myracull wos brought galeciam spayn nero claudi wos emour regned xiij yere vij monethis nero wos cursid made gret wast empire wold fish bot nettis gold ropis sylke gret part lordis rome kylled wos enmy men bot good men kylled brod er wife mother master killed also petre paule wold neu er wer cloth ij timys horsse mulis wer shod wt sylu er last set gret te rome fyere su say se troy brened sum sayeth roman coplayned stretes wer narow whe brent gret part rome nero sayd ther wos space bild ther stretis wyd er senatours wt comyn pepull com vpo kyll hym fled nyght subbarbis cite hid mong vine hered karlys begers cu bi hym sayed wist wher emour war shuld neu er skape nero thought shuld gret derogacion name wer slayn chorlys gret stake ran hi self hert died ther wos bereid dules keped body moy day gret hurt pepull tyll myracull lord ye bodi wos fond take way dules voydet seneca wos tyme mast er nero iuuenalis peeta lucanus poeta iacob ye la ye apostil bisshop ierlm wos slai ye iues ye sext yere nero ye euagelist marc wos mart er ed first yer hi circa annu cristti lxxiiij linus ytalicus wos pope rome x yere iij monethis xiij dayes linus successari clet thurgh ther holy cou er sacio war made mynist er tresur ye regned vij monethis wos made emour bi pouer spayn land nero leuyng aft er ye deth nero brought rome ther wos slai ama yt come wt whete rome smot heed bore yt wos emour next seyng noe helpyng pin manys day com gret retricio rome fro spayn wos fyrst eu er taught ye science opynli name wos quitilian otho regned aft er hym regned bot iij monethes vitellus yt wos presedent fraunce chalanged empyre itali tuyx thes tow wer iij gret batels ye fourth batel otho saw shuld ower cumyn gret dispare kiled self vitellus regned aft er otho regned viij moneth foloer nero speciall glotony synging fowll songes festis ettyng mesur myght kepe vaspasianus regned nex aft er ix yere x monethis xij dayes wele gou er ned men rome seig cursit successio nero send aft er vaspasian vn palysti ther wos son tit wich beseged ierusale whe herd yt nero deid wos send vn ierusalem herd thes cursed men regnyng instance wise men rome wyllely toke vpon hym empire none commyn rome ower come tyrand otho let hym draw thurgh rome aft er tybyr tyll wos deid let hym saile owt sepulture pepull desiered pthis man curit waspes nose none beleued lord ihu wos thecause went ierusalem venge cristes deth xxxij tymes fought enmis xiiij yere v monethes fyrst wos esy aft er ward full vnresonabull mich senate wos distruid bi mali also mich kynrad began secund persecucion nero ayenst cristyn men wich persecucion iohn euangeliste exiled pathius emprour put tun oyle brinnyng hurt hym thys man folower fadir vaspasian ne brother titus bot rather like nero kynred thes wicked condicions wos slayn palace rome xxvij yere age clemens martir wos pope ix yere succedid cletus clemens fyrst sent petre saied wos ordand successari hym ell wold lynu cletum shuld popis lest thurgh ensampull prelatis shuld ordane vndir sum euer wold pthis gou er ne pepull hym nota traianus hyspanicus emprour xix xere traia mony men sayed wos best emong emprours bot thyng alon vicius mych luff fals goddis wos bout distruy cristyn fayth iugyng hi self plese god sum men sayth hym self bot sued criste fayth ye end lyfe bot deth pand al lauuig set noght bot sent gregori meuyd pytte wepyng prayed vn owr lord god hym yt wold haue marci vpo hi bi prayer anacletus martir wos pope ix yere greke monyschyd cristen men prestes shuld worsshipped bown men sayng prestys doyng sacrifice god shuld borne vexid bot worshipp prestys sayed masse shuld haue witnes martir wos x yere vij monethes pope anacletus man ordand man woma shuld weddit opynly shuld blyssed opynly thee prest fadre mother martired thee iij yere adrian beried sent petre alexander roman pope viij yere v monethes alexandre parte thee senetours conuerted vn lord ordant holy water shold kest cristyn menys howses bred syng shuld made clere bred yt litill quantite last martird vnd er adrian wos emprour mony conuerted faythe sixtus roman wos pope x yere iij monethes man ordant sanctus sanctus sanctus etc shuld sayed masse holy thynges chirche shuld towched bot mynisteris cherche also tabuls ther dettys twix hym briynt opynli marketh place changed helped hi necessite phow kyng lucie regned aft er fadre good become cristen kyng coill regned lucie son good man god pepull sent rome appostell eulethre tho pope saied wold become cristen man resaue baptym name god turne right faieth beleue peulenthre sent ij legats wer called pagan elibayn lond baptised kyng mayne went toune toun baptised pepull tyll al land baptised wos yere clvi incarnacion lord ihu crist kyng lucie made tho land ij arche bisshoppes canterberi yorke many bysshoppis yet lond pand thes ij legate baptised land ordeyned prestys fer baptise chyldren make sacrament went ayene rome kyng dulled land regned mekyll honour xij yere died lieth glocestre phow lad wos log wt kig britos chose kig kyng lucie none heire body begoten thatt ward gret harme sorow land aft er kig lucis deth none ye gret ye lond wold suffre kyng leuyd debate emonges selfe l yere kyng befell afterward yt gret price come fro rome land called seuerie nought bot saue right rome nerthe le duelled half yere land bot breton hym kylled tho rome wist seuerie wos slai sent gret lord lond wos called allec yt strong man myghty body duelled land long tyme moch sorow breton aft er pure malece chosen akyng emenges wos cald astlepades assemled gret host breton went london seche allec ther fond killed hym hys felows one yt wos called walon defendid hym fersely fought long wt breton last discofited bretos toke bond hym handes foot cast hym awater wherfor wat er afterward called eu er walbroke ptho regned astlepades pee till erles yt wos called coill made afair toune ayenes kynges wyll let call toune colchestre aft er name wherfor kig wos full wroth thought destruy begon vpo hym brought gret pouer yaf erle batell erle defendid hym fersly power slew kyng self bataill tho wos coill crowned made kyng land pthis coill regned gou er ned reame well nobilli wos nobull man welbeloued among breton tho rome herd astlepades slayn wer wo der glad sent gret prince roman wos called constance come kyng coill chalengf tribute yt wos wot payed rome ye kig answerd wel wisely sayed wold pay rome right reson wold full good wyll acorded tho good contake bothe dueled ged er loue pthe kyng coill yaf hym doughter elene vn haue hir spouso wos bothe fair wise good weli lettred constance spoused hir ther moch honour befell sune afterward kyng coill dyed xiij yere regne lieth colchestre entired pof kyng constance wos roman chosen kyng aft er deth coyll mych hed spoused elene yt wos kyng coill doughter kyng coill constance made kyng crouned mych spoused kyng coilles doughter wos heir land wich constance regned well wortheli gou er ned land begat wife elene son wos called constantine kig bore trew faieth trewly vn rome life regned xv yer died lieth yorke phow constantine yt wos kig constancis son ye son seynt elin gou er ned ruled land emprour rome kyng constance deth regned constantine son son sent eline fond holy crose holy land constantine become emprour rome hit befell tyme ther emprour rome wos sarzyn tyrant thas wos called maxence put deth beleued god destruyed holy chrche pouer slew cristen men myght fynd emong let marter sent katrin mony cristi pepull drede deth yt fled come lond kyng constantine told hym sorow maxence cristite wherfor constatine pitte gret sorew made assemled gret host agret pouer went ouer vn rome ther toke cite kylled ther wos wer mysbeleue myght ther fynde tho wos made emprour good man gou er ned hym well londes hym wer attendaunt vnd er gouernance pand duell tyrant maxence yt tyme wos land grece herd tydynge hee become wode sodanly died endid lyfe consta tine went land vn rome toke hym mod er elyne moch wisdom coude iij gret lordes loued called hoell called taberne thrid morhin toke lod kepe vn erle cornwaill called octauian pand anone octauian wist lord duellyng rome seised land hand ther wt among hygh law held hym kig whan tydynges come constantine emprour wonder wroth toward erle octauian sent taberne wyth xijm men destruye erle falsenes ariued portesmouth pand octauian wist asse led agret pouer breton discofited taberne taberne fled then scotland ordened ther gret pouer com ayene land tyme yef batell octauia pwhen octauian herd tell assemled gret power com ayen towardes taberne moch myght tho ij hostys metten gedre vpo stanysmore strongly smot gedre tho wos octauian discomfited fled then vn norway taberne seysed land hand tounes castelles moch ther sith octauian come yen fro norway wt gret pouer seised land hand drofe roman wos tho made kyng regned phow maximian emprours cosyn rome spoused octauians doughter wos made kyng land octauian gouerned land well nobully none heir saufe doughter yong chyld loued moch lyfe mych thatt waxed seke wos poynt deth myght longer regne wold haue made one nepheus haue ben kyng wich nobull knyght strong man yt wos called conan meriedoke shuld haue keped kynges doghter haue maried hir whe tyme bene lordes land wold suffer yaf hir councell maried sum hygh gret honour might haue hir lust cosell thee emprour constantyne hir lord counsell accorded chose tho cador cornwaill wende ye emour message toke way went rome tolde emprour tydyng well wysely emour sent land wt cosyn yt wos vnkyll son nobull knyght strong wos called maximian spoused octauians doughter wos crouned kyng land phow maximian wos emprours cosyn conquered land amorican yaf conan meriedok kyng maxmian becom riall thoght conquere land amarican gret rich herd tell wos land ne left man wos worthines knyght squyer ne none othir man ne toke gret damage lond left home behynde man kepe land bot toke hym fro land xxxm knyghtes wer doughty menys body went ouer land amorican thor slew kyng yt called imball coquered lond pand whe done cald conan said mich o kig octauian haue made yow kig breto thurgh ye werlett distrobled yt ye wer kig yeue yow land amorican yow ther maketh kynge pand moch ye ben breton wyll thys land haue name called amorican bi called litell bretan land fro whens ben comen shall called moch bretan pand shall men knaw bretan fro conan meridok thanked hendely wos made kyng lytell bretan pand done maximian went fro then vn rome tho made emprour constantine conan meriedok duelled lytell bretan mych honour ther let ordand ijm plough men land erie land harow sowe effed hem richely wer pand miche o kyng conan none knyghtes ne none pepull wold take wyfes nacion fraunce hee tho sent gret breten erle cornwaill men cald dionothe yt shuld che e thurgh land xim madens say viijm mene pepull iijm thee grettest lordes shuld spouse pand whe dionoth vnd er stode made acomandement thurgh land bretan mony o nobro come assemled ged er maydens ther wos man durst withstonde commandmetes mich land take hym warde kepe done thinge good liked pand thes maydens wer assemled let cum fore iym att london let ordan shippes hasteli o mich neded vyage toke doughter wos called vrsula wos fayrest creature thot man wyft wold haue sent hir kyng conan shuld haue spoused hir made hir quene land made preuali god vowe chastyte hir fadre wyst ne man el wos leuyng vpon ethr phow vrsula xim maydens wer hir company went toward litell bretan wer martired coloyn vrsula chose vn hir company xim maydens wos ladie mastresse wet shipp tyme water called thamse co manded hir kyn hir frendis almyghty god sailed toward litele breton bot whe wer comen hygh see strange tempaste arose wos goddis pand vrsula wt hir shippes hir company wer driuen hundland thurgh tempast ariued hauen cite colonie kyng land wos called gowan tho cite wist tyding mony faier maydens wer ther arriued toke elga brother houshold wt hi wet shippis se faire company whan saw faire companie wold haue ou er layne take fro ther maydenhod vrsula good mayd concelled prayed warned taught wer hir felowes shuld defend ther myght rather suffre deth suffren ther bodi diffoylled tho maydens become stedfast god defended thurgh grace noe pouer shame pwherfer kig gawan wax sore anoyed yt wroth slew eu er icho anoe right sower tho maydens martred loue god lieth coloyn phow kyng gowan come destruy land man gret power thot wos called gracian defended land wos done kyng gowan wos sarazen called brother elga said hym shuld go conquere land tho fair maydens wer borne pand ordened tho gret pouer pehites denmarke orkenay norway come land brenttounes slew folke cast doune chirches house relegio robed land length breed put deth tho wold forsake right beleue cristyndom pfor mich o ther wos souerayn moght helpe kyng maximian taken hym worthi men whe wet conquere litell kretan tyme ye tell sent albone martired thurgh woed tyrant dioclician place wher abbaye made sent albone while yt wos apaynem pbut conu er ted hi god thurgh predicacio clarke wise yt called ancibell wos herbored nyght house incarnacion ihu crist ijcxxvi yere shuld vnd er stand sent albone suffred martirdo fore sent edmude wos martired therfor sent albone called fyrst marter englond pthis gowans brother folk yt wer sarazenes wet thurgh land destrued thig yt found thig spayred whe tydyng come rome kyng gowan begon stroye land emour tho rome sent strong gret pouer yt wos called gracia xxiiijm men well fightig cast tho sarezenes lande ariued porte mothe pmaximian myght cu hym self moch o wos chosen emour aft er deth constantine wos sent elene son pwhe gracian wos ariued wt host let spi preueli wher kyng gowan myght befounde vpo hym sodanli lain ther beddes descomfited hi slew ther beddis eu er ichone none ascaped safe gowan fled moch sorow cotre psone aft er befell yt maximian wos slayn rome thurgh treson gracian wyst tydyng let croune hym kyng land phow gracian made hym kyng whan maximian slai afterward breton kylled hym wikkednesse gracian begone regne become wikked sterne moch sorow breton yt slew hi emong ptho kyng gowan vnd er stond gracian slayn done deth assembled gret pouer come ayene land first done harme tho moch tho destrued land ye criste pepull yt wos moch bretan yt wos hardi nempne god yt anoe put strange deth pbut bisshop lodon wos tho yt called gosselin scaped wet then rome sech socour help destru sarazenis yt destruyed lond pand ye roma saied yt oft annoyed ther sendyng aft er folke bretan help bretens wold pand bisshop gosseline wet thes wt ony socour helpe tho went kig litell bretan yt called aldroie thrid kyng aft er gowan meriedok sayed pthe bisshop prayed kyng aldroie helpe socour kyng pitte hert herd bisshop fled cristyn men wer slayn gret bretan thurgh paynems sarazenes graunted hym constantine brother hym helpe pouer folke araye hors armur shyppes thig neded viage pand thyng redy called bisshope hym sayed take heir helpe socour costantine brother vpo couenaut god yef hi grace ye paynems ye sarazenes shend discomfited ye make hym kyng bisshop grauntid good pconstantine bisshop toke lefe kig aldroye betoke god toke ther men xijm went ther shippes sailed toward gret bretan ariued totnesse pwhen bretans herd tidynges yt come socour wer strongly holpen ordeyned huge nombre pepull come vnd er fenge hem mekyll honour gowan anone wyst thynges asemled sarezenes come ayenest yaf batal constantine slew hym hondes tho sarazenes wer discomfited slayn noe asscaped tho conu er ted vn god phow constantine kynges brother litell briton wos crouned kig myche breton worthenes anone bataill went london crouned ther constantine made hym kyng land bysshoppe goselin sette croune heed annoyntid hym o befalleth kyng bene tho bigan cristyndom ayene land anoe kyng constantine wos creuned anone spoused wife thurgh counsell breton begat iij sonny hir pthe frist wos cald constance aurilambros thrid vter constance eld er brother come age made hym monke wynchestre constantin ther fadre thurgh tresone wos slayn befell tyme pehite come hym vpon day message sayed wold speke kyng preuali councill kyng let voied chambre men ther wer withyn ther bode mo bot kyng pehite made countinance tho hee wold haue spoken ye kig ere ther kylled hym wt long knyfe went quaiteli owt chambre od er chabre last man wyst wher wos bicomen pwhen kynges men wyst ther lord wos deid made moch sorow wist done pfor myche ij sonnes aurilombros vter wer yonge noe myght kyng thrid brother wos moke wenchestre saied befoor vortiger wos erle westsexe thought priuyly hert thurgh quetance kyng went wynchestre ther constance monke hym sayed constans quod fadre deid ij bretheren ben gosseline bisshope london norissh ben yong none may kyng pwherfor councell yow ye forsake habit come shall make sych meyn vn breton ye shall made kyng pof constans yt wos kig costantine son moke wynchestre wos made kyng fadres deth thurgh consell vortiger wos erle westsexe mich aurilambros vter ij brether wer yong age vortiger let sle hym kyng hym self vortig r consceled constance mych tyll forsoke abbot went hym anone wos crouned kyng assent breton pthis kyng constance whan wos crouned made kyng wist ne knew bot litell world na coude thing wat knyghthod axed made vortiger chief mastir conceller yaf hym hys pouer ordeyne mych reame apertened hym self thyng entermelled onli bare name kyng pwhen vortiger saw land warde gouernall wyll thought preuy treson sle constance kyng myght hym self crouned made kyng regne let send hundreth knyghtes pehetes worthiest al land heeld wyth hym duell kepers body wold wende thurgh land ordeyne thynges apperteyned kyng pand vortiger honoured moch hondred knyghtes moch yafe gold silu er riche iuelles robe hors thynges plente wherfor held hym lord kyng pand vortiger told yf might kig ye wer thurgh treson wold make hem richest land last thurgh gret yeftes yefuen largeli cried thurgh court thatt vortiger wer better worthy kyng constance wherfor vortiger made semland bene wroth departed then court saied gon elles thinges done tratour saied encheson shuld hym slee say constance pwhen vortiger wos gone befell sone tho hundreth knyghtes pehites broken dores ef kynges chamber ther hym slew smote heed bore vortiger ther duelled vortiger saw heed wepped full tenderly eye nerthelees wos somedell glad deth pand anoe let take houndreth knyghtes pehites bynd ther handes hynd led london ther wer dampned deth fals tratours anone bretans land bi commune assent crouned vortyger made hym kyng land anno domini clxxiiij sother martir wos pope auicetu ix yere wich decreit nune shuld towch pall awt er ner pit sence bretan treson falsenese vortiger engist beginith fift parte coing danys thys tyme come saxon wer pagons fyrst bretonow called englond vnder vortiger wich wos crouned kyng lond time tho thies ij chylder kepyng wich constantine sonny say aurilambros vter thurgh ordinance gosli bisshop london ther faderes deth say constantine durst duell thys land tho chyld conueyd vn kyng lityll breton moch tho wyse treson vortiger tho wos made kynd thurgh constance ther eldyr brother wos slayn wherfor hundreth knyghtes pehites wer put deth beren blame vortiger wist ther nether consented pand kepers tho tow childer dred lest vortiger wold put deth thurgh treson falsnes done ther brother forne therfore wer lad ouer litell bretan kyng resaued moch honowr let norissh ther duelled till become fair knyghtes strong fers thought auenged vpon deth constantine ther brother saw ther tyme ye shall tell afterward phit wos long aft er yt tidiges come ouer see kynred tho hundreth knyghttes pehites wer dampned put deth thu gh vortig er land therfor wer wodirly wroth suore yt wold auenged ther kine deth come lond wt gret pouer robbed moy place killed sorow yt myght whan vortig er wist made moch sorow sore anoyd place also tydynges come hi aurilambros vter brother ordined assembled gret host cum mekell bretan yt say land auenged vpo constance ther brother deth half brought moch sorow ne wist whider wende phow engist xi thousand men come land vortiger yafe place called thongcastell sone sorow tydyng come vortig er yt grete nauye stranger wer ariued cutre kent wylt whens wer ne wherfor wer come land pthe kyng sent anone messenger thider sum shold cum speke hym wit folk wer axed cutre wold goo pther wer ij brether master prince yt strong copany yt wos cald engist yt horsse engist went kyng told encheson wherfor wer comen land pand sayed syr cuntre called saxonie land eermayne wher moch sorow pepull mony lond may susteyne pand master prince haue lond gouerne rule make cum men woman boldest ben amonges fight best may trauaill diuerse landes pand shul yef hors hernes armuri thing nedeth aft er shall say gone contre wher mowe lyuen ther auncestres fore pand therfor sir kyng yf ye haue ought company come land wyth good wil serue land kepe help defend enmys yf ye nedeth pwhen vortiger herd tydyng sayed wold gladly withold vpon sich couenant myght dalyu er land emnys wold yef resenable londes wher shuld duell eu er engist thonked goodly man er companye xim shold duell kyng vortiger moch thurgh ther boldnes deliu er ed land clene emnys tho prayed engist kyng mo h land myght make hym cite hys meny pthe kyng ansuerd wos done conceill breton pengist prayed hym eftsones moche place o myght compas thonge skyn wher vpon myhht maake maner hym duell pand kyng hym granted frely ptho toke engist bull skyn cut smale myght thuong round ther compassed o mych land vpon faire castell castell made let call thwong castell mych place wos marked wt thwong pof ronewen engistes doughter kyng vortiger spoused hir hir bowte castell made full well arayed engist preualy send letter cuntre wher come fro hondreth shippes fyllid men wos strong bold also well fightyng batellis shuld also bryng ronewen doughter wos fairest creature man myght se pand tho pepull wos come sent aft er toke castell moch ioy hym self vpon dey went vn kyng prayed hym ther worthely wold cum see new maner made place compassed thuong skyn pthe kyng anone graunted hym frely hym went thid er wos well payed castell fair werke ged er ther eten dronk wt moch ioy pand whan nyght come kyng vortiger shuld go chamare take ther nyghtes rest ronewen wos engist doughter come cup gold hir hand kneled fore kyng saied hym wassaill kyng wystnot wos mene ne shuld ansuer moch hym self ne none breton coud english speke ne vnd er stond spekyn longage breton done yit pneutheles latimer told kyng full vnd er stondyng therof wassale shold ansuer drynk haill pand wos fyrst tyme wassaill drink haill come vp land tym vn tyme well vsed land pthe kyng vortiger saw fairnes ronewen armes laid bowt hir nec iij swetly kytsed hir anone right wos namered vpan hir desired haue hir wif asked engist hir fadre pand engist granted hym vpon couenant kyng shold yef hym cutre kent thhe er myght duele pepull pthe kyng graunted preuely good wyll anone spoused ye damysell yt wos moch fusion self pand therfore breton become wroth cause spoused woma mysbeleue wherfor went hi nothyng toke kepe ne help hym thing done phow vortimer wos vortigers son made kyng engist wos driuen vortimer wos slayn engist went kent seised land hond hym hys men come lityl whyle gret pouer moch pepull men wyst lytell tyme wich wer kynges men wych engist men wherfor breton hym dred sayed among bot yf ne toke counsel twen ye land shuld betrayed thurgh engist pepull vortig er ye king goten fyrst wife iij sonny fyrst wos called vortimer yt secud catagren thrid passent pthe briton eu er ychon asset chose vortimer ther lord souerayne counceller eu er bataill crouned hi made hi kig wold suffre vortig er longer regne encheso aliance bituix engist hi britos ordined gret host driue engist co panie land yaf hi iij batallis yt fyrst wos kent ther wos lord secud wos tetford thrid shire athis half cooll pand botell met catagren horne engistes brother ych slew bott moch o cutre wos yef log horne thurgh vortiger tho spoused cosin ther made fair castell called horncastel name pand vortimer wos annoyed bred deth catagre yt wos deid sich man er wherfor anoe let fell ye castell gronde pand aft er yt ne left night ne day till driue engist pepull ye lad whe engist wos driue way ronewen dought er made sorow nowe quentely spek yt wer next ye kig vortimer priueyst wt hi moch yaf hi yeftes yt wos enpoisened died london iiij yere regne ther lieth phow bretos chose tyme vortig er ther kig engist come land fouhten gedre vortimers deth briton hir commune asset eft sone made vortiger hir kyng vpon conuenient shold neu er suffre engist ne none eftsones come land pand whe wos done ronewen quene preuely sent letter enegist enpoisend vortimer vortiger hir lord ayene bare croune rened shuld come land well arraied moche pepull venge hi vpon briton wynne land ayein pand whan engist herd tydynges made gret ioye apparelled hastely xv thousand men yt wer doughty euery bataill come land pand whan vortiger herd tell engist come ayene grett pouer lond assemled breton tho went ayens engist haue yef hym bataill folke pbutt engist drad sore breton thei driuen beforne discomfited hym strength wherfor engist prayd hym loue day sayed wos cuyn lad fight haue land ayen might accord wt breton haue luffe grace pthe kig vortiger thurgh counsell breton graunted loue day thus wos ordeyned thurgh breton saame day shuld holdin fast side salisberi vpon hyll pand engitt shuld come thidre iiij hundreth knyghtys mo kyng mony wisest men land pand yt day kyng come counsell wos ordined engist warned knyghtys preualy commanded euery shuld put long knyfe hosyn whan saied fair sers tyme speke loue pee euery none shuld draw knyfe sle breton killed thousand lxi knyghtes moch sorow mony ascaped pand kyng vortiger ther hym self tho wos taken lad thongcastell put prison summe engistes men wold kyng bene brent quyke pand vortiger tho haue lyfe granted moche wold axe yaf vp land tounes castelles cite brughes engist folke pand breton fled then wale ther held styll engist went thurgh land seysed lond wt fraunchisos eu er place let cast doune chirches house religione destruid cristidom thurgh land let change name land man wer hardy aft er yt tym call lond britan call engist land deted land men ther made vij kiges strenght lad breton shuld neu er cu aft er ther pthe fyrst kyngdom wos kent ther engist self regned wos lord mast er ouer pthe kyng southsexe chichestre thrid kyng westsexe pthe iiij king estsexe pthe v kyng estangill called northfolk southfolk merchemerich say erldom nicholl pthe vi lecestre shiere northhamto shiere hertford huntyngdon pthe vij oxunford gloucestre wynchestre warwik derbyshire phow vortiger went wale bigan ther castell wold stond morter tempred blod engist deted land maner betwen men deliu er ed vortiger prison suffred frely gone whidre wold toke way went wale ther breton dulled moch land strong wekked wyn engist neu er come ther ne neu er know befor yt land vortiger held ther wt bretas axed concell hi wos best doo pand yaf hi concell make strog castel yt might hi self ther kepe defend nede wer pmasos hast tho wer fet bigan werk vpo ye hill breigh c er te th fel werk yt ye masos made day doun fel nyght thei wist might ther kyng wos soro anoyed chance wist doen pwherfor let send wisest clerkis also lerned yt wer thurgh wale myght found shuld hym tell wos best done pfor shuld tell wharfor foundment failed vnder werke shuld hym tell wos best done pand wisest men long tyme studied sayed kyng shuld done seke chylde borne woman neu er man done chyld shuld sle tem blod mort werk shuld werke eu er endure ende phow kyng let sech merlin thurgh wale speke hym kyng herd commanded mesangeres anone wend thurgh wale seke chyld yf myght hym fynd shuld hym bring forth vn hym recorde witnes thyng tak lettres ne wer destrobled man ne lette pand tho messangeres went then sped fast thatt come toune called karmardine o passed forth ther way funden ij child xxiiij yere age chydig yf hasty wordes sayed donebat quod ye wrong chide strife wyth pfor ye haue wit ne reso haue certes merli wit ne reson make force tell minly ye haue thyng god almygfty sith ye neuer fadre eu er mau knaweth well mother pthe messingers kynges vortiger herd strife tuix tow gromes axed stood besides whens marlyn wos borne also hym norisshed folke hem told gret gentyll woman hym bare karmardie wos called adhan neuer myght man wit fadre pwhen kynges messangeris herd tydyng went anone hym wos wardayne toune toold hym kynges letter shewed hym wherfor wer comen theder pmerlyn moder anone wer sent fore wardayne toune comanded shuld gone kig wos ordand massengers pmerlyn moder went then come vn kyng ther wer vnderfonge moch honour kyng axed lady yf child wer hir son hi begate pthe lady ansuered full tendirly wepyng sayed neuer company man worldly pbut sir quod o wos yong mayden faders chambre gret linage wer copany yt often tymes wont play solace beleft allone chambre wold gone forth byrnyng sone pand tyme ther come fair bachelar entrid chambre ther allone come wher wist neu er ne yit wot dores wer fast barred game loue ne myght ne pauer defend fro oft come vn fore sayed man er begot child neu er myght wit pof ansuere merlin wherfor kyng axed whi castille myght stond gonne ner proue merlin herd mother said spake kyng man er psir wos begoten ax ye falleth yow ne noe wit telleth encheson wherfor brought wherfore ye haue sent aft er certis quod kyng wise cowncelers haue done vnd er stond mort werke haue gone behoueth tempred wt blod foundamet shall faill eu er psir quod merlin ye sle blod tem wt mort ye quod kyng el shall neu er castell stand councelars done vnd er stand ptho ansuerd merlyn kyng sir sayed let cum fore tho wise concelers wyll preue say well ne trewly pand wise wer com marli axed blod wer encheson make werke stand endure tho wise wer abashed coud ansuer pmerlyn tho sayed kyng sir shall tell encheso wherfor werke th faleth may thand pther vnd er montayn ther ye haue belden tour gret pond wat er ye botom ye pond vnd er wat er ther ij dragos yt white reed yt fighten god ayens werke pdoo ye myne depe till men come pond doth men take way wat er ye shall se dragon haue told ged er fighte ayens werke pand encheson wher fore fundament faleth pthe kyng anone let digge vnd er til yt come yt pond let done way yt wat er ther fond ij dragon marlyn told egorly foughten ged er pthe white dragon egrely assayled reed laid hi strongly yt myght endure bot drew rested ye caue pand restyd hym went assayled ye reed dragon angrely held hi sore yt myght ayens hi endure drew hi restid aft er come ayen ye white dragon strongly fought wt reed dragon bote hym euell hym ou er come fled then come ayen poff syngnificacion thas ij dragon thot wer thee bottom ponde foughten gedre kyng vortig er men saugh batayll gret meruell prayd merlyn telle hym myght betoken psir quod merlin shall yow tell pthe reed dragon betokeneth white betokeneth folk saxonie fyrst ye toke held land thatt fightten ayens yow yow haue driuen enchaced pbut breton linage ouer comen driuen way sithen commyng ayene saxon recouered land held eu er driuen briton lond ther destruyed cristido thurght land pye first ioy ther cumynge turned gret damage sorow pfor tho ij brethern constance wos kyng wich ye let sla shall cum bi quinzeme passed gret pouer litell breto shul venge deth ther brother shall brin yow fyrst sarow afterward shall sle gret part saxon shall driue remenant land therfor abyed ye longer make castell ne none werke bot anone go el wher life saue god take treuth haue sayed thinges shall fall pand vnderstond ye well aurilanbros shall kyng bot shall enpoysened litell tyme shale regne pof kyng aurilambros pursued vortiger engist diden merlen modre deted kyng turned ayen karmardine pand sone aft er tydyng come breton aurilambros vter brother wer ariued tottenesse wyth gret host pand anone thee breton assemled went vnderfonge aurilambros vter wt gret nobulnes vn london croned aurilambros made kyng vn hym humage anon axed wher vortiger kyng myght founden wold avenged brother deth aft er wold vpo paynems pand told hym vortig er wale lade hym thid er ward pvortiger wist well tho brether come hi conquere fled then castell wos cald gerneth stood vpon hygh mantayn ther hym held paurilambros vter brother ther folke beseged castell full long tyme castell strong well arayed psoo last kest wildfyre brent house men ther aray o mych o castell vortiger brent among died moch sorow ptho engist kent regned ther hard tydyng anone fled wold haue gone scotland haue socour aurilambros men met northcuntre yaf hym bataill engist men defended while myght folke wer discomfited slayn ta son fled vn yorke aurilambros hym foloed egrely otta litell ayens stod aft er ward put hym merci pand arilambros vnd er feng hi men yaf cuntre galeway scotlond ther duelled pthe kyng arilambros wet thurgh ye lond put away name engistland engist aft er name called tho let call ayen gret bretan let make ayen chirches house relegion castelis cite burghes tounes saxon destruyed come londo let make walles cite wich engist folke casten doune pthe breton lad hym mount anbrian som tyme house religion tho wos destruyed thurgh paynyms pwher knyght called anbry tyme wos found house therfor hyll wos called mount brian wos called ambresbury shall euermore phow aurilambros redresse lond gret bretan destrayed thurgh saxon kyng aurilambros let med redresse house amlesburi ther put monkes ther bennonnys littell plaace wos called salisburi ther saxon kylled bretans wher engist shuld haue made loue day wich tyme ther wer slayn mlxi knyghtes thurgh treson engist pthe kyng therof gret pitte th ught make mynd monumet ston myght endure ye wordes end thing toke ther counsell ther wos best done ptho spake kyng bysshop london wos called ternekyn shuld enquere aft er marlyn coud best tell thig myght best made merlin aft er wos sought foud come ye kyng pand kyng toold hi monumet yt wold haue made ptho ansuerd merlin kig sayed ther bene gret stonys irland long vpo ye hill kyan yt called geats karoll wer place thei ther wold endure eu er remebrance thoo knyghtes yt heir entered pper oy kig hard stone land irland psoth qd merlin pbut land ther none soch geantes set grete good self eu er tyme wer woundet ony man er hurt wesshen stone wt hote wat er wesshe ther anoon wer hole phow breton wet sech gret stons irland thes breton herd thing went swore emong wold gonne seche tho stonnes toke vter kynges brother ther cheftayn vm men merlin counselled go vn irland diden pand kyng irland wos cald guillomer herd tell stranger wer ariued lond asse bled gret pouer fought ayens folke discomfited pthe bretans went till come mout kylian climed vp vn mout pbut saw stone man er stood gret meruell sayed bitwyn self man shuld hem remeue strength ne engyne huge wer long merlin thurgh craft remeued brought ther shippes come ayene land merlin set stone ther kig wold haue set maner stoden irland pand kyng saugh made thanked merlyn richeli rewarded place let call stonhenge eu er phow passent wos vortigers sone kyng guillomer come land tratour called cappa enpuysened kyng aurilambros men shall vnd er stand stat passent vortigers sone leued tyme come land gret pouer ariued north cuntre wold ben venged faders deth vortiger pand strongly trusted vpon componye brought hym land germayne conquered north cuntre vn yorke pand kyng aurilambros herd assembled gret pouer breton went fight passent wos discomfited pepull passent ascapped thes wt sum men fled then irland come kig guillomer prayed hym help socour kyng granted hym good sayed wold help hym vpo yt couenant self must gone pouer breton wold venge vpon breton rather cum land token stone strength called geantes karoll kyng guillomer let orde shippes went see xvm men ariued wale gon rob moch sorow phit befell kyng arilombros lay seke wynchster myght helpe self sent name vter brother pouer helpe wale thed er ward went moch o myght kyng irland passent herd tell aurilambros seke hym ther come sarizen called coppa sayed sir duell ye pee host hyght thurgh quentize shall sle kyng aurilambros seke sayed passent ye doo shal yow richely auaunce ttoraur coppa put vpon abbyt relegion let shaue hym brod croune come vn kynges court sayed wold help kyng hys maladie tho sayed tretour coppa vn kyng sir ben good comforth shall yef sich medicin ye shall swete anone right lusten slepe haue good rest thee tratour yaf hym sich poysin slep anone right died hys slepyng ye trator sayed wold gone feld till wer waked scapped way man suspeccion cause habbit wos clothed also brood shauynne croune kynges men wist wos deid become wondir sorus fast sought tratour myght fynd hym coppa turned ayene host fro whens come pwhen aurilambros deid sterre morne wos sei clere light bught beme wos seyne hed horribull dragon kyng aurilambros wos thus deid enpoysened wynchester morne aft er wos deid bowt tyme prime ther seyne stere gret clere beme sterne wos bright er son bought beem pered dragos heed mouth come ij huge lightes wer bright ony fier brennyng pand one beme toward france stryght ou er see thiderward pand beym rome vij bemes full clere long light fier pthis sterne seyn mony man none wist wat betokened pvter wos kynges brother yt wos wale wt host bretos saw yt sterre ye gret light yt yaf wodred ther gretli myght betoke let call merli prayed hi tell myght betoken pof betokenyng stere merlin saw starre beheld long tyme sithen quoke weped tendirli sayed ala ala nobull kyng worthy deid pand doo vnd er stand aurilambros brother enpeysened se well sterre betoked bi heed drago sei bought beem shal kyng regne pand beem standeth toward est vnd er stod yt ye shall get son shal conquere al fraunce landes yt belongeth croune fraunce shal worthier kyng honour eu er wos ony auncetours pand bi beem strechys toward irland betokened ye shall get dought er shall quene irland pand vij bemes betokene ye shall haue vij sonnis eu er ichon shall kyng regne wt moch honour abyde ye longer heir goth yef bataill enmys fight wt bodely ye shall ou er cu haue victori pvter thanked hertely merlyn toke men went toward enmy foughten gedre mortali discomfited enmy distroyed self kylled passent wos vortig er son pand breton killed guillomer yt wos kyng irland men pand vter anone aft er bataill toke way toward winchester done entere aurilambros kig wos brother pbut tho body borne stonhe ge moch honour done made remembrance breton ther wer slai thurgh treson engist sam day shuld haue bene accordid place entered aurilambros secud yere regne al worshipe myght belong sich kig who soull god haue ci pof vter pendragon werfor called ye shall ouer take wyth loue fe igerne erle cornewaill wife ye deth aurilambros vter brod er wos crouned regned well worthely remembrance dragon wos likened let make ij dragon thurgh councell breton made one borne hi went bataill abide winchester bisshoppis chyrche pand yt cause wos called euer aft er vter pedrago pand otta engistes son commendid vter bot lytell wos made new kyng ayens begon meue ordined gret company frendis kin os brother take land fro humber vn yorke tho yorke held strongly ayenes nold suffer cu ye cite nother yeld cite beseged toune anoe right yaf therto strong assaut bot cite hem keped well strogly pand whe vter herd ther come thed er wt gret pouer help rescu toune put away sege yaf strog bataill otta copany defedid well myght last wer discofitid slai otta os wer take put prison london pand vter hi self duelled yorke aft er went london estir aft er wold bere croune hold solempne fest let soman erles baron thei shuld cum fest tho wyfes shuld bringe also fest come kynges cummandmet wer cummaundid pthe fest wos richely arrayed holdyn worthely set mete wer astat erle gorloys cornwaill igern wif set alther next kig kig saw fairnes lady pand wos rauysshed hir beaute oft made hir nyse sembland lokig laughyng last erle ceyued preue lokig laughyng loue bitwen ro vp fro ye ullull wroth teke wife called hi knyghtes went then wroth takig leue kig king anone sent aft er hym shuld cum ayen goo then despite hym pand erle wold cum ayene man er wise pwherfor kyng wos full wroth wrath hym deffied deidly enmy erle went then cornewaill wife castell tyntagell pand kyng let ordin gret host come cornwaill distruy erle myght put hym sich castell strong well arayed tyntagell wold yeld hym kyng kyng anone beseged ye castel ther duelled xv dayes yt neu er myght sped eu er thought vpo igerne vpo hir laid moch loue yt wist done ye last called hym knyght callid vlfyn yt wos preue told hi councell axed wos best done psir qd doth send aft er merlyn anone tell best counsell ony man leuyng merlin anone sent aft er come kyng kyng told councell psir qd merlin shall done moche thurgh craft yt yt shall make cu nyght ye castell tyntagell shall haue lady phow vter bigat igerne wos erlis wife cornewaill arthur kyng merlyn thurgh craft coud changed kynges figure liknesse erle vlfyn garlois cha berlayn figure iordan wos erles chambirlayn yche wos transfigured od er lekenesse pand merlyn done sayed kyng sir qd may ye go sodenly castell tyntagell axen entre ther haue kig toke priueli host gou er ne lede knyght mich loued toke way toward castell wt hi toke vlfy chabirlayn merlin pand come theder porter went bene hys owne lord tyme come go bede pthe kyng went bede igerne erles wife dyd hir bigat vpon hir son wos called arthur pand vpo morow kyng toke leue lady went ayen hys host pand nyght kyng lay igerne bedde yt wos erles wife kynges men yaf gret assaut vn castell erle men manli defended last befell assaut erle hym self wos slayn castell taken pand kyng none turned ayen tyntagell spoused igerne moch honor made hir quene sone aft er tyme come shuld deliu er ed beyr child son wos called arthur aft er gat doughter called amya come age nobull baron called aloth wos lord leon wed hir pwhen vter long tyme regned ther come vpon hi gret sekenes wer sorow pand meyn tyme tho yt kepe otta wos engist son os brother tho wer prison let gone gret yeftes yt hom yaf went pand tho ij bretheren wer ascappid come ayen ther cutre ordined grert pouer begon eftsones vpon kyng phow kyng vter chese aloth kepe land breton while wos seke moch myght seknes moch kyng vter wos seke myght nott help hym self ordined aloth son eleyn tho chosen wardeyn cheftayn folke anone bretans assemled gret host yaf batell otta folke otta last wos discomfitid phitt befell thus afterward thes breton dedignacion aloth wold hi attendant wherfor king wos anoid wond er let put hym litter host emonges folke pand lad hi veroloyn tho fair cite ther yt sent albon wos martired aft er wos yt cite destroied wt paynis thurgh thed er thei set otta os ther peple entrid toune let make fast yates ther thei held kig come beseged made strog assaute tho yt wei wt mali defended pthe kig let ordeyn gones engynes brek walles walles wer strog yt nothig myght mysdoo potta pepull gret despite yt kig liggyng lytter beseged toke concell monges stand vp morow cu yef batall kig yt batall wer otta os slayn tho yt ascapped lyue fled scotland made colegu ther chyftayn saxon wer lyue ascaped fro bataill brought ayan gret strength emoges sayed yt kig vter wer deid shuld well coquere ye land amonges thought enposin kig ordeyned dede yaf yeftes gret plente thyng done ordined hem thid er ward ther yt kig duellig clothed hem pouer wede bett er sped therlyd purpose neu er theles ther falsnes quatize might neu er cu nyghthe kig pbut last aspied yt ye kig draknoe oth erlycour wat er cler wel yt negh beside pand thes fals tratours vpo day preuali wet ye wel put theri poyson yt ye wat er enpoysened anoe aft er o kig dronkyn ye wat er bego fuell sone aft er died o moy dronk wat er died also pand anoe wos aspied folke toune let stop well eu er pwhen king wos dred folk bere hi stonhenge gret solempnite bisshoppis baros werther hi bery besides aurilambros brother aft er turned ayen tho eu er ychone send arthur son made kig land moche reu er ence fadres deth xvij yere regne phow arthur wos son vter crouned fadre deth drofe colegrin saxon cheldrik almayne lond arthur wos made kyng ye lond wos bot yong age xv yere wos fair bold doughty body meke folke wos good curtas large spendyng made hym wonderly well beloued among men ther wos need pand begone regne swore ye saxon neu er shuld haue pee ne rest till driue lond assembled gret host faught wt colegri wich aft er time otta wos deid saxon mayntened colegrin wos discomfited fled vn yorke toke toune ther hym held pand kyng beseged hi ther myght nothyng sped cite wos strong toune kepped cite well orpedly pand meyn tyme colegrin let toune bladulf fled hym self cheldrik wos kyng almayne haue socour kyng assemblid agret pouer come ariued scotlond vc shippis whe arthur wist tidig pouer strength nough fight ayens cheldk let sege went london sent anone letter king litill bretan called hoel nepheu sustres son shuld cu hi wt pouer yt myght assemblid gret host ariued southinton pand kig arthur wist wos glad nough went ayens resaued moch honour tho ij hostes met assembled toke ther way euen vn nichol cheldrik beseged wos taken pand come vpo cheldrik pepull wist wer yt wer egrely asseilled pthe kig cheldrik meny defedid maly bi ther pouer kig arthur kylled mony saxos neu er wos seyne sich slaught er pand cheldrik men yt wer left lyue fled way pand arthur pursued droue oute wod myght ferther passe cheldrik men saw well wer brought moch disese yold arthur man er wyse shold take ther hors ther armur must onli gone fote ther shippis wold gone home ther land neu er cu ayen land pand vpon assurance thyng yeuen hym good hostag pand arthur coucell men granted thyng resaued hostage ther vpo wet ther shippes pand wer hy see wynd changed deuell wold thei turnd ther nauy come yen land ariued totnesse wet shippes toke land clen robbed moch pepull slew taken armur myght find wet forth till thei come vn bathe men toune shitte fast ther yates nold suffre cum toun defendit well orpedly ayens phow arthur yaf bataill vn saxon com ayen land beseged toune bathe ou er come arthur herd tydyng let hong anone hostage left hoel bretan nepheu kepe marche toward scotlond halfe pepull hym self wet helpe rescu toune bathe come thed er hee yaf strong bataill childrik kylled almost peple man myght hym withstond ne endure vnd er thee stroke swerd pand ther bothe wer slayn colegrin bladud brether pand cheldrik fled then wold haue gone shippis arthur wist toke xm knyghtis cador erle cornwaill let stop cumming pand arthur hym self went toward marche scotlad messing er told hi yt scottys beseged hoil bretan ther lay seke therfor hasted hym thed er ward pand cador pursued aft er cheldrik toke er might come vn shyppis kylled cheldrik pepull pand cador done viage hasted hi ayen fast o myhht towardes arthur fond hym scotland ther rescued hoel britan scottys fer wt mounref ther held arthur pursued fled then lymoigne wer thatt cutre lx iles gret plente briddis gret plente egels wer woned cry fight ged er make gret noyse whan folke come rob land moch o myght scottis wer gret rauenours yt toke al yt thei might fid ye lad lymoign wt ani sparig ther charged ayen folke scotland wende phow kig arthur axed merlin aueturs vi last kig yt wer regne englond land shuld enden sir qd merlin yere incarnacion ihu crist mccxv shall come lamb wynchestr yt shall haue white tong trew lippi shall haue write hert holinesse pthis lam shall make mony goddis house shall haue pee lyfe shal make fairest place world tyme shall fulli made end pand ye end life wolf strange land shall hym moch harme sorow thurgh wer end lamb shall master thurgh help red fox yt shall cum northwest shall ou er cum wolf shall dy wat er tyme lamb shal lyue bot shal die phi seede shall strange land thee land shall gou er nour litell tyme tyme shall come dragon melled wyth mercy eke wyth wodenesse shall haue berde goot shall yef englond shadow shall kepe land colde hete foot shall set wyke london shall enbrace habitacions shall opyn mouth toward wale trimbilyng hidour mouth eres shall strech toward mony habitacions cutres breth shall full suete strange land pand tyme shall reuers renne blod brayn shall make place land walles shall moch harme vn seed aft er tyme pthen shall ther cum pepull owt north west regne shall lad thurgh wikked hare dragon shall doo croune kyng aft er ward shall fle ower see cummyng ayene dred dragon p tyme son shall reed blode shall se thurgh world yt shall tokyn gret pestylence deth folke thurgh dynt suerd pepull shall bene fader le tile tyme dragon die thurgh hair shall meue ayens hym vn end life shall fully endit tye pthis drago shal hold tyi best bodi world shall die side march strange land land shall duell fad er le wt good gou er n men shall wepe deth ile shepey vn hauen mareil pwharfor ala shall ther song fadroles folke shall ouer lyuen land destruied aft er dragon shall cu goot kar shal haue horne berd siluer ther shall cum nosthrell domp shall tokyn hunger sorow gret deth pepull moch land begynnyng regne shall wasted pthis goot shall go ou er france shall opene flour lyfe deth tyme ther shall rise egle cornwaill shal haue fetres golde pride shal pere land shal despise lordes blood shal flee shamfully bere gauersech aft er shal made breggis men vpon costes see stonys shuld fall fro castels mony tounes shall made playn pin tyme shall seme ye bere shall brenne bataill shall done vpo armes see feld ordeyned sheld pand bataill shal die moi whitte heedis wherfor batal shall called white batiill pand forsayed bere shal done goot moch harme shal cu southwest blod shal goot lese moch land till time shendship shal hi ou er cu shal clothe lion skyn shal wyn lost ther pfor pepul shal cu northwest shal make goot soyr drad hee shal venge enmys thurgh cuncel two owles fyrst shal perel vn done old owle shall wend away certayn tyme aft er shal cum ayen land pthes two owles shall gret harme moy thei shal councel goot arere ayens forsayed bere last goot owles shal cum burton vpon trent shal wend ouer dred bere shal fle swan fro company burton toward north ther shall wt hard shoure suan shal taken slayn wt sorow bere taken heded alther next nest shall stand vpon broken brige son shall cast bemys mony shall hym seke vertu hym shall cu pin shal die sorow care pepul land mony landis shal vpo bolder afterward tho two owles shal moch harme forsayd flour lyfe hir shal lede distresse shall passe ou er see fraunce make pee betwen thee goot flourdelise ther shall duell til tyme hir seed shal cum sech hir shall styl till tyme shal hem clothe wt grace shall sech owles shal put despitous deth pand shall goot brought disese grett anguissh sorew shall leue life goot shall cum wyndesore bore shall haue hed white lion hert pytuus lokig phi visage shal reste seke brest shal stachig therst thersty worde shal gospell bering shal meke lamb pin fyrst yere regne shal haue gret payne iustifie vn trew tyme shall land multiplied aliandes pand bore thurgh fersenesse hert shal haue shall make wolfe becum lambis shal called thurgh world bore holines fersnes nobulnes mekenes shal done mesurably shal vn burgh ierusalem shal whette teth vpon yates paris vpo iiij landes spayn shal tremble dred gascoyne shall swet fraunce shal put winge gret tayll shall rest englond softely almayn shall quake dred pthis bore shal yef mantel ij tounes englond shall make reu er rene blod brayn shal make mony medous reed shall get moch auncestres deid shal beyr iij crounes shal put land gret subieccion aft er shal releued tyme pthis bore aft er deid doughtynes shal etered coloyn land shall fulfilled al good boor shall cum lamb shal haue foot leed heed bra hert loppe swynes ski hard tyme land shall pee fyrst yer regne shal make cite world shal speke ther pthis lamb shall lese tyme gret paart land thurgh hidous wolfe shall recou er yeue lordship egle land egle shal well gouerne till tyme prid shall ou er cum ala sorow shal die brethers suerd aft er shall land fal forsayd lamb yt shall gou er ne land pee life tyme aft er shall die land fulfylled maner good lamb shal cum moldwarp cursed goddes mouthe caytyfe coward hare shal haue elderly skyn goot vengeaunse shal fall vpo syn pin fyrst yere regne shal haue good grett plente land toward also land shal haue gret presyng til tyme shal suffre pepul lyue mich pride chastisyng wherfor god wyl wroth pthan shall arise vp dragon north shall ful fers shal meve ayens forsayd moldwarp shal yef bataell vpo stone pthis dragon sholl gadre ayen company wolf shal cum west meve ayens tho forsayd moldwerp sied shall drago bynd ther tayles ged er pthan shal cum lion owt irland shal fall companie wt hem shall trembull land shal called englond aspyn leef tyme shal castels fellid doune vpo thamyse shall seme seuerne shall dri body shall fall deid therin iiij cheif flodes englond shall ren blod gret dred shall anguissh yt shull arisen pafter thee moldwarp shal fle dragon pthe lion wolfe shal driue way land shall ye moldwarp shall haue man er pouer saf onli ship wher mawend pand aft er shall gone lond whan see wt draw aft er shall yef thrid part lond haue fourth part pee rest aft er shal life sorow life tyme pand tyme hote bathe shal beco cold aft er shall molwarp die auentou sli rightfull heyris englond ende phow arthur ouer come guillomer kyng irland scotes become men guillomer kyng irland hard tidyng kyng arthur entred glastenbury ordeyned gret pouer irissh men come see irissh pepull come scotland ouer see ariued fast ther kyng arthur wos host anone wyst ther went towardes yaf bataill ou er come anone right guyllomer fled men ayen irland pand done discomfited arth turned ayen ther wos place ther left scotys wold haue slayn bisshoppes abbotes folke cuntre lady open heed co befor kyng arthur cried mercy sayed sir gentill kyg myghty haue mercy pytte vpon u o selfe right law hold maynten cristindom full gret dishonour shuld kyll beleueth al myghty god ye done goddis loue haue mercy pytte v suffre v haue moch sorow pyne saxones mony tyme passed thurgh lond bot ynough often tymes haue v done serow disese pfor casteles haue taken bestes slain eten moch harme haue v done ye wold v kyll hit wer honour kyng kill cry mercy pfor ynough ye haue done v v ou er cumyn loue god ye wyll suffre v life haueth merci criste peple yt beleuen crist o ye doo pwhe kig arthur herd sorow pytte yaf liyfe lym harme fell doune fete kyd become leige men toke homage pand aft er kyng arthur turned ayene host come vn yorke ther bydyng made viage pand tho yaf loegers aloth spoused sustre yeftes gret plente tho gawen cosin bot yong age men seruid yaf rich yeftes thanked moch ther good seruesse phow kyng arthtr spoused gunore wos gunores cosi erle cornwaill aft er conqured guillomer irland arthur brought land pee rest good state wos well eu er cuntre tho toke wedded wife called gunor made hirquene fair lady gentill cador erle cornwaill norisshid chambre wos cosin neu er child gedre neu er theles kyng arthur loued hir wond er well derly pand anone o wynt er passed let
