vauce yt werhier pand kyng arthur thatt table briton frenshme norman flemynges burgos mauser loherms landes half monte go rye lad breton ye gret cornwail wale irland scotland shortely tell lades yt wold worship cheualrie seche come kyng arthur courte phow kyng arthur went fraunce conquered yt land froll roman kylled syth befell kyng arthur thurgh conceill baron lordis wold go conquire fraunce tho called galle thurgh roman tho held land ther pouer ther gou er nance roman take yt land nobul knyght worthy bodi yt wos called froll wist yt arthur come ordend host gret pouer fought wt kig folke wer discofyted fled vn paris entred cite closed yates ther hem held parthur wyst yt frol wos gone paris pursued aft er come thed er hi beseged cite strong wel araied tho yt wer therin defeded well manli pkyg arthr duelled thermore moneth ther wos moch peple cite dispedid al ther vitails yt wer gret hunger bicom amoges yt died wond er thikke withi cite hunger come frol prayed accorded kyng arthur haue pee wold yelde vn toune also pfroll saw longer myght hold toune ayens ther wil trust gretli vpo stregth set kig arthur shuld cum fight body body shuld dete fraunce betwene two pkyng arthur anone grated wold none peple vndertoke bataill hi pand vpon morn bothe come well araied paris ther shuld fight anone smyten ged er fersly well foughten sidis man coud deme better pand befell froll yaf arthur stroke kneled ground wold nold o frol withdrew swerde wounded kyng arthur forhed blood fell doune eyn face parthur anone stert vp hertely felt hurt man semed almost wo toke tabourne good suerd feaulte vnd er fenge toke good hostage kyng arthur aft er went forth host conquered augien angiers gascoyn pehito nauerne burgon berri lotherne turyn peithers land fraunce coquered holli pand whe coquerd taken bi humages feautes turned ayen paris ther duelled long tyme ordined pee long tyme ou er al cutre thurgh fraunce pand whe pee wos made ou er al thurgh noble kynghthod yt also worthines pand werhe neu er gret lord durst meue ayenst hi nod er arise make ye lod france quiet pe woned ther ix yere mo gret wond er reproued moy proud men lither tirantis chastised afterther deseruise phow kig arthr auauced al yt trauild ser uis aft er ward befell thus estren ther held fest paris richly gan auaunce knyghtis ther seruice holpen comquest phe yafe stoward wos called key augien angiers bedewere come next hill oden widew openhed sittig besides tombe sore wepyng gret sorow made oft sayd eleyn elein key bedewere axed wherfor made moch sorow say tombe qd sorow mysauentur fair lordes seke ye geant may heir fynd sle anone pbe styll good wife qd ther dismay ye tell v soth whi thow makest moch sorow wepyng psirs quod damysell norisshid brest yt called ellin nece hoell kyng breton wos bold hardy thyng dismade saied go bodile goddis name ayens roman lede sarasens paynyms man er trust haue god vpon ther strength pgo sech sharpely name almyghty god sle paynyms cristyn men ayenes v distruy cristyn men god shall v help ou er cum haue right oppynyon therfor haue trust god doo enmys cristi dom god may destruyd ou er cumyn men may recorde worthines knyghthod pwhen kyng arthur thus saied cried high vois pgod fadre almyghty worsshipped thy name end amen grante v grece well destru enmys yt ayens cristido ye name fad er son ye holi gost ame god yef neu er grace ne worship world ne mci hi haue day shall feynt wel smyt egreli riden softeli ordyned wynges well wysely pthe emprour herd tell kyng arthur folke wer redy araied fight thed er come ordined wynges ye best man er myght kynges paynyms wond er moch pepull pand kyg arthur men foughten well roman paynyms strength withstond xx shepe ayens v wolfe pand befell bataill showre wos wonder hard long side emprour amonges ther arthur wos full sorus aft er wer comen lond mordred myght ayens endure anone wos discomfited fled then nyght men vpon morne come london bot tho cite wold suffre cum then fled winchestre ther held pepull come pkyng arthur let take body gawen cosyn body augnissell let borne scotland ther cuntre ther wer entired pand aft er anone kyng arthur toke way distruy mordred fled then cornewail pand quene gunor wos kyng arthur wife thatt tho sogerned yorke herd mordred wos fled then might endure ayens king arthur wos soradrad gret dout wist wos best done wyst well hir lord kyng arthur wold neu er hir haue mercy gret shame done toke h way preuali iiij men mo come karlion ther duelled hir life tyme neu er seyn amonge folke hir life parthur wist mordred wos fled cornwaill let send aft er men scotland northhu berland vn humber let assemble folke nomber come fro then cornwaill sech pursue aft er mordred pand mordred assembled folke cornwail pepull wt nombre wist arthur commyng leu er die take chaunce longer fle aboid yaf hard bataill kyng arthur pepull moch pepull slayn side yt man wist bettir parti pbut fell last mordred wos slayn folke ye good chiualri kyng arthur gadred norishid diu er landis also nobull knyghtis round tabull moch prased thurgh world werther slayn arthur self wounded deth let borne litter vyoun heled woundes yet breton supposen liueth lond shall cum yit conquere breton pbut certis prophesi merlin sayd deth shall dowtous saied sothe ther yit haue dout shul haue eu er sayen pfor men wot whed er lyue deid parthur borne auyon xxij yere regne aft er incarnacion lord thu crist vc xlvi yere phow kyng arthur deliu er yd reame vn costantine son cador niphu kig arthur wist myght regne longer let cum costantine wos cadors son erle cornewaill cosin bitoke reame sayed bad therof kyng till come ayen moch o none heire body begoten harme wos nobull kyng doughty o wos child body begoten thyng god wyll haue done must done who name blissid end amen phow kyng costantine wered mordredes ij sonnis thys costantine wos nobull knyght worthy bodi tho ij sonny mordred begoten grete envy vn costantine tho crouned kyng pand befell begon meue ayenes hi assembled gret host wer fore mordred bene driuen away moch sorow thurgh land brother ordeyned london take cite wynchistre pbut costantine come london slew ther aft er wet wynchestre slew ther also bothe enmys wer deid pand costantine regned worthel iiij yere died lyeth london pof kynges adelbright edell kyng costantines deth ther wer ij kynges bretan called adelbright yt wos danoys held cutre northfolke southfolke yt hight edell waas breto held nichol lidesei al lad vn huber pthes ij kiges fast wered ged er aft er wer accorded loued ged er o thei bore bodi pthe kig edell sustre wos called orewenne yaf hir thurgh gret frendship kyng adelbright wife begat vpon hir doughter called argentill thrid yere aft er come vpo hi stronge sekenes yt nedes must die pand sente kyng edell brother law shuld cum speke wt hi come wt good ptho prayed kyng iured also name god aft er whe wer deid shuld take argentill dought er land yt keped hir well norisshe hir chambre pand wer age shuld maried strongest worthiest man myght find shuld yeld vp hir land ayene pedell granted oth cofermed hys prayer whe delbright deid entered edell toke ye damisell argentill norisshed hir chambre become ye fairest creatr yt might lyue ony find phow kig edell maried ye damisell knaue kiche king edell wos vncle damisell argetil bethought myght falsli haue land fro nece eu er falseli ayenest oth thought dissaue thee damisell marie hir knaue kichen wat cald curan become worthiest strongest man body ony man wist ony land tho leued thought hir shendfulli haue maried haue hir land aft er ward bot wos clen dissaued pfor curan wos hauelockes fo wos kyng kyrkelane denmarke curan co quered wife lond aft er ward slew kig edell wos wife vncle hir land o place telleth openli ne regned bot iij yere saxon danys hi killed gret harme breton bretans bore stonkenge ther entered moch honour pof kyng conan wos curan cosin curan regned conan yt cosi wos wond er proud knyght regned coud haue man er loue eu er medelyng pepull toke vn kill killed ij child pthe saxon wered ayens often tymes ou er come wos pee life tyme regned xiiij yere died lieth london pof kynge cortif gurmond come thurgh thee paynyms briton conan regned cosin cortif yt bihated pepull nothyng beloued cortef lost britan thurgh tyme fell gret myschef breton cristyndom wos destroyed briton wer driuen owt land land lost w th ony recouer aft er ward left lod saxon ye aft er ward shal heir pfor time ther wos paynyme yt called gurmond wos kynges son daufrikes paynymys folke reame aft er fadre wos kyng sauf bequaeth yaf brother saied nold neu er kyng yf myght get conquere reame strong cutre pfor wos bold strong bodi phesied merly sayed shuld wolfe see let assemle paynyms nombre let ell shippis wet moy landdis toke homage feautes mony went bi see conquered mony diu er se londis pso come irland coquered yt land oft tymes wered vpon breton breton vpon oft wonen oft losten yef hostage breton sent gurmond ther irlond shuld come briton help ayens briton help deliu er land thei wold hold gladly ther lord wos paynym wer paynim breton wer cristin well ought help wer lawe pwhen gurmond herd prayer hasted hi moch myght ariued scotland come northhuberland ther yt saxon wer duellig thei cofirmed ye conauntes bi twen yt wer made bi othes hostage beir trew fay hold lord pay truage yere ptho began saxon affricans destruy rob brenne tounes destru thing moch o myght spared nether man ne woman ne chyld lered ne lewed bot al thei kylled cast doune tounes castels chirches pand put land gret destruccion sone o thei might fleyn fled then well poer rich bisshoppis abbotes chanons gret small su litell briton sum cornewaill tho shippis myght haue phow kyns gurmond drofe kyng cortif chechestre killed breton thurgh quentise get toune cortif kyng sled then chechestre tho good cite strong ther held xx dayes gurmond come beseged cite strong yt might get maner wise ne engyn myghte done ptho bythought thei vpon gret quetise brenne toune made engynes glew nettes toke peces tunder fier bond sparous fete afterward let fle anone right flow logged toune ther ther nestis wer stakkes euyssinges house fyer began tende brend ye toune pand britans saw eu er side hied faught bot anone wer slayn discomfited while bataill dured kig priueli hid hi stale way wale wiste neu er wher become toune chechistre taken destruied pand gurmond went destruied city tounes neu er wer afterward made yene seyn yit land mony place phow lond called englond name engist mony kenges wer made aft er land gurmond destroied land thurgh hee yaf lond saxon anone thei toke good saxon long tyme desiered moche wer engistes kynred fyrst land breton lete called englissh men cause engistes name lond let call englond ther langage folke bene called englisshmen o moch o tyme wos called engist lond conquered vortiger spoused dought er tyme brut come first englod lod called breton folk briton sith tyme gurmond eftsons conquered yaf vn saxon thei anone right changed name o fore sayd pand whe wos done gurmond passed ouer fraunce ther coquered mony landis destruyed cristen pepull ther come saxon duelled land bigane fast inhabit ther wold haue made new kynges lordis myght neu er assenten haue kig entendat therfor thei made mony kxnges diu er se shire engistis tyme pthe fyrst kyng wos kent southsex thrid westsex fourth estsex v northuberland vi estangle say yt strongest toke hym febelest wos long tyme yt kig crouned emog ne cristyn man wos tho amonges ne cristyndom nother pbut wer paynyms till sent gregori wos pape rome seyn child nacio englong cite rome felawes sent austyn come fyrst englond ariued ile tenet passed forthe come vn cantorberi ther soiourned kyng adelbright kent ye wos lynage engist fair vndirfenged sent austyn felaws moch honour fonden neded ouer yaf fair place cadled abbay sent austin wich place lieth self shiyned pthis kyng adelbright wos good man wyth good herd sent austyn predicacions yaf leue preche thurgh land kent turne conu er te thee pepull might pit befell aft er ward thurgh goddis grace litell tyme kyng self conu er ted god pepull land baptisid pand meyn pepull turned god sent austyn come rochestre ther preched word god paynyms therfor hi scorned cast vpo reigh tailles mantell honged full thes reigh tayles pand dyspite cast vpon guttys reighes od er fische wherfor good man sent austyn wos sore annoied greued woman shold deliu er ed ther child brigges end wich house yit wome cite bene deliuered chyld pwhen sent gregori herd tell englissh pepull wer turned god u er ted set vn sent austyn pallione bi bisshop yt wos called paulin mad hi premat erchebisshop englond sent worde shuld ordein make bi shoppis land pand anone austyn pallio dignite ersbishop made ij bisshoppis felaws yt come wt fro rome yt called wet preche southsex turned moch peple god sent austin hi self preched thurgh englond phow sent austyn wet wale ther yt breton wer nold obedient erchebisshop cantorbury englond wos baptised turned god sent austyn went land ther breton wer kepe englisshmen say wale ther founden monkes abbey vij bisshoppis pfor ye briton destroied way cristyn pepul yt sent austi u er ted saied bisshoppis yt wos legat rome p mat englod yt thei shuld bi reso hi obediet saied nold pbut erchebisshop carlio wold nold neu er man er thig obediet englishman pfor englishman thei said bene adu er saries enmis haue driue v cutre cristi men eu er bene englismen haue eu er bene paynyms bot late yt cou er ted psent austyn might none onsuer haue otherwise said pertely nold neuer meke ne pope rome pand sent austyn turned ayene tho kyng adelbright kyng kent told folke nold man obedient bot erchebisshop karlion pand whe kig herd wos sore annoied said yt wold destruy sent elfrid kyng northhuberlad wos frend shuld cum pouer yt myght shuld mete leycestre fro then wold gone wale ther destruy erchebisshopp carleon tho refused sent austyn phow king adelbright kig elfrid kylled brecinal wos kyng breton held contre leicestre befell ther wos kyng breton held cuntre leicestre cuntre name brecinall pand breto herd tell yt tho ij engli h kinges wold mete ther leicestre wend wale let ordi pouer yt fight thes ij kiges litell availed hi folke wer slain self fled lost landis euer pand thes ij kyng adelbright elfrid duelled leicestre detid ye land amoges toke homage feautis folke cutre aft er thei wet toward wale tho wale herd tell scomfitur yt brecinal leicestre wer wonder sore drad tho ij kynges toke chose amonges good men holy hermytes monkis prestis pepull gret plenti went barefote wellewerd haue merci thes ij kynges pbot tho kig wer sterne wicked nold neu er speke bot kylled eu er ychon palas sorew ne spared hem tha wolfe doith shep smyten ther hedis eu er ychon thei wer martired come vnderstand vc xl aft er ward went then baugore kyll thoos myght ther find breton pand ye breton herd assemled ordeined ther pouer fight tho wos ther abarou wale yt wos called bledrik cornewaill su tyme lord denshyre kyng adelbright driuen ito wale aft er ther yef bataill bataill wos kyng adelbright slayn elfrid wouded sore soke feld ye te pepull slayn elfrid fled northhumberland wos land pand pepull leicestreshire made strength cadewan yt wos brecynals son kig leicestre aft er regned nobulli gret honour phow cadewan kyng leicestre elfride kyng northhuberland wer frendis debait wos betwe edwyn cadwalyn wer ther go northhuberlond destruy kig elfrid sle hi might whe wos come thid er frendes wet betwen made accorded man er elfrid shuld hold ye land fro huber vn scotland cadewan shuld haue al ye land athis side huber south aft er yt become good fredis ther life tyme loued ged er ij brether pand elfrid son ye wos called edwyn yt held land northhu berland aft er fad er deth fad er holde life tyme pand cadewan son yt wos caled cadwalyn yt held fad er lond held while wos liue loued ged er brether pand ye loue lasted bituix bot ij yere aft er began debate bitwen thurgh lither euyus cosin cadwalyns yt wos kylled thurgh kyng cadwalyn peanda oswy wos sent oswaldes brother regned kylled peanda edwyn wos slayn offris son vndertoke ayens cadwalyne eme offris died pand deth offris tho regned gentill cristyn man moch loued god almyghty land northhumberland heritage cald oswald wos kyng land pbut moch wos frend edwyne held gret part lad cadwalin cadwalyn wered vpon drefe toward scotland pand cadwalyn saw wold abyde cadwalyne nold longer hym pursew toke folke peanda brother law prayed peanda pursew oswald till wer taken slayn cadwalyne turned home ayene pwhen oswalde herd tyding cadwalin turned home ayene wold longer fle aboid peanda yaf bataill peanda wos discomfited fled come ayen cadwalyn sayed wold neuer hold fote land yf wold venge oswald pcadwalyn let assemble gret host fight wt oswald peanda come northhuberland yaf bataill vn oswald bataill oswald slayn heid smyten wos entered abbay bardeney wich place god hath wrought mony fair miracull ther el pand anone oswy brother seysed land rastored ayen proper reame fyrst dyngnyte kyng aleyne graunted askyng pthen apparrell take way viage land prayed god almyghty deuoutly wold make demonstracion yef prayer land wer hym plesaunt none pfor ayenes god almyghti wolde thing done whan thus deuoutly made prayer wi fro heuen sayed bad leue iornay way englond shuld go pope rome almyghty god breton regne breton ne neuer recou er land vn buerne good man place wos gone tyme see pfor often tymes wont ther aspie theues robers oft tymes wer wot cum land rob brene sle pthe lady yt buernes wife wonder fair woman kyng com vn hir hir housbond wos absent trastid none harme vn kyng welcomed moch honour worthely serued thing pwhen kyng eten toke lady hand leed hir chamber sayd wold speke hir councell folke fro chamber made void saf lady lady lordis ye land made playn thee dispite kyng hi done said yt wold auengid eu er yt wer frendis concelled grented wend vn yorke ther kyng wos pand buerne toke hys meyne come kyng whe ye king hi saw redy tho ij bred token leue kige godryn went toward see wend ouer englond fast myght spede buerne well comforthed fast hyed danois bene ariued north cuntre comen thurgh holdernesse destruyed cuntre ther cosin phit befell thus kyng elle gone wode disporte venison sum take o sat wode mete knyght sayed haue well sped moch venisan taken pand word come man sayed yf ye moch venison wonnen hondreth kyng edmond sothe quod catf tell ther kyng went castell also whether shall ascape die att godis myght pwhen sent edmunde neuenid god wisten well self anone hubba hu gar toke sayd shuld god sake cristyn law mony done beforne pand sent edmond said nold neuer rather wold suffre deth goddis loue lawis kepe tho toke king edmund bond vn tre made ther ardheres shote arous till bodi stykked full arows vrchon full prickis payn nold neu er god forsake payn turment died betoke sowle myghty god pand saw wos deid smyten heed maner o ye haue hard sent edmond martired phow hubba hungar toke toune redyng sent edmond martired hungar hubba wet then ther danois vn redyng pand o went thederward brenned tounnes cite kylled cristy pepull wold god forsake cast doune church come redyng toke toune ther held till kyng edelf westsex come theder pouer take toune tho comen danois yef bataill kyng edelf bataill wos kylled erle danys callee cidrak vpon morow come kyng eldred brother alured stronge pouer gret host pand kyng edelf come ayen foughten day bataill pand danois tho comme fight bataill wos wonder strong mony man wos ther slayn danois day victorie kyng eldred brother alured day wer discomfited pbut iiij day aft er ward danois englisshfoughten gedre time vpon ekeldene ther wos slayn kyng denmarke wos called rafing iiij erles gret pouer day danois shame thei wer driuen vn engilfeld pand xv day aft er danois englisshmen foughten tyme rafyng ther wer englisshmen discomfited then danois yt wos called roynt went redyng host distroid yt myght take kyng eldred faught hi wos tyme vnrightuysli wich also translat empire grekis frenshmen paulus roman pope x yere verey holy man gret almos faderles childer prison er wedouys poer men myght folower sent paule constantine roman secund wos pope aft er paule ij yere constantine wos lay man sodenli made prest o tyrant toke dignite pope gret sclander chirche pope litell tyme bot faithfull men put put eeyn wos fyfth infamyd pope emong mony hed er holy gost yt holy apostyls seet kepid honour holines pinfenit martirs wer made tyme constatin emprour heritike men trowe ther wos neu er emour ne pagon kylled mony marters tyme yelden vp gost eu er lastig payn pthe empire rome deuydid tyme stephen pope tranlatid itili karolum yet yong man constantyne held lond grece wyth landis ower se gret labur mony rebellyng pthis tyme karolus magnus wos nobull yong man began regne vpon fraunce son pippini mother wos called berta stephenus thrid pope iij yere mendid errurs constaotine degrated tho ye wich constantine ordand fadyrs secund rome cl fadyrs beyng present charles kyng fraunce granted leberte eleccion pope ordane apostils seet leo fourth regned emprour grekis v yere leo cursed man bot moch o fader wos couetus man toke away certan croune chirche put vpon hede anone corruppid wyth axis dicessid cursed wiffe wich regned hir son constantine wos emprour leo wos meke put away mother fro kyngdom might take heed vn hir woman warke botshe fenyt rankyr put eeyn afterward hys childireyn also regned ayens iij yere last wos haue weddid whe grekis sauyd wold weddid gret karolus thei toke hir shethir vp monastari toke nichofe rum ther emprour pthe v vniusall study wich old tyme translait athyns vn rome bout thys tyme tranlatyd vn paris bi karolus kyng fraunce nichoferus wos emprour constantine wos vere nygoij exaltid empire grekis bot fettit tyme est impariall wos brought nought roman put vnder karolus magnus pierusalem bout tyme wos recouerid karolum holy land seckit sarisens wos distruied strongly destruccion wricchis come michaell wos emprour ij yere verey cristi wos well beloued also wos cunnyng science tho nichoferus hurt destressid ther goodis bi couetusnes michaell restorid made riche ayene nota karolus magnus frist sant wos emprour aft er michaell wos crouned emprour leo pope wich tyme empire wos translatyt fro grekis frauce germane translacion empire grekys way wer defectieu vn roman grekys strofe eu er bot wos wt venuys wordis strength craft bataill thei gret enuy roman nold obey chirche rome certanly popis wold writt vn obey chirche rome wrot ayene said ye haue take kynrad name tho ye wich made popis ye secud o moch thei archaged name shuld thei chaged ifeccio life ye iij lest ye wich chosi excedig degre shuld hurte name leo wos pope aft er sergius viij yere leo wos placenciam anno domini viijclxxiij pof kyng alured danois tyme prayd merci myght gone land aluredus thys tyme come danys englond deth eldred regned brother alured dolfynes cald ptho went danois asse danois pouer ayens hi withstod come london host ther wer danois soiourned ther wold haue foughten bot danois durst fight prayed hi pee myght go ayen ther cuntre neuermore cu englond ayen say ony harme done pand vpon couenant shuld yef plege good hostage soch englissh men wold axen phow hubba hunger wer kylled chippenham danois brought ther kyng vn kyng day danois departed froo london fast riden bothe nyght day neu er toke rest goyng till thei come vn excestre token tho toune ther held pwhen kyng alured herd tydyng anone let take hostage went then vn excestre pouer pand danois herd tell cummyng went then vn wes sex come chippenham ther moch harme cuntre robbid folke brought prison pthe king alured pursued come vpon fersly assailed ther wer slayn bothe hubba hunger brother buerne bocard bataill wos moch folke slayn te gree feld left danois moch o kyng come litell companye pthe kynge hasted moch o myght wend ayene ye danois fonden hubbais body liyeng deid entered made vpon hit gret logge let call hubeslow cald vn thiys day place deuenshire pthe baroens somerset wilteshire dorset herd tell ther king wos descomfited ordeined pouer myght haue come kyng ther wos thanked god hym found liue went danois slayn ptho toke councell king baron wold gone seche danois fight ther riden yt nyght seche come morow prime habyngdon ther danois weer pthe kyng alured baron tho assembled ther assayl danois eg er ly ther yaf strog bataill ye danis nobulli put log tyme yt wist whed er te pepull wes slai pbut th befell god wold yt king alured victorie moch honour danois wer driuen yt ne wisten whid er turne xv day king pursued wyll glad fayn wer speke pee acord toke good hostage sayd nold neuer vpon ne debate arere pand ouer behighte kyng aulured wold go bring ther kig vn ther kyng shuld baptised pand vpon condicion kyng alured hem granted lyfe limme said vn thei shuld gone ther kig seche c er tayn day cum ayene wos set wenten forth fast come ayene ther day wos assined danoys wos old man mo childre hir saw edel wold wos fair yong knyght worthi riche wos well beloued kyng thought doughter shuld well maried beset vpon granted hi doughter good lord kyng wold consent ther pthen thys edelwold come ayene kyng told wos fair ynough vpon see wos wond er lothly tho ansuerd thee kig said toke bot litell charge sir qd edelwold tho hir fadres heir riche landis ye wold co sent grant myght hir haue shuld rich ynowghe goodis name qd kyng consent ther edelwold thankid tho kyng moch went ayene deuenshire spoused damisell cuntre duelled pand th befell vpon tyme told counsell thing vn wife howe maner begiled lord kyng wold haue hir vn wife anone wist loued neu er afterward o pthis lady consaued bi son tyme wos yt ye child shuld borne edelwold come kyng prayed hi heue son fontstone kyng granted let call hi edgar name pand wos done thought syker ynowgh kyng yt wold taken wife moch lord wos oly amerous phow kig edgar weddid estrild aft er deth edelwold thus befell men kyng edgarys court thospeken sayed edelwold richely avaunced thurgh mariege wife yit sayd vaunced hondreth fold spoused fairast woman euer seyn kig herd speke moch hir bewte thoght edelwold dessaued begiled thought priuely hart wold gone deueshire wer till hut hert hynde wild bestis shuld se ther lady deted then lady wos duelling maner place beside forest ther king wold hut man er wos herburghed nyght tyme come kyng shuld sope sone shone kyng asked gossip aft er godson edelwold made hir cu kyng neu er theles otherwise myght haue bene shuld haue comen sight pthe lady welco ed kyng swetly cussed toke hir hond tho next hir set soppid gedre ther custom vsage land tyme dronke drinker shuld say wassayll shuld ansuer say drinke haill thus kyng lady mony tymes also kyssed aft er sopper tyme go ed kyng went bed thynkyng hertely fairnes yt lady tho ou er comen hir loue thought yt shuld die bot wyll hir vpon morne kyng aroos forest went disport hertis hyndes wild bestys hertis gret plente itali wherfor pope od er roman called otto yt might deliu er wich toke berigar strength twyes owtlayd toke lothori wife wich tyrand prisoned leo viij wos pape aft er benedictus yere iiij monethis man stepmother let sle encheson make hir son eldred kyng thus aday wos slayn ye shall heir afterward pit befell thus day yt kyng edward wet wode play south cutre beside toune yt called warham wich forest wos grete plente hertis hyndes ben ther hi play thought vpo brother eldred wos mod er quene hir place wos nygh forest thought go thider viset se brother toke bot litell meny went tho toward stepmoders house time soiourned castell corfe rode thiknes wode aspy gam befell went mys lost mey come last come wode lokid abowt saw ther faste beside man er stepmod duelled thid er ward went allone anone wos endentures iiij bisshoppis aboue said toke part endenturs yt part endenturs bore shew kyng pwhen kyng saw forme vnder stode held full well apayed man er thyng ordeyned sauyng techig restitucion goodis make ayen yt thyng wold accorde send word ayen iiij bisshoppis shuld put way poynt restitucion pbut ansuerd thei wold done word tho sent kyng erchebisshop tho iiij erchebisshoppis shuld cu catorburi thus standith holy enter dited cursed wronges ye haue done holy chyrche clarge pand moche ye duell beth bide malace wricchednes woll cum ther ne amedment ye shall vnderstand tyme aft er ward sentance vpon yeffen holdeth stede strength vpon tho haue communed tym whethir erles baron knyghtys eu er assoyle saufly vn day fro tyme afterward condicion som eu er curse comyn ony word sentanse vpon openly crouned ptho said ye kig bi yt almighti god wist yt ye come land yt ye brought sich tyding shuld haue made ride yere ptho ansuerd padolf full well wed oure frist comig yt ye wold haue obedient god holi chirch haue fulfillid popis commandemet haue shewed vn nouncid popis wer charged ther ye haue said ye wist cause comyng yt ye wold haue made v ride hole yere well ye myght haue said ye wold haue pandolf herd comandemet kig stert vp smartely anone axed boke candill wold haue cursid set vpo ye clarke hand pandolf hi self went sech cro kig folowid hi deliu er id hi clarke bi hand yt shuld wt hi walshmen myght take pand tho strength myght made assaute vn castell swandon get castell pand dauid price brother herd tydyng ordeyned flight pand lewelin prince saw brother fled sore abassed pouer maynten pand lewelin gan fle wened well haue scappid morow sir roger mortemer met x knyghtis set round went smoten hede presentid vn kyng edward pand maner prince wale taken hede smyten al heiris disherited eu er thurgh rightfull dome landis reame phow dauid lewelins brother prince wale wos put deth dauid price brother wale thurgh prid wened haue bene prince wale brother deth pand vpon sent walshmen parlament dinbigh folishly made walis arise ayens kyng began meue ayens kig edward sorowe disese myght bi pouer pwhen kig edward herde thyng ordeyned men pursue vpo dauid fersly defendid till come toune sent morice ther wos dauid take fled lad kyng pand ye kig commaudid shuld honged draw smyte hede quartir send hede londo iiij quartirs send iiij chief toues wale shuld take exampull therof beware pand aft er ward kyng edward let cry pe thurgh walis seised land hond gret lordis wer left liue come done feaute homage kyng edward ther kynde lord pand tho let kig edward amed lawis walis yt wer defectiue pand aft er sent lordis wale bi letter patent sh uld cu lament wer comen kyng said full curtesly lordynges ye welcome behoueth coucell help wend gascoyn ame de trespaces wos dene wos ther entret pee bitwen kyng aragon prince morrey pand kynges liege men erles baron consentid grauntid therto pand tho made kyng edward redy went gascoyn let amend trespaces wos done gascoyn debate wos betwen kyng aragon prince morrey cesid made accordid pand whyle good kyng edward quene elienore wife gascoyn good erle cornewaill wos made wardeyn englond till kyng edward come ayen pand tho enquerid traitours congetten falsenesse ayens eche vnderfenge ther dome aft er deserued pbut mene tyme good kyng edward beyond se done make amendis ayens trepassid ther fals thefe tratour wos called risap meridoc began make ayens kyng edward wos encheson sir payne tiptot wrongfully greued disesed forsaid risap meridoc pand kyng edward herd sent bi letter risap meridoc shold begynne make shuld pee loue come ayen englond wold vnd er take quarell amed wos mysdone pthis forsaid risap meridoc despisid kynges co mandemet sparid sorow yt myght ye kig men englond anone aft er wos takyn lad yorke ther wos draw honged felonye pof redressing kyng edward made iostices clerkis done ther falsenes drofe iues englod ther vseri misbeleue kyng edward duelled iij yere gascoyn wylle come wend ayen englond wen wos cume ayen fonden mony playntes made iustices clerkis done moy wronges falsenesse wondir wos pand wich falsnes sir thomas weylond kiges iustice forswore englod ye toure lundo falsenes men put vpo wherof wos atteint proued fals pand anoe kyng wyll iustices ptho let enquere aspi iues desaued begiled pepull thurgh ther sine falsenesse vserie let ordeyn priue parlamet among lordis ordeynid emog iues shuld void englod ther misbeleue also ther fals vseri vntill cristyn men pand sped make end thig communite englond yaf vn king xv peny ther goodis meuabull wer iues driue englod pand tho went iues frauce ther duellid thurgh leue kig philip tho wos kig frauce phow king edward wos seised land scotland thurgh sent graut lordis scotland long alesander kyng scotlod deid dauid erle huntindone kynges brother scotland axed clymed kyndom scotland brother wos deid encheso rightfull heir mony gret lordis scotland saiden nay wherfore gret debate arose bitwen ther frendis moch wold consent coronacion mene tyme forsaid dauid died pand befell yt dauid iij doughtres yt worthely wer maried frist dought er wos marid bailloll secud brus ye thrid hastig forsaid bailloll brus chalenged land scotland gret debate strife arose bitwen iij encheson ych wold haue bene kyng pand lordis scotland saw debate bitwen iij come kyng edward englod seisid land scotland chefe lord pand kig wos seised forsaid lordis scotland forsaid bailloll brus hastynges come kynges court axed kyng wich shuld kyng scotland pand kyng edward wos full gentill trew let enquere croniclis scotland gret lordis scotland wich wos eldest blod wos foude bailloll wos eldist kyng scotland shuld hold kyng englond feaute homage pand aft er thys wos done bailloll went scotland ther wos croued kyng scotland pand tyme vpo see gret bitwen eglishme norma vpo time ye norma arriued dou er ther martired holy man called thomas dou er aft er ward wer norman kylled ther ascappid pand sone aft er kig edward shuld lese duchie gascoyn thurgh kig philip fraunce thurgh fals castyng douseperis land wherfor sir edmond wos kig edward brother yaf vp homage vn kyng frauce pand tyme clerkis englond grautid kyng edward halfendele holy chirch gooddis helpyng recou er land ayen gascoyn pand kig sent thid er nobull company bachilers self wold haue gone portesmouth wos let thurgh maddoc wale seised castell swando hand encheso ye kig turned wale cristemase encheso yt ye nobull lordis englod yt wer set gascoyn coforth ther lord ye kig wer take sir charles frauce yt say sir iohn breta sir robert tiptot sir raufe tany sir hugh bardolf sir adam creting yit ascencio madoke take wale yt wos called morgan wer sent tour londo ther wer heded phow sir iohn bailloll kig scotlad withsaid homage sir iohn bailloll kyng scotland vnderstode yt kyng edward wos wered gascoyn reame scotland delyu er ed falsely tho ayen oth said homage thurgh procuring folke sent vn court rome thurgh fals suggestion assoiled othe swore vn kyng englod wos letter enbulled ptho chosen scotland dousspers nymme edward right pand tyme come ij cardinales court rome fro pope celestine trete accorde bitwen kng frauce kyng englond pand tho two cardinales speke accorde thomas turbeluill take liouns made feaute homage warden paris hi put ij sonys hostage thought go englond till aspie cuntre tell come englond brokyn kynges prison frauce nyght said wold done yt al englisshme walshmen shold bow king frauce thyng bring ende swore vpo couenant dedis wer made betwen shuld haue yere poudes worth lond bring thing ende pthis fals tratour toke leue wet thes come englond vn kyng said wos brokyn priso put ill loue wherfore kyng coude moch thanke full glad wos commyng pand fals tratour fro day aspied doyng kyng also cousell kyng loued wel full priue clerke englond wos kynges house fraunce herd treson falsnes wrot clerke tho wos duellyng edward kyng englond thomas turbeluill done false coniectyng councell englod wos writte haue sent vn kyng frauce thurgh foresaid letter clerke sent fro frauce hit wos foude vpo wherfor wos lad londo honged draw ther treso ij sonys yt put frauce hostage wer tho beheded pof counquest berewyke tho two cardinales wer went ayene fraunce trete pee cambrey kyng sent thider erlis barouns say sir edmond brother erle lancastre leycestre sir henri lacy erle nichol willm vessy baron baronettis xiiij best wisest englod pand tyme king edward toke viage scotland vpo iohn bailloll kyng scotland pand sir robert roos berewyke fled fro englisshme went scottys kyng edward went toward berewike beseged ye toue tho yt wer within manly defendid set fire brint ij kyng edwardis shippis said dispite reproue pweneth kyng edward long shankis haue get berewike al vnthankis gas pike done gas dike pwhen kyng edward herd scorne anone thurgh myghtynes passid ou er dike assailed toue come yates gat conquerid toue thurgh gracious pouer kylled xxv thousand vijc scottys kyng edward lost man renoune saufe sir richard cornewaill kylled flemmyng reed hall quarell foresaid richard helme commaudid yeld put kynges grace scottis wold wherfor hall brent castyn doune tho wer therin wer brant pand king edward lost mo men viage symple estate xxvij englisshmen wardeyn castell yaf vp key assaute pand ther wos takyn willm douglas sir symond frisell erle patrike yeld pee bot inghm humsremille robert brus wer kyng edward forsoke kyng edward held scottis aft er ward wer takyn put prison aft er king yaf ther trespasse deliu er id prison pand tho let kyng edward close berwik wally dychis aft er ward robert rous went tindale set wuyebrugge fire exham lamerstok kyllid robbed folke cuntre pand went then vn dumbarre pand frist wedenesday marche kyng sent erle garenne sir hugh perci sir hugh spen ser fair companye besege castell pbut wos called sir richard syward traitour fals man ymagyned begile englisshnen sent englisshmen dissaue said wold yelde vn castell yf wold graute viij dais respit myght send tell sir iohan bailoll wos kyng scotland men faired wer castell send hi word bot wold remeue sege englisshmen wold yelde castell vn englisshme pthe messinger tho come vn sir iohan bailoll tho wos kyng scotland wher wos host messing er told hi al ye case pand sir iohan toke tho host come morow erly toward castell pand sir richard siward saw cum wos master counsell ke castell said vn englissmen qd se fare copanye well appariled gon ayens mette assaill pand sir hugh spen ser saw falsenesse treson said tratour take proued falsenesse shall vaill hugh ye spe ser comadid anone bynde hi hast wet ayens ther enmys killid scottys xxijm scottys time man honour sauf sir patrik graham yt manli faught long last kylled tho said englisshmen reproue scottys pthes scaterand scottys hold sottis wrench vn ware erli mornyng euell tymyng went ye fro dunbare tho castell saw scomfiture yolden vp castell vn englisshmen boude hir body londis castellis kig edward thei wer take ther castell iij erles vij baron xxviij knyghtis xi clerkis vij picardis wer presentid kyng edward sent vn toure londo keped ther phow kyng edward gret grace deliu er ed ayeij scotis prison wer chieftens land drew frensshmen thurgh cousell willm waleis kyng edward made tho end taken chefetayns scotland tho come sir iohane bailloll yelde vn kyng edward put grace lad london kyng edward come thid er wer brought kig axed wold make amendis trespasse losse thei done thei put merci plordiges qd kig wyll landis ne goodis wyll ye make oth vpon goddis body trew neu er thys tyme ayenst bere army sentid kynges swore vpo goddis body pthat say sir iohan comyn erle strathorne erle carrik also iiij bisshoppis vnd er toke clarge kig deliu er id yaf saufe condithys wend ther land long aft er ward ne arisen ayen kyng edward encheson wist well kyng edwardis folke take gascoyne sayed sir iohn bailloill kig scotland wist well land shuld haue sorow shame ther falsenesse hast went ou er se landes ther held come neu er ayen wherfor scottys chosin vn ther kig willm waleis ribaud harlot cumen vp noght moch harme englisshmen pand kyng edward thought myght haue deliu er ance pepull wer take gascoyn hast went ou er see flaudres vpon kig fraunce erle flaundres vnd er fenge moch honour grauted landis pand king frauce herd tell kynge englond wos ariued flaudres come huge pouer hi distruye praied trews ij yere englissh marchantis also frenssh might saufely go cum bothe sidis pthe king edward grauted must haue men pson wer gascoyn ye kig frauce grautid anone wer deliu er id pand ye tyme scottys sent bisshop sent andrew frauce kig sir charles brother sir charles shuld cum pouer scotland wold cum ther pouer shuld go englond land distruy scotland vn comen kent scottys trastid moch vpo frensshme thyng man er graute pand notheles scottis began robbe kill northumberlod moch harme phow willm waleis let sle sir hugh cressingham bataill fonkirke tidyng comen te kyg edward willm waleis ordeyned strong pouer also scotlond vn wos entendant redy kyll englissh men distroye land sore annoyed sent annone letter erle garren sir henri cy sir willm latomer sir hugh cressingham tresorer shuld take pouer wend northumberland forth scotland kepe cuntris pand william waleis herd hir commyng gan fle englishman folewid drefe till come striuelyn ther held castell pand walsshmen eu er day escried manaced dispite myght ye englisshme vpo tyme mornyng wet castell moutenace x mile passid ou er brigge willm waleis come strong pouer drofe bake englisshme ayens tho myght fled yt myght take brigge ascappid sir hugh kynges tresorour ther slain mony also wherfore wos made mich sorow ptho kyng edwar sped nedis flaudris wos ayen comen englond hast toke way scotland come thed er ascencio tide foud set fire brent pbut poer pepull scotland co wond er thyke prayd goddis loue wold haue merci pitte pwherfor kyng ho commandid man shold harme wer yoldin ne man ordir ner house religion ne man er chirche let aspie myght wher myght find ony enmys ptho come aspi vn kyng told wher scottys wer assembled bide bataill pand sent mari magdelene day kyng come fonkirke yaf bataill scottis bataill wer kylled xxxiij thousand scottys englishe men xxviij mo wich worthy knyght slayn wos knyght hospiteler wos callid freri brian iay pfor willm wale fled bataill thatt frere brian pursued fersly hors ran start myere mary vp bely pand willm walis turned tho ayene kylled forsaid brian yt wos moche harme pand kyng edward wet thurgh scotlad enquere myght find enmys yt land duelled long likyd ther wos none enmye yt durst abide pand sone aft er ward kig edward wet south hamto wold abyde scotland wynt er seson esemet pepull come londo let amed mony misdedis wer done ayens pee law yt wos flaundres pof last mariege king edward went thrid tyme scotland aft er ward ordeyned thurgh court rome yt kig edward shuld wedde dame margaret kig philip sustre frauce ye erchebisshop robert wynchelse spoused gedre thurgh wich mariege ther wos made pe betwen kyng edward englond kyng philip fraunce pkyng edward went tho thrid tyme scotland tho within first yere enfamined land ther left ne come merci sauf tho yt wer castell estreuelin yt wos well vetaled astorid vij yere phow castell estreuelin wos beseged kyng edward come huge pouer castell estreuelin beseged castell litell vailed might scottis none harme castell wos strong well kepid pand kyng edward saw thought vpo queyntize let make anone ther ij paire high galews tour ye castell made oth moy wer castell wer erle baron wer take strength wold rather yold shuld honged vpo galewis pand tho wer within castell heerd come yeld kyng grace merci kig yaf maletalent pand ther wer gret lordis scotland swore kyng edward shuld cum london eu er parlament shuld stond ordynance phow troylebastonne wos first ordeyned kyng edward went then londo wenet haue rest pee wich wos ocupied xx yere say wale gascoyn scotlad thught myght recouer tresour spendid let enquere thurgh reame tyme yt bene reame men called troillebaston ordeyned ther iustices man er recou er yed tresour nombre pand encheso wos thought till haue gone holy land haue werid vpon goddis enmis encheso crossid long tyme pand neu er thelas law ordeyned moch good thurgh englond wer mysbode tho trespassid wer well chastised afterward moch meker better thee poer commyns wer rest pee pand tyme kig edward prisoned son edward encheso walter langto bisshop chestre wos kynges tresorar made vpo complayn said forsaid edward thurghe cousell curment pers ganaston squyer gascoi brokyn parkis forsaid bisshapois pers cou cellid lad edward pand cause kyng odward exiled son englond eu er pof deth willm waleis fals tratour whe kyng edward enmys ou er cummyn wale gascoyn scotland distroyd traitours ribaud willm wale neu er kig wold yeld last toune sent dominic yere kyng edward regne xxxiij fals tratour wos take presentid kyng kyng wold se sent london und er fenge iugement vpon sent bartholomes eue wos honged draw hede smyten hys bowelis take bodi brint bodi quartired sent vn iiij best tounes scotlad hede put vpo spere set vpon london brigge exampull scottis shuld haue mynd amys ayens ther leige lord eftsones phow scottis come kyng edward amed ther trespasse done ayens mihelmasse tho next commyng kyng edward helde parlament westmynstre thider come scot say bisshop sent andrewes robert brus erle carik simod ye frisell iohu ye erle athell thei wer accordid kig bounde oth swore aft er ward misbore ayens kyng edward shuld disherited eu er pand whan ther pee thus made toke ther leue priueli wet home vn ther cuntre phow robert brus chalenged scotland aft er robert brus erle carik sent letter erles baron scotland shulde come scone morow concepcion lady hegh nedes land lordis come day assined pand day sir robert brus said fair lordis full well ye know son duelled right reame scotland o ye wate well rightfull heir sith sir iohan bailoll wos kyng v hath forsaken left land pand though kyng edward englond wrongfull pouer hath made assent ayens wyll ye wyll graunt may kyng scotland shall kepe ayens kyng edward englond ayens man er men yt word abbot scon arose vp said reson helpe land ta kepe defend tho said presens wold yef thousand pound maynten land grauted land hi ther pouer help defied kyng edward englond said robert brus shuld kig englond phow sir iohn comyn yen said crounyng sir robert brus lordynges said sir iohn comyn thenketh vpon truth oth ye made vn kyng edward englond touchyng self breke myne oth man went company tyme wherfore robert brus tho consentit wer wonder wroth tho manaced sir iohn comyn ptho ordeyned councell domfris wich come forsaid sir iahan comyn duelled ij myle domfris ther yt woned sodiorne bide phow sir iohn traitours kylled robert brus wist grete lordis scotland wer commyn scone sauf sir iohn comyn sodiorned tho nygh scone sent aft er specialli sir iohan comyn shuld cum speke vpon come speke gray freris damfres thursday aft er candilmasday sir iohn grauntid wend pand herd masse toke soppe drank aft er ward bestrod palfray rode way come domfres robert brus saw cum wi daw chambre tho made ioye ynough come ayens coled nec made hi goode semblant pand erles baron scotlad wer present ther probert bruse spake said sirres said ye wot well encheson commyng wherfore ye graunte might kyng scotland right heir land lordis wer ther said vois shuld crouned kyng scotland wold helpe maynten ayens maner men liue wer nede die pthe gentill knyght tho iohan comyn answerid said certis neu er ne haue moch help vaill boton oth haue made vn kyng edward englond shall hold whil lefe last worde went companie wold haue wened vpon palfrie robert brus pursued drawen sword bare thurgh bodi sir iohan comyn fell doune vn erthe whenne rogier wos sir iohn comyns brether saw falsenesse starit sir robert brus smote hym wyth knyfe false tratour wos armyd vndir stroke myght done harme moch help come bout sir robert brus rogier comyn ther kylled hew pes pand robert brus turned ayen ther sir iohon comyn nobull baron lay wounded pyned towarde deth side high auter chirche gray freris said vn sir iohan comyn traytour thou shall deid neu er let myne vauncement shoke swerde high auter smote hede brayn fell doune vpon grounde blod stert high vpon walles yit vn day blod seyn ther water may washe way died nobull knyght holy chirche tratour robert brus saw man wold let coronacion commaunded pouer shuld cum vn crounyng sant iohanes toue scotland pand befell vpon lady day annuncion bisshop glaston bisshop sente andrewes crouned ther kyng robert brus sent iohanes toune made kig pand anone aft er drofe englisshmen cut scotland fled come plened vn kyng edward robert brus driuen land disherited phow kyng edward dubbed westmynstre xxiiij score knyghttis kig edward hered myscheef swore yt shuld bene venged therof said tratours scotland shuld bene honged draw shuld neuer raunsomed pand kyng edward thought vpo falsenesse scottis done sent bachelars englond thei shuld cum londo witsontide dubbed westmynstre xxiiij score knyghtis pth ordeyned nobull kig edward wend scotland vpon robert brus sent hi scotland sir aymer valauce erle penbruke sir henri percy baron wt afair copanye pursued scotis brend toues castels aft er ward come kig hi self wt erles baron fair companye phow robert brus wos discomfited bataill symond frisell slayn friday next assumcion lady kyng edward met robert brus beside sent iohanes toune scotland componye wich companye kyng edward kylled vij thousand pwhen robert brus sawe mischief gan fle hid man might fid sir symond frisell pursued sore turned ayene bode bataill wos worthi knyght bold body ye englisshme pursued eu er sore eu er side kylled stede sir symond frisell rode vpon toke lad vn host pand sir symond began flater speke fair said lordis shall yef iiij marke silu er myn horse myne harnes myne armure becum beggar ptho ansuered theobaude peuenes wos kinges archier god helpe nought thou speketh gold englond wold let go wt maundement kig edward pand tho wos vn king edward kyng wold se commauded lede way haue dome london pand lady eue na te wos honged drow dnd hede smyten honged aye chynes yren vpon galowes hede set vpo london brigge vpo spere ayenst cristemasse body wos brenned encheson men keped body nyght saw mony deuels rampaand gret yren crokys rennyng vpon galowes orabuli turmented body mony saw anone aft er died drede waxen mad sore sekenesse pand bataill take bisshop baston bisshop sent andrewes abbot sconne armed yren men armes fals traitor fals prelatis ayens ther oth wer brought kyng kyng sent vn pope rome shuld done wt phow iohn erle atheles wos taken put deth bataill fled sir iohan erle atheles went chirche ther hid drede myght haue ther refute enchesan chirche wos enterdited thurgh generall sentens chirche wos taken pand sir iohan went well haue scapped deth encheson clamed kynrad kyng edward king nold longer trayed traitours sent hi london hast ther wos honged hede smyten body brend assis prayer ye quene margaret encheso yt clamed kig edwar kynred drawyng wos foryeue phow iohn yt wos willm waleis brod er wos put deth gretest master scotland wer thus done euell deth shendid ther falsenesse iohan wos willm waleis brother wos take done vn deth sir iohn erle atheles wos phow robert brus fled scotland norway tyme wos robert brus moch hated among pepull scotland wyst wos best done hide hi wet norway thee kyng spoused sustre ther held socour haue pand robert brus might foude scotland kyg edward tho let crie pee thurgh lad lawes wer vsid ministres serued thurgh land phow kyng edward died kyng edward abated enmys turned ayene southward maladie toke burgh vpsand marche scotland wist well deth full nigh called hi sir henri laci erle nicholl sir guy erle werwik sir aymer valece erle penbroke sir robert clifford barone prayd vpo faith owed shuld make edward carnariuan kyng englond raathe o myght shuld nat suffre pers ganaston cum ayen englod make son riot grauted wt good pand kig toke sacrement holy chirche good criste man shuld died veray repetance whe bene kig xxxv yere died wos buried westmistre wt moch solempnite vpo who soule god haue mercy pof merlin phecies wer declarid kyng edward wos kyng henri son kyng edward phecied merlin called dragon secund vi kynges shuld regne englond said shuld medeled wyth merci also strength sternesse shuld kepe englond cold hete shuld open mouth toward wale shuld set fote wyke shuld closen wt walles shuld moch harme sede pand said soth good kyng edward medled merci fersenesse wt merci ayens enmys wale aft er scotland fersenesse whe put deth ther falsenesse tratori deseruied pand well keped englond colde hete sith keped maner enmys ronne vpon hym done wronge pand well opyned mouth toward wale made quake thurgh hidour mouth whe coquerid thurgh dynt swerde prince leuelin dauid brother ri morgan wer put deth ther falsenes ther foly pand set fote wike conquered berewyke wich conquest wer slayn xxv thousand vij hondreth take wer brend reed hall pand walles let make shall noyous vn sede shal aft er see lifee sir edward camarauan son pand yit said merlin shuld make riueris ren blod brayn semed well weris ther mastrie pand yit merlin said ther shuld cum pepull north west regne forsaid dragon shuld lad yll grehound shuld drago croune king afterward shuld fle ouer see drede dragon cummyng ayen wos proued sir iohan bailloll kyng edward made kyng scotland falsely arose ayens fled vn landes fraunce neu er come ayen scotland drede kig edward pand yit said merlin pepull shuld lede forsaid grehond shuld fad er le vn till c er tan tyme said soth pepull scotlad gretly wer disesed siith yt sir iohn bailloll ther kig fled fro scotland pand yit said merlin yt son shulde become tyme reed ony blode tokenyng gret mortalite pepull yt well knaw ye scottis wer slayn pand sith said merlin ylke dragoij shuld norish fox shuld meue gret ayens shuld tyme endid pand semed well robert brus yt kyng edward norished chambre sithene stale way meued gret ayenst wich wos endid hys tyme pand afterward merlin told dragon shuld bene hold best body world said sothe good kig edward wos worthiest knyght world tyme pand yit said merlin yt dragon shuld die marche land land shuld long without ony good ke yt shuld wepe deth fro ile shepei vn ile marcill pwherfor ala shold ther songe arthur dredfull well knawen thyn open traitorie euell dethe shalt thow die thow hast well diseruyed pand tho set vpen hede scorn hold chapelet wos rent wos worth half penne pand set vpon leue white toward heuen kyng heuen yef v merci erthely kyng hath v forsakyn frere prechour wenten castell till com place endid lyfe vn shrofe life pand gentill erle held frere wond er fast clothis said fair fadre abide v till dede flesh quaketh drede deth pand soth say gentill erle set vpon knee turned toward est ribaud called higone moston set hand vpon gentill erle saied despite sir traytour turne toward scottes thy soule dede vnderfenge turned toward northe pthe nobull erle thomas ansuered tho myld vois said fair lordis shall done woide frere went sore wepyng anone ribaude went smote hede xi kal auerell yere grece mccc xxi palas eu er getill blod shall done deth cause reson pand tratorsly wos kyng coucellid whe thurgh fals counsell ye spe sers suffred sir thomas vncles son put deth bene heded ayens man er reson gret pitte also nobull kyng shuld desceiued mysgou er ned thurgh counsell fallis spenseres wich tho maiteneyd thorow loselrie ayens honour eke fite aft er ward ther fell gret vengeaunce englond encheson foresaid thomas deth pwhen gentill erle life passid priour monkis pountfret getten body sir thoms kig beried high aut er right side pthat day gentill knyght dede ther honged draw quarell pountfret sir willm tuchet sir willm fitz willm sir warreyn ysell sir heri brad borne sir william cheynye baron iohane page esquyre pand sone aft er yorke draw honged sir rogeri clifford sir iohan mambray baron sir goselin dauill knyght pand bristow drawe honged sir henri wemyngton sir henri mounfort baron glocestre wer draw honged sir iohan geffard sir willm elmebrugge baron pand london wer honged drow sir henri tyes baron wynchelse sir thomas colepepir knyght windesore sir fraunces waldenham baron cantorburi wos draw honged sir bertholome badelesmere sir bartholomewe asshebourneham baron kerdyfe wale sir willm flemmig baron phow kyng edward wet scotland hondreth thousand men armes might spede kyng edward englond brought flour chiualrie vn ther deth thurgh councell consent sir hugh spenser fadre sir hugh son become wode lyon pand eu er spenser wold haue done well kyng loued might done wt thyng liked wherfor kyng yaf vn sir hugh spenser fadre erledom wynchestre vn sir andrewe herkela erdom cardoill preiudice harmyng croune pand kyng edward tho thurgh sell spenser disherited bene ayens quarell thomas lancastre mony oder wer disherited also encheson stat spenser couetted haue ther landes wold desire wrong ayens reson ptho made kyng robert baldok fals piled clerke chauncelar englond thurgh caunsell forsaid spen ser fals ribaud couetise couceled kyng moch kyng let take warde goodis lordis put wrongfully deth hond well token goodis wer holy chirche goodis wythout let bene put tresorie london let call forfaittis bi ther councell kyng wrought eu er dysherite goodis owghten pand thurgh ther counsell let rere talliage goodis englond pwherfor richest kyng eu er wos englond willm basterd norma die conquerid englond pand yit thurgh councell semed ynough bot made yit eu er toune englond find man army vpon ther costages gone vpon scottis wer enmys wherfore kyng wet scotland hondreth thausand armes witsontide yere lord ihu crist mccc xxij pbut scottis went hid moutayns woddis taried englishman fro day day kig myght maner thyng find playn feld pwherfor mony englishme yt litell vitayles died ther hunger wond er fast sodenly goyng comyng namly tho bene ayens thomas lancastre robbed men vpon landis pwhen kyng edward saw vitayles failed wos tho wonderfore discomforted encheson also men died myght speed enmys last come ayen englond pand anone come iames douglas also thomas randulph hoge host englond northumberland englishman wer driue englod come robbed cutre kylled pepull also brend toune wos called northallerton mony toues yorke pand kig herd tidyng let sompne man er men might trauell englishman mett scottis abbey beigheland xv day aft er mihelmasse yere abouesaid englishman wer ther discomfited pand yt scomfiture wos toke sir iohan bretan erle rochemond helde cuntre erldom lancastre pand paied huge raunsome wos let go aft er wente frauce come neu er afterward ayen phow sir andrewe herkela take put vn deth wos erle cardoill tyme sir andrew herkela new made erle cardoill cause taken good erle thomas lancastre ordeyned thurgh kynges mandement englond bring pouer might help ayenst scottis abbey beigheland pand fals tratour gadred pepull myght shuld haue come kyng vn abbey beigheland pthe fals tratour lad cuntre thurgh copeland thurgh erledom lancastre went thurgh cuntre robbed killed folke myght pand forther fals tratour taken gret soume gold silu er sir iames douglas ayens kyng englond bene helpyng holdyng scottis thurgh who treson kyng englond wos discomfited beigheland come thed er pwherfor kyng wos toward wond er wroth let priueli enquere cuntre wos pand men enquerid aspied last trewth foud sought atteynt take fals tratour ye good erle thoms lancastre told wer put vn deth takyng burbrugge pand said yere wer done shuld take hold tratour pand wos holy man said wherfor kyng sent preueli sir anthoyn lucy knight cuntre cardoill shuld take sir andrew harkela put vn deth pand bring thys thyng vn end kyng sent comission andrew take cardoill led vn barre maner erle worthely arrayed swerde gurt aboute hi hosed spored ptho spak sir anthoyn maner sir andrew king put vpon moch thou hast bene orped thy dedis ded moch honour made erle cardoill thou traytour thi lord kyng ladest pepull cuntre shuld haue holpe bataill beiland thou ladest way cuntre copeland thurgh erledom lancastre wherfor lord kyng discomfited ther scottis thurgh thy treson falsenesse thou hadest comen tymes bataill treso thou diddest gret soume gold silu er thou vnderfenge iames douglas scot kynges enmye pand lord kyng ordir knyghod thou vnderfeng thyn honoor worship vpon thy body al brought nought thi estate vndone knyghttes lawer degre mow aft er war wich lord hath vauced hugli diu er se cuntreis englond yt may take exsample ye ther lord aft er ward trewly ser ue ptho commanded knaue anone hewe spors heles aft er let brake swerd ou er hede wich kyng yaf kepe defed land ther made erle cardoill pand aft er let vnclothed furred tabard hode furred cote gurdel wos sir antonye said vn andrew quod art thow knyght bot knaue thi treson kyng thow shalt bene honged drawe thyn hede smyten thi bowelels taken thy body brent thy body quartired thyn desent london ther shall stond vpo londo brigge iiij quarter shall sent iiij toues englond may war chastised bi pand antonye said done maner thyng last day october yere grace mccc xxij yere pand sone turned blod pepull saw durid morne till xi cloke day pof myracles god wrought sent thomas lancastre wherfore kyng let close chirche doris priore pountfret yt shuld cum therin body offren sone aft er good erle thomas lancastre martired ther prest long tyme blind dremed slepyng shuld gone vn hill ther yt good erle thomas lancastre wos done vn deth shold haue sight ayen dremed iij nyghtis fewyng pand prest let lede hill com place martirid full deuoutly made ther praiers prayed god sent thomas myght haue sight ayen o praiers laid right hand vpo place yt good man martired drope dry blod smale sand cleued hand ther striked eeyn anone thurgh might god sent thomas lancastre sight ayen thanked tho almyghty god sent thomas pand whe miracle wos knowen among men pepull come thider eu er side knelid made ther praiers toumbe priorie pountfret praied holy merter socour help god herd ther prayer palso ther wos yong child drenched well toune poutfret wos dede iij dais iij nyghtis men come laid deid child vpo sent thomas tombe holy marter childe arose deth liue mony man saw pand also moch pepull wer owt ther mynd god hath sent ther mynd ayen thurgh u er tu holy martir pand also god hath yeuen ther also crippils ther goyng crokid ther handis ther fete blind also ther sight mony seke folke ther helth diu er se malady loue good martir palso ther wos rich coundom gascoyn maladie right side roted fell away fro hi yt men myght se liu er hert stonke vnneth men might cu ny hi wherfor fredis wer hi wod er sorus bot last god wold praid sent thomas lancastre yt wold prai almyghty god prisoner behight go pountfret done ther pilgrimage thoht yt mertir sent thomas co annoynted ouer sike body pand ther good man awoke wos hole fleshe wos restorid ayen wos roted fallen away pfor wich miracle good man fredis loued god sent thomas eu er mere pand good man come englod toke wt hi iiij felowes come poutfret vn yt holy mart er ther pilgrimage good man yt seke come thed er naked safe priue clothis pand whe done turned home ayen ther cutre told miracle wher eu er come pand also ij haue heled ther mormale thurgh helpe yt holy mart er though yt euell holde incurabull p whe ye spen ser herd yt god miracle holi nold leue man er wise bot said opeli yt grete heresi vertu hi beleue pand sir hugh ye spen ser son saw doyng anoe sent messang er fro pountfret ther duellid ye kig edward tho wos grauen scipton cause kig shold vndo pilgrimage pand o ribaud messiger went toward kig done message come bi hill ther good mart er deth place made ordure went toward kig strong flix come vpo come yorke tho shedde bowel foudement pand sir hugh spen ser herd tydig somedele drad thought vn pilgrimage myght ony man er way pand anoe kig went said shuld gret skland er thurgh cristidom deth thomas lancastre suffred peple ther pilgrimage pountfret coucelled kig comauded closse chirche dores pountfret wich chirche holi marter sent thomas entered thus ayen frauchises forsaid rog er thurgh cousell yaf drinke lest slept ij dais ij nyghtis meyn tyme scappid away wat er yt say bi thamse wet ou er see held fraunce pwherfor kig wos sore annoyed tho put thee stephen costablerie phow quene isabell went fraunce treten pee bytwen hir lord kyng englond king fraunce hir brother kyng went tho vn london ther thurgh cocell sir hugh spen ser fad er son master robert baldoke fals piled clarke chanceler let seise tho quenes landes handis also landis wer sir edward son wer put hir wage ayenst man er reso yt wos thurgh falsenesse ye spesers pand whe kig frauce yt wos quene isabelles brod er herd falsenes sore annoyed ayens kig englond fals coucelers pwherfor sent lett er kig edward vnd er seal yt shuld cu frauce c er ten day done homage ther somened hi elles shold lese gascoyn pand ordeyned englond thurgh kig coucell yt quene isabell shold wend frauce tret pee bitwen hir lord hir brother oliu er yngham shuld wed gascoyn haue vij thousand men mo armes seneshall wardeyne gascoyn wos orddyned yt quene isabel wet ou er se come frauce wt hir went sir aymer valace erle pebrok yt wos ther mordred sodeli ipue sege bot yt wos thurgh godis vegeaunce wos ye iustices yt sentid sent thomas deth lacastre wold neu er aft er repete hi yt wikkid dede yt tim sir oliu er yngha went ou er gascoi moch harme ye kig fraunca tho gat ayen kyng edward lost moch ther phow kyng edward sent sir edward son eldest fraunce quene isabell quart yere duelled frau ce bot sir edward hir eldest son axed leue tho wende fraunce speke mother isabell quene pand fader kyng grauted good said go fair sone goddis blissing myne thike cu ayen hastely thou may pand went ou er see come frauce pand king frauce vncle vnderfenge moch honour said vn fair son ye welco cause fad er come done homage duchie gnyhene auncestres wer wont yeue yt lordship hold heritage man er aucestres fore wher fore called duke gnyhenne phow kig exiled quene isabel edward heldest son kyng edward englond herd kyng edward spen ser herd quene isabell sir edward hir son alied erle henaud wer exiled owt englond encheson thomas lancastre wer sorus thei wist done pwherfor sir hugh spen ser son said vn sir hugh driuen exiled fraunce pand among thynges wer brought deth priuely myght pbut almighty god wold arnold wos high see wos take se land re met high see toke lad ther lord erle henaud moch ioye made taking last arnold priueli stole away fro then come london pand takig od er thiges erle henaud said quene isabell dame maketh meri good chere ye richer ye wened haue bene take thes v barell full silu er wer encheson shuld ordeyn parlament certain place england rodresse amend state reame pand kyng edward ansuerd said lordis quod ye see full well lo haueth seal yef yow pouer ordeyn parlament wher yt ye pand toke ther leue come ayen baron englond pand kiges patent thyng shewed lordis pand tho ordeyned parlamet shuld westmynstre vtas sent hillarie pand gret lordis englond let ordeyn ther ayens yt tyme parlament shuld pand wich day parlament wos kig wold cum ther man er thyng set self assigned pand notheles baron sent vn tyme suore godis soule nold cu ther fote wherfore wos ordeyned gret lordis englod yt shuld longer kyng deposid said wold croune edward sone elder king yt wos ye duke gnyhenne sent tydyng vn kyng ther yt ward vnder sir iohan erle garen sir iohan bothun bisshopp ely sir henri percy barone sir willm trussell knyght wos erle sir thomas lancaster yeld vp ther homage vn englond pand sir willm trussell said thes wordis sir edward encheson ye haue traied pepull englond haue vndone mony gret lordis englond outen cause ye shall deposid ye withstond thanked god pand also encheson ye wold cu lamet ye ordeyned westmynstre lett er patent contend tret lege men kyng shuld pand therfore thurgh comuns assent lordis englond tell vn yow thes wordis ye shall vnder stond sir baron englond assent ye kyng englond vtterly haue put yow rialte eu er pand bisshop ely said tho kyng psir edward heri yeld vp feaute homage erchebisshoppis bisshoppis englond clerge ptho said sir iohan erle garenne sir edward yeld vp vn yow feaute homage erles englond pand sir heri percy yaf vp also ther homage baron englond pand tho said sir willm trussell yeld vp vn sir myne homage also knyghtes englond holden seriauntre man er thyng pso day aft er ward ye shall clamed kyng nother kyng holde pbut fro thys tyme afterward ye shall bene holden singuler man pepull went then london ther lordis englond abode sir edward abade prisonne good kepig wos day conu er sion sent paule thee xx yere regne pof phecie merlin declarid kig edward sone kyng edward frist kyng edward phecied merlin said ther shuld cum goot carre shuld haue horn silu er berd white snow doppe shuld cum nosethriles shuld betoken moch harme hounger dethe pepull gret losse land begynnyng regne shuld hauted moch lechorie pand said soth ala tyme kyng edward kyng edward son bonre carnariuan wale soth horne sylu er berd white o snow made prince walis moche yaf hi riot folie pand soth said merlin prophecie ther shulde cum nose doppe tyme gret honger among poer pepull strong deth among riche died strange land moch sorow scotland aft er ward lost scotland gascoyn while self wos kig ther wos moch lechori hauted pand also merlin told said goot shuld seche flour lyfe deth said soth spoused isabell kynges sustre fraunce pand tyme merlin said thei shuld made brigges folke vpo diches se well seyn banokkes borne scotland whan discomfited ther scottis pand merlin told also stone shuld fall castels mony tounes shuld made playn pand said soth whan kyng edward wos discomfited scotland come tho southward scottis beseged tho castels moch harme brend tounes vn herd erthe pand aft er ward merlin told egle shuld cum cornwaill shold haue fetherris gold pride shuld haue peir shuld despise lordis blod aft er shuld die thurgh bere gausich propheci full wel know found soth pfor egle vnderstond sir pers ganaston tho wos erle cornewaill wonder proud man dispised baronage englod aft er ward heded gausich thurgh erle lancastre thurgh erle werwik pand merlin told tyme sholde seme bere shuld brenne bataill shold vpon arme see feld araied like sheld wher shuld die mony whit hedis pand said soth bi brennig bere betokened gret dred thurgh cuttyng swerdis bataill miton ther come scottis maner sheld man er wynge slew vpo swale men religion prestis seculers wherfore scottis called bataill dispite englishme white bataill pand aft er merli said yt ye forsaid bere shuld goot moch harme shuld vpon southwest also vpon blod said also goot shuld lese mich dele land till tyme shame shuld ou er cum shuld cloth lyon skyn shuld wyn ayen lost thurgh pepull shuld cum northwest shold make bene adrad venge vpon enmys thurgh councell ij owles frist shold ell vndone pand tho two owles shuld wend ou er see strange land ther shuld duell vn till c er tan time aft er sh uld cum englod ayen pand tho two owles shuld moch harme vn moy yt shold cocell goot meue ayens foresaid bere pand ye got owles shold cu arme see borton vp trent shuld wend ou er yt drede ye bere shold fle wt swan copanye buri toward north thurgh vnkind outpulter swan shall slayn sorow bere shuld slayn full ny owne nest shold stond vpo poutfret vpon sonne shall shed bemes mony folke shall seke vertu said soth good erle thomas lancastre borne northwest cosin kig vncle son pand law made kyng lese moch land wich purchesed wilfulli till last kyng ther toke shame self filled wyth cruelte pand gat ayen yt lost moch thurgh folke let assemble northwest yt made adrad venged baron thurgh coucell sir hugh spen ser fadre sir hugh son fore wer owt lawed englond ther wikkednes pbot afterward cume ayen engloed sir hugh spen ser fadre fraunce moch coceled kyng shuld vpon thomas lancastre pso kyng spenser erle arundell ther pouer met thomas lancastre burton vpon trent ther discomfited sir humfry erle herford wos companye pand aft er fled forsaid thomas humfrey ther company burbruge sir andrew erkela called vnkind outpulter pand also sir symondward erle yorke come mete thomas lancastre huge companye ther discomfited scomfiture erle herford wos slayn vpo bruge couherdly spere foundement erle thomas wos take lad vn pautfret tho heded beside castell aft er ward mony men sought miracle god pand tyme merli said sorow harme shuld die pepull land wherfore mony landis shuld vpo bolder pand said soth encheson baron wer done deth sent thomas quarell lancastre pepull mony landis become bold meue vpo kyng ther blod wos turned moy nacions pand aft er ward merlin told said forsaid owles shuld moch harme vn floor life deth shuld bring hir moch disese yt shuld wed ou er se frau ce make pee ye flour delise ther shuld bide till tyme hir sede shuld cum sech hir tho shuld biden bothe till tyme shuld cloth grace tho two owles shold seke put vn pytuus deth phecie wos well know full soth pfor sir hugh spen ser fadre sir hugh sone moch sorow persecucion vn quene isabell thurgh procurment hir lord kyng pso ordeyned amonges put vn hir wage say xx shylling day pwherfor kyng frauce hir brother sore annoyed sent englond letter vn kyng edward shold come vn hys lament paris fraunce kyng edward sore adrade cum ther wened haue bene arested till made amendis trespase sir hugh spenser fadre sone done harme done vn thee quene isabell sustre pwherfor thurgh hir ordeynaunce consent spen ser quene isabell went ou er se frauce make accorde bitwen kyng edward kig frauce hir brother pand ther duelled frauce till edward hir eldest son come hir sech duelled ther till yt aliance made bitwen gentill erle henaud wt ther help might destroi ou er cu venym falsenes spenser yt sir edward shuld spouse dame philip worsshipfull lady erles dought er henaud pwherfor quene isabell sir edward hir son sir edward wodstoke kynges brother englond sir iohn henaud sir roger mortimer wigmore sir thomas rocelin sir iohn crowell sir willm trussell mony liaunce getill erle thomas lancastre wer exiled englond quaril wer disherited ther landis ordeyned gret pouer ariued herewich southfolke pand sone aft er pursued spen ser till wer takyn put vn spitouse deth said ther company also gret falsenes yt thei kig edward pepull pand merlin said also goot shuld put ito gret disese gret anguysh gret sorow shuld lede lyfe pand said soth aftir tyme kyng edward wos take put ward till spenser wer put vn deth pand also encheson wold cum vn lament london ordened assigned baronage also wold gou er ne rule pepull ne ream king shold done pwherfore sum baron englond come yeld vp ther hamages vn ream day u er sion sent paule yere regne xx put rialte eu er eu er leued lyfe afterward moch sorow anguyssh lodewicus fourth wos emprour aft er henri iiij yere lodewic wos duke banare dispised coronacion pope wherfore pope deposit moch labour mony ell aft er trubled gretly vnite holy chirch wos chosin ayens frederik duke austrich ou er come duke boid rebelion end gret parell soule last karolus wos chosin ayens wich puayled sodenly lodewik fell doue horse decessed iohan maundevill doctor fesike knyght borne wos englond bout tyme made meruelus pilgrimage went almost bowt world wrot dedis iij langages decesid wos buried sent albons benedictus xxij wos pope aft er iohn vij yere man wos monke youth wos good conu er sacion doctor diuinite wos made pope reformed ordir sent benet thyng yt necessari wos hard man graut benefice lest grauted vnconyng man made decretall wich began benedictus deus donis suis wos veray cruell faithe som men litell loued wos stout man almost wold know cosyns anno domini miijc xxvij pof kyng edward thrid conquest king edward carnariuan regned sir edward windesore son wich wos crouned kyng annoynted westmynstre thurgh councell consent gret lordis reame sonday candelmasse eue yere grace mcccxxvi w age yt tyme xv yere encheson fadre warde castell kenilworth eke wos put doune rialte reame englond king fromme fest sent katerin yere abouesaid vn fest candelmasse tho wer man er plees kynges bynch astent pand tho wos comanded shereues englond thurgh writ warn tie defendautis thurgh somnyng ayen pand also forthermore prisoner wer kynge gailles yt wer attached thurgh shereues shuld let gone quyte pthe kig edward aft er coronacion praier besechig liege reame grautid chartre stedfast pee yt wold axe pand sir iohn henaud copanye toke ther leue ye kig lordis reame turned home ther cotre ayen eche full rich yeftes eu er ych wos value estate pand tho wos englond pee rest gret loue bitwene kig lordis comynly english men said amoges deuell dede tresour kig fadre tresour spen ser fadre son erle arundell master robert baldok yt wos kinges chancelar detid quene isabellis ordenaunce sir roger mortimer wigmore kyng nothyng ther hir hir deliu er ance ne ther landis aft er ward ye shall phow kig edward wet stanthop mete scottis yit tyme kyng edward castell kenilworth vnder kepyng sir henri erle thomas brother lancastre tho wos erle leycestre kyng grauntid erledom lancastre kyng fadre seised hand put thomas lancastre brother pand erle lancastre leicestre eke stiward englond brother wos tyme sir edward wos kig edwardis fadre made sorow end myght speke wyfe ne wt sone wherfor wos moch mischief though wer wos lad ruled fals councell yit wos kyng edwardis ne called edward long schankis come worthiest blode world pand whome wos woned yeue gret yeftes large wer pue wt kig son wer enmys bi nyght bi day procurid make debate cotake bytwen hi son isabell wife bot frere prechours hi wer good fredis eu er cast bi nyght bi day myght bring hi priso pand amog ther copany yt freris priueli brought ther wos frere called dunhened ordeyned gadred gret copanye folke kepe yt nede frer wos take put castel poufret ther died prison pand sir henri erle lancastre kinges fadre keping thurgh comandemet kig deliu er ed edward kiges fad er bi endetur sir thomas berkeley sir iohn mautreus led castell kemlworth castyll berkeley kept ther saufly pand estren next coronacio kig ordyned huge host fight ayens scottis sir iohn ye erles brother heenaud fro yond se come help kyng edwarde brought hi vij houdreth men armes ariued dou er leue go forth till come yorke ther yt thee kyng abode pand scottis come thed er kyng make pee accorde accordement lasted bitwein tham bot litell tyme pand tyme englisshmen wer clothed cote hodes peynted lettres floures full semeli long berdes therfor scottis made bill wos fastyned vpo chirch doris sent petre toward stangate th said scripture dispite
