debate phow englishman stoppid scottis parke stanhope turned ayen scotland tyme scottis assembled ther pouer comen englond kylled robbed thatt myght take also brennet distroid north cuntre thurgh till come vn parke stanhope wyredall ther scottis held buschement pbut kyng herd thurgh certayn aspies wher scottis wer anone right host beseged within forsaid parke scottit wist wher gone vn ther harmis abiden parke xv day vitales failed eu er side wer gretli appaired ther body pand sith brut come fyrst bretan vn tym wos ther neu er seyn fair host englisshmen lyens men fote wich ordeyned fight scottis thurgh eggyng sir henri erle lancastre sir iohan henaude wold haue gone ou er wat er haue foughten scottis pbut sir roger mortimer co sentid ther priuely takyn mede scottis help myght wend away ayen ther cuntre pand mortimer councelled moch thomas brotherton erle marshall kyng edwardis vncle fersaid thomas shuld assembull tyme vn scottis assentid wist doyng bitwene scottis forsaid mortimer pand encheson marshall englond teyned eu er vauntward sent hasteli erle lancastre sir iohan henaud shuld fight scottis preiudice harmyng fee shuld stond ther perrill pand forsaid erle marshall al araied bateill reredoos erle lancastre haue fought folke meued fight proud scottis pand maner deceyued wist nothing treson thus kyng principalli dissaued pand wos nyght mortimer wach kepe host nyght distrobled wach nothyng myght done pand mei scottys stole nyght toward ther cuntre fast myght pand wos kyng falsly betraied wened traitours land bene brought end wos said pnow ye lordis tratoursly kig edward dissaued meruelusly boldly scottis iamys douglas cc men armes riden thurgh aut host gyng edward nyght scottis wer ascaped toward ther cuntre aboue said till com kynges pauilon killed ther mony men ther beddis cried naward naward od er time douglos douglas wherfor kyng wos pauilon mech od er folk wond er sore afraied blyssid almyghty god ye kyng wos taken gret parell tho ream englond pand yt nyght mone shone full clere bright kig scottis ascappid harmeles pand ye morow wha ye kyng wist yt scottis wer scappid ther cuntre wos wond er sorus full hertely wepid yong eyn yit wist nott hi done yt treson bot yt fals tresoun full well knaw good aft er stori telleth ptho kig edward come ayen yorke full sorowfull host deted eu er man went cuntre full heuy chere mornyng semblant henaudes toke ther leue went ther cuntre kynge ther trauell hugeli rewardid pand encheson viage kyng dispendid moch tresour wasted pand tyme wer seyn ij mones firmament clere derke men might se thurgh world gret debate wos yt tyme ayens pope iohan xxij aft er sent petre emprour almayn tho made emprour ayens popis wyll tho held see auinion pwherfor epror made crie rome ordeyned od er pope yt hight nycholas yt wos frere mynor yt ayens right holy chirch pwherfor wos cursed pouer od er pope sone wos leid encheso suche meruellis wer seyn said world nygh end pof deth kyng edward carnariuan go ayen sir edward carnariuan yt kyng edward fadre sum tyme kyng englond put doune dyngnite ala tribulacion sorow befell thurgh fals councell loued triftid vpo moch aft er ward wer destroyed thugh ther falsenesse god wold pand edward carnariuan wos castell berkelay vnd er kepyng sir moris berkeley sir iohan mautreus made complaynt sorow disese oft tyme axed warden trespased ayens dame isabell wife sir edward son yt made new king yt wold viset pand tho ansuerid wardeynes said worthy lord displese yow shall tell encheson done vnd er stond lady wife come thing ny ye wold hir strangle kyll also ye wold lord son ptho ansuered simple chere ala ala prison god hit wote thought neu er wold wer dede wold god wer wer sorow passed phit long tyme kyng thurgh cell roger mortimer grautid ward kepig sir edward fadre vn sir thomas toiourney forsaid sir iohn mautreuers thurgh kynges lettre put holy forsaid sir morice ward kyng toke led kyng vn castell corfe wich castell kyng hated deth keped hi ther till come vn sent mathewes day septe bre ye yere grace mcccxxvij yt forsaid sir roger mortimer sent man er deth wise shold done deth pand anone forsaid thomas iohan seyn letter commaundemet made kig edward carnariuan good chere good la myght soper nothig ye kig wist ye tratorie pand whe time wos go bedde kig went vn bed lay slept fast king lay slept ye tratourys fals sworne ayens ther homage ther feaute come priueli kynges chambre ther company laid huge tabull vpo wombe men pressed held fast doue iiij corner tabull vpon body wherwith good man awoke wos wond er sore drad dede ther slayn turned body tho vpsedoune ptho toke ye fals traitours wode tirantis horne put hys fundement depe myght toke spit coper brennyng put thurgh horne body oft tymes roulled ther bowel kylled ther lord nothyng wos saued aft er entered glocestre phow kyng edward spoused philip erles doughter henaud yorke aft er cristemasse tho next swyng sir iohn henaud brought wt hi phelip brother dought er yt erle henaud nece englond kig edward spoused hir york moch honour pand sir iohn bothum bisshop ely sir wyllm melton erchebisshop yorke songen thee masse ye sonday eue u er sion sent paule yere grace mcccxxvij encheson kyng wos bot yong tendre age wos crouned full mony wronges wer done fadre leued encheson trowed councelers wer fals bout counceled done wise reson wold wherfor gret harme done reame kyng directid ky dede almighty god wote wher fore wos ordeyned kynges crouning yt kyng tendre age shuld gou er ned xij gretest lordis englond wt wich thig shuld done sai erchebisshop cantorburi erchebishop yorke bisshop wynchestre bisshop herthforth erle lancastre erle marshall erle kent yt wer kiges vnches erle garenne sir thomas wake sir heri perci sir oliu er yngham iohn roos baron pall thes wer sworne trewly councell kyng shuld ansuer eu er yere lament yt shuld tyme yt gou er nall bot ordeynance wos sone vndone yt wos moch harme englond pfor kig ye lordis shuld gou er ne hi wer gou er ned ruled kyng mod er dame isabell sir roger mortimer pand wold thyng wos done emong high low token vn castels tounes landis rentis gret harme losse croune kynges estate mesure phow pee made bitwene english men thee scottis also iustifieng troylebastone kyng edward witsontide secund yere ragne thurgh councell modre sir roger mortimer ordeyned parlament northamton lament kyng thurgh hir councell none land wt age graunted accordid scottis man er yt feautes homage scottis shuld vn thee croune enlond yaf vn scottis eu er chartre enseled pand forthermore endeture wos made scottis vn kyng edward wos kyng henris son wich endenture called rageman wich wer contenyd thee homagis feautes frist kyng scotland prelatis erles baron reame scotland ther seales set theron chartres remembraunces kyng edward baron ther right foresaid reame scotland wos yeue ayen holy chirche also blake crosse scotland wich good kyng edward conquerid scotland brought owt abbey scone full preciouse relique pand also forthermore relesid yaf landis thebarons englond scotland old conquest pand pee hold last scottis wer boud vn kyng xxx thousand pound silu er paid iij yere eu er yere x thousand pound evyne porcions pand forthermore aboue speke bitwen teis aboue said dauid dritonautier kyng robert bruit son fals tyrant fals forsworin ayenst othe arose ayens liege lord nobull good kyng edward falsely made kyng scotland age v yere pand thurgh cursed councell dauid spoused barewik dame iohane toure thatt kyng edwardis sustre geest telleth vpo mare magdalene day yere grace mccc xxviij gret harme empeiring kynges blod wher gentill lady come ala tyme wond er moch fair damisell disaged sith maried ayens commune assent englond fro tyme brut coquered albion named land aft er name bretan called englond name engest pand reame scotland wos holden reame englond croune bi feaute homage pfor brut conquered land yaf vn albanak wos secund son called land albayn name heires yt comen shuld hold brut heires sai kynges bretan feaute homage fro tyme vn tyme kyng edward reame scotland wos holden reame englod feautes seruices aboue said crenicles englond scotland bereth witnesse planarly pand acursed tyme parlament ordeyned northamton ther thurgh fals councell kyng ther falsly disherited yet age pand yit whan kyng edward wos put rialte englond yit men put feautes seruices reame scotland ne fraunchises disherited fer euermore pand neu er thelas gret lordis englond wer ayens confirme pee trew abaue sayd sauf quene isabell tho kynges mother edward bisshop ely lord mortimer bot reson law wold finall pee shuld made twene comune assent englond pof debate yt bitwen quene isabell sir heri erle lancastre leycestre ridig bedford forsaid dauid spoused dame iohane ur toune berrewik fore sayed scottis despite englisshmen called dame iohane cou tesse make pee cowardyse pee tho wos ordeyned kiges son bare wite blame wronge makyng accorde wos done thurgh quen roger mortimer pand long quene isabell ne toke hir hand lordship pountfret almost landis wer value apperteyned croune englond pso kig dispende bot v escheker quene isabell mortimer gret menye ther retenauce yt folowed euermore kynges court went toke kynges prises hir peny worthes good chepe pwherfore contre thei comen wer full sore drad almost distroid ptho began comminalte englond haue enuy isabell quene moch loued hir wen come ayen pursue fals traitours spen ser fraunce pand tyme fals traitour robert holand betraied lord sir thomas lancastre tho deliuered owt prison wonder priue quene isabell also roger mortimer pbot auailed litell taken myhelmasse tho come next sewyng rode toward quene isabell londo sir thomas wither smote heed besides toune sent albons pand sir thomas duelled wt sir heri erle lancastre put hidig dred quene loued wonder moch prayed vn kyng thomas myght exiled englond pand nobull erle sir henri lancastre oft tymys herd comune clamor englishme disese wer done englod also diuerse wronges wer done among comune pepull wich kyng bare blame wrong bot full yong tender age thought good man done way slake sklandre kynges parson myght maner wise kyng ther nothyng gylty wherfor perell lyfe lyme pand assembled retenauces went spake vn kynges honour also amend estate sir thomas brotherton erle marchall sir edmond wodstoke wer kynges vncles also men londo made ther othe maynten quarell pand ther cause wos kyng shuld hold house meny kyng ought done haue riallti yt quene isabell shuld deliu er hir hand kynges man er lordshippis rentis tounes castels aptened vn croune englond quenes hir medle none thyng pand also sir rog er mortimer shuld duell vpon landis wich landis holpe disherited moch pepull comune pepull wer distroyd thurgh wrongfull takyng pand also enquere thee king betraied falsly disceyued stanhop thurgh whois councell scottis went way nyght thee kyng pand also thurgh who coucell ordenaunce made kynges coronacion put doune sai kyng amendement helpyng reame honour shuld gou er ned ruled xij gretest wisest lordis reame shuld thyng ben graunted ne done said wich couenantis maliciusli wer put doue fro kig werfor moni harmes shame reues haue falle kyng ream vnderstond moch edward sum tyme kyng englon ordeyned assent cominalte playn lamet vnd er warde gou er naunce henri erle lancastre cosin saluacio body take castell kemlworth ther ward thurgh colour quene isabell mortimer consent lament toke lad ther neu er aft er none kynrad myght speke ne se aft er tretoursly toke mordred who deth arose sclandre thurgh cristendo done pand also tresour sir edward carnariuan left moy place englond wale wer wasted borne away without kyng edward son destruccion folke also thurgh who councell kyng yaf vp kigdo scotland wich reame kynges ancestres full sore trauaill mony nobull man ther right deliu er ed vn dauid wos robert brus son right right reame world wist pand also bi chartres remembrance yt ye right scotland wer take tresorie taken vn scottis ye kynges enmys disherityng hys successours gret harme vn liege gret reproue vn englisshmen eu er palso wherfor dame iohana tour kynges sustre edward wos disaged marid vn dauid yt wos robert brus son yt traitour enmye vn englond thurgh who councell wos take enmys handis englond pand meyn good erle henri lancastre companie toke councell thes pointes aboue said myght amendid vn worsship kig fet fite also liege pand quene isabell thurgh coniecting sotelti also mortimer let ordeyn parlament salisberi pand yt lamet mortimer made erle march ayenst baron englod preiudice kyng croune sir iohn eltham kyng brother gurt swerd cornwaill tho wos called erle cornewaill eu er quene isabell moch pracurid ayens hir son kyng ward forsaid sir edward landis pand lament erle lancastre wold cum ordeyned al pouer ayens quene isabell mortimer men londo ordened v hondreth men armes pwhe quene isabell wyst doyng swore god bi name full angrely euell tyme thought vpo tho pointes ptho sent quene isabell mortimer aft er ther retene kynges retenue ordeyned amonge theem huge host councelled kyng yt vpo nyght riden xxiij myle toward bedford erle lancastre wos pani thought haue hi destroied yt nyght rode bi side king hir son knyght armed dred deth pand done kyng vnd er stond yt erle henri lancastre companie wold haue distroid kyng coucell euer wherfor kig wos somdele towardis hi heuy annyed pwhan erle marshall erle kent kiges brod er herd tyding riden message bitwen king grauted pee erle henri lancastre c er tan rau sone xim pound yt wos neu er paied aft er ward pand thes wer lordis held sir henri lancastre sir henri beamot sir fouke fitzwaren sir thomas rocelyn sir willm trussell sir thomas wyther hondreth knyggtis mo yt wer concentid tho wer exiled thurgh coucell quene isabell mortimer mortimer weited haue ther landis myght thurgh ony maner iecting couetous moch wos gret pitte phow kyng edward went ou er see homage vn kyng frauce duchie gnyhen wos long aft er kyng fraunce thurgh co cell dousepe sent kyng edward englond shuld cume paris done homage reson wold duchie gnyhen pand thurgh counsell lordis englond kyng edward went ou er see ascencion tide come vn paris thrid yere regne homage vn kyng frauce kyng vnd er fenge homage made hi moch ioye worsship pbut kig edward made homage hasteli sent englod thurgh quene isabell moder anone hastely come ayen englond vpon witsonday takyng leue kig frauce wherfore wos wond er wroth phow sir roger mortimer bare proudly hie shall ye sir roger mortimer wygmore dissired couyted high state yt kyng graunted called erle marche thurgh lordship pand become proud hauteyne wold lese forsake name ancestres euer pand encheson let call erle marche none comuns englond durst call bi name name called thurgh kyng crie men shuld call erle marche pand mortimer bare hauteyne proud wond er wit also disgised hi wt wond er rich clothes man er reson shapping wering wher englisshmen gret wond er whot maner myght contreue find man er pride said amo ge comenli prid shold long endure pand tyme sir geffrey mortimer yong yt mortimer son let call kyng folie befell aft er ward dede wos full pride writchednesse held rou de tabull wale men thid er come contrefete doig man er kyng arthur tabull bot openli failed nobull kyng arthur wos worthy lord renoune yt world tyme yit come neu er none aft er al nobull knyghtis cristendome dede armes asayed duellid kyng arthur held ther lord soferen pand wos well sayn quered bataill roman wos called froll get reame frauce kylled handis pand also faught geant wos called dinabus kylled rauesshed fair eleyn wos kyng hocles nece kyng litell bretan pand aft er ward kylled bataill emprour rome wos called lucie assembled ayens king arthur fight moch pepull roma phethis sarisens yt man coud nobre discomfited stori telleth pand ye tyme comune loo sprong englod thurgh coniecting ordinauce freres prechours sir edward carnariuan wos kyng edward fadre geest telleth said liue castell corf wherfor comyns englond wer sorow dred wherfor wer wist traitoursly mortimer done mordrid phow edmod wodstok yt wos erle kent kinges brother edward carnariuan heded wynchestre vpo tyme befell sir edmond wodstoke erle kent spake vn pope iohan xxij auinion said almyght good oft tymes done thomas loue lancastre mony gret miraclls mony men woman wer thurgh diu er se malady undone vn world thurgh praier wer brought vn ther helth pand sir edmond praied pope herteli wold graute grace yt forsaid thomas myght translatid pope said nay shuld translatid vn tyme wer bett er c er tefied clargie englond seyn ther obedece thyng god done loue thomas lancastre suggestion forsaid edmod erle kent vn made pand whan edmond saw myght spede purpose tochyng translacion praied coucell toching sir edward carnariuan brod er said long gone wos kyng englond thig might best done toching deliu er ance sith comune fame thurgh englod liue hole sauf pwhan pope herd hi tell sir edward liue comauded erle vpo benison shuld help wt pouer yt myght yt wer deliu er ed prisun ue body man er yt might bring thig end assoyled hi copani pena culpa tho holp deliu er ance ptho toke edmod wodstoke leue pope come ayen englod wha sir edmond wos come su frere precheurs come said yt sir edward brod er yit wos liue castell corf vnder kepig sir thomas gurnay ptho sped forsaid edmod fast o might till come castell corf queynted hi spak fair wt iohn dauerell yt stable castell yaf rich yeftes haue acqueyntance knaw coucell pand thus befell forsaid sir edmod praied specially tell priuely lord brother sir edward leued wer dede wer liue praied ons haue sight pand sir iohan dauerill high herted man full curage ansuerid shortely vn sir edmond sad sir edward brother helth vnder kepyng durst shew vn man sith defended kynges half edward edwardis son carnariuan also thurgh commaundement quene isabell kynges modre sir rog er mortimer shuld shew body vn maner man world sauf vn vpon lesyng life limme disherityng heiris eu er pbut fals traitour falsly lied ward wos take then lad vn castell berkeley thurgh sir thomas gurnay thurgh maudemet mortimer til wos dede said sir edmod wodstoke wist nothyng edward brod er dede wher vpon toke lettre vn kig edward brod er worthi lord pand vnderfeng letter hight message man er faill sir edmod toke leue forsaid iohn wet tre lordship kent ther pand anone iohn wist yt sir edmond wos gone kent lordship anone went hast myght fro castell corf comen vn sir roger mortimer toke letter sir edmod wodstoke erle kent take closed enseled seale pand sir rog er mortimer vnd er feng letter vnclosid saw coteyned theri began rede wherof begynnyng wos pworshippes reu er en brother legeaunce subieccion sir knyght worsshipfull dere brod er plese pray hertely yt ye good coforth shall ordeyn ye shall cum prison deliu er ed disese ye vnd er stondeth gret lordship haue assentant almost ye gret lordis englond ther apparaill sai wt armure wt tresour nombre maynten yor quarell ferforth ye shall kyng ayen ye wer haue suorne vpon boke well prelatis erles baron pwhen sir roger mortimer saw vnd er stode myght thee strength lettre anone hert wroth gan boll euel hert bare toward sir edmond wodstoke erle kent hast myght went vn dame isabell quene wos kiges mod er shewed hir sir edwardes lettre purpose coniected ordeynde put doune kyng edward wyndesore hir son rialte kyngdom pnow certis sir rog er qd hath sir edmond done fadre soule quod bene therof auenged god graunte life shorte tyme pand quene isabell went vn ye kyng edward hir son ther thee lament wynchestre haue mende wronges trespaces doon among pepull reame pand tho toke shewed letter sir edmond wodstoke erle kent made enseled seale bad vpon hir benyson shuld venged vpon edmond vpon dedely enmye ptho quene wroth toward sir edmond erle kent cessid neu er pray vn hir son till sent hast pand vpon kyng sent lettres aft er sir edmond wodstoke shuld cum speke wynchestre man er thyng left pand whan sir edmond saw kyng sent aft er lettres enselid hasted myght till come vn wynchestre wen quene wist ser edward wos cumyn wynchestre tho anone praied fast went vn kyng edward hir son good erle wos restid anone lad vn barre robert hamond wos coroner kynges house hold associed vn sir roger mortimer tho spake foresaid robert said psir edmond erle kent ye shall vnd er stond done v witt principally vn liege lord kyn edward englond myghty god saue kepe ye dedely enmye tratour also comune enmye vn reame ye haue ben bout mony day make priue deliu er aunce sir edward sum tyme kyng englond brother wich put doune rialte comun assent lordis englond pesyng lord kyng estate also reame ptho ansuerid good man said forsoth sir vnd er stondeth well neu er traitour kyng ne ream god world therfore kinges leue shall pue defend man aught ptho said mortimer sir edmod ferforth know may well gaynsaid yt presens shal well proued fals mortimer lettre sir edmond taken vn sir iohan dauerill castell corf take kyng edward brother sir edmond wist ne supposed thyng sir iohn dauerell bene fals deliu er letter wise vn mortimer thought man er thing yt letter tha mortimer said sir edmod shewed lett er seled axed yt knew yt letter seal pthis sir edmond loked ther vised long tyme printe seal might se lett er wos theri wist well seal thought letter yt bore gret charge thought thing od er lett er said openly hering ye forsoth seall forsake plo quod mortimer sire ye hereth said knowleches hi yt lett er seal ye shall conteyued ther pand mortimer opened letter folden afore gedre red openli word word hering pand whe lett er red said lo sire ye haue herid written yt hath knowlecheth letter seal may go ther fro pand cried yaf dome shuld honged draw hede smyten man er trator heiris disherited eu er lad forth put prison pand wos done quene wist wos dampned way law life limme heires disherited eu er thurgh opyn knowle chyng playn court pwherfore thought wer good forsaid sir edmond wer hasteli kylled wittig kyng el kyng lyghtly wold yef deth shuld turne moch sorow o wos enpeched pand anone quene thurgh councell mortimer ony councell sent hast balifs wynchester shuld smyte sir edmond hede wodstoke erle kent maner bydyng respite vp payn lyfe lyme shuld haue none execucion cause tarieng withstonding iugemet tho toke balifs sir edmond priso lad beside castell wynchestre ther made gong fermer smyte hede none durst done died ther ala sai x day october iij yere kyng edwardis regne whan kyng wist ther wos wond er sorus let entier frere mynors wynchestre pof deth sir roger mortimer erle march befell tyme sir roger mortimer erle marche proud se hauteyn helde lord reame pere tho become couetous yt folowed dame isabell quenes court wos kyng edwardis modre beset penyworthis wt offics quenes housold man er kynges officer made takyng tochyng vitalles also cariagis spensis gadre tresur nombre yt myght ptho made hym wond er priue quene isabell moch lorship reteneu yt al gret lordis englond wer adrad wherfore ye kyng cocell towardis hi wer agreued ordeyned among vndo hi thurgh pure reso law cause yt king edward yt kyng fadre traitoursly thurgh mordred castell berkeley bofore said planly ye part boke deth pand su wer ye kynges cocell loued ye martimer told priuete kig coucell wer fro day day hi shend vndon wherfor mortimer sore annoyed angri ye deuell ayens yt wer kiges coucell said wold tha bene avenged euer toke pit long aft er ward kynd edward dame phelip wife dame isabell kyng modre sir rog er mortimer ne went vn notyngham ther sodiorne befell quene isabell thurgh councell mortimer toke hir key yatis castell notingham man mygh cum nother ne nyght thurgh commaundement mortimer ne kyng ne none councell pand fell mortimer deuell wroth bolled also wrath ayens kyng men edward principally ayenest accused kyng ye deth sir edward fadre pand puely coucell take bitwen quene isabell mortimer bisshop lyncoln sir symond beford sir hugh trumpyngton od er priue ther cou cell vndone accused mortimer vn kyng fadres deth treson felonie pwherfore al tho wer kynges councell whan wyste thee mortimer castyng priuely come kig edward said yt mortimer wold destroy cause yt accused kig edwardis deth fadre praid yt wold maynten ther right pand thes lordis pursue quarell sir william mountagu sir humfrey de bo hun sir william brother sir rauf stafford sir robert hereford sir willm clinton sir iohn neuil hornby moy othre ther conset thes sworen vpon boke mayten quaril moch myght pand befell aft er sir william mo tagu ne none kiges frendis must nat herbrugged castel mortimer went toke ther herbrughe diu er se place toune notyngham pand tho sore adrad lest mortimer shuld destroy hast thei come vn kyng edward ser william mountagu tho yt wos castell priueli told ne none companie shuld take mortimer coucell help willm eland stabul castel c er te kig loue wel therfore councel yt ye go forsaid stabull commaund name fiend help take mortimer thing left vpon parill life limme ptho said mountaygu sir lord grout mercy ptho went forth forsaid montaygu come custabull castell told ye kyng pand ansurid said ye kynges shuld done moch myght yt wold spare fore man er deth swore made oth ptho said sir willm mountagu conestabull hering helpyng vn quarell pnow c er ti dere frend v behoueth worch quentyse take mortimer sith ye ke castell haueth keyes ward sir quod constabull ye vnd er stond gate castell ben lokked lockis dame isabell send hider nyght hath key therof lieth vnder leuesell bed vn morow ye may cu castell bi ye yates man er wise pbut knowe aley stretcheth ward vnder erth ye forsaid castell goth west wich aley dame isabell quene ne none hir men ne mortimer ne none companie knoweth pand shall lede thurgh aley ye shall cum thee castell aspieng oni yt ben emnys pand thee nyght sir willm mou tagu ye lordis quarel stabul also wet horse made semblat wer wend mortimer sight pbut anone ye mortimer herd tydyng wet yt wold haue gon ou er see dred hi anone companie token councell amonges let ther passage sent lettres anone thee porte none ye gret lordis shuld wed home ther cutre bot arestid take pand amog od er thing willm eland conestable ye foresaid castel priueli lad sir william mountagu compain foresaid way vnd er erth til com ye castell went vp toure mortimer pbut sir hugh trumpyngton ascried hidously said traitours nought ye comen vn castell ye shall die yit euell deth eu er ychon anone mountagu companie vp mace smote hugh vpo heed brayn brest fel ground dede euell deth ptho toke mortimer armed toures dore hard noyse dred quene isabell saw mortimer taken made moch sorow hert thes wordes vn said pnow fair sire pray ye ne harme body worthy knyght welbeloued frend dere cosyn ptho went then come brought mortimer presentid vn kyng edward commaunded bring sauf ward anone yt wer consent vn mortimer doyng herd tell taken went hid priuely nyght went toune eche side heuy hert mornyng leued vpon ther landis well myght pand yere mortimer take retene ix score knyghtis squyers sergiauntys armes fote men pand tho mortimer lad london sir symod beford lad take conestabull toure kepe pbut aft er ward wos mortimer liif examined westmynstre kig al gret lordis englod ill yt might fall reame enquere also wich assentyng sir edwardis deth kiges fad er also thurgh scottis ascappid stanhope scotland kyng edward pand also chartre ragman deliu er ed vn scottis wherin homag feautes scotland conteyned yt scottis shuld done eu er english kig reame scotland wherfore abs dampned draw honged treson myschief come vn sent andrewes euen ye yere incarnacio lord ihu crist mccc xxx phow kyng edward get ayen vn grociously homage feautes scotlad wher put thurgh fals coucell isabell modre sir roger mortimer new made erle marche ye haue hard lordis sir iohan bailloll time pee chosen kyng scotland encheson come eldest doughter erle dauid hontigton thas wos kyng alexandre brether scotland died heir body begoten iohan made feaute homage kyng edward henris son iij land scotland aft er ward withsaid homage thurgh councell scottis yere lord mcc lxxiiij sent vn ye pope thurgh fals suggestion yt made oth vn forsaid kyng edward ou er astate wich othe pope assoilled thurgh bulsis hi sent pand none kig edward wist ther ordeyned anoe baron come vn berewike querid toue wich coquest ther sloyn xxvm vijc bailloll kig scotland co yeld hi good kig edward kig aft er ward deliu er ed hi tour londo gret lordis scotlad tho taken berewik yaf sauf condithis gone scotland pand scottis sith thurgh ther falsenesse wered vpon good kyng edward pand sir iohan bailloll kig scotland saw went ou er see vn dunpier leued ther vpo landis well myght till scottis wold amend thermisdedis trespace lad sir edward son wherfore scot dispite called sir iohan turnlabard beca wold offende ne trespace ayens good kyng edward englond pand soke reame scotland set thar litell price pand sir iohn long tyme duelled fraunce till died ther sir edward son vnderfeng heritage homage vn kyng fraunce landis dunpier fell aft er ward edward yt wos iohn bailloll son hi squyer englod wos borne yorkshire called iohn barnabi edward bailloll loued moch wos ny full priue pand iohn barnaby debate frensh man toune dunpier killed wet wai hast myght castell haue socour help lord pand anoe come ye officer toue take iohan barnaby felon sir edward lord holp hym rescued nyght made hi wed castell went way come englod harme pand kyng frauce saw sir edward rescued felon become wond er wroth ayens sir edward anoe let arestid toke hand landis ptho duelled sir edwar prison vn tyme sir henri beaumont come fraunce wich henri sum tyme erle angos scotland thurgh wife wos put forsaid erldom whe accordemet bitwen englond scotland thurhh quene isabell sir rog er mortimer ther copani mariage made bitwen dauid wos robert brus son dame iohana atte toure kyng edwardis sustre englod well vnd er stode yt end shuld cum right wer thurgh sir edward bailloll right heir reame scotland pand kyng frauce lowys loued moch sir henri full priue thought make deliueraunce sir edward baillolls body migh man er wyse ptho praied kyng yt wold graunte grace sir edward baillolls body vn next lament myght lyue rentis meyn tym myght stand iuged bi peri parlamet pand kyng grautid praier made forsaid edward deliu er ed prison man er aboue said anone wos priso sir henri toke forth lad englond made duell priuely maner sandhall vp onse yorkeshire lady vescy ordeined ther houge retenaunce pepul englisshmen also alien conquere ayen heritage pand yaf moch silu er vn sowdiours alien help hi pand behight help myght failed hi nede pand tyme donald erle morrif herd tell sir edward bailloll wos priuely cum englond come made gret ioye comig ayen said vn behight gret lordis englond shuld entendant shuld hold hyng right heir scotland homage feaute ptho come sir henri beaumont kyng edward englond praied way charite wold graut grace vn sir edward bailloll myght saufly gone bi land sandhall vn scotlond coquere right heritage scotland pthe kyng ansuerid said suffre ye bailloll wend thurgh land scotland pepull wold say shuld assentyng vn compani pnow sir pray yow ye wold yef leue tak wt hi soudiours englishman myght saufly lede thurgh yowr land vn scotland pand sir vpon couenaut befal god forbide discomfited batell thurgh scottis also lordis holden wt bailloll bene eu er rentis haue englond pand ther kyng vpon thys couenaunt graunted ther bone tochyng tho wer quarell wich clamed haue landis rentis ream englond pand thes wer name lordis pursued mater say sir edward bailloll chalenged reame scotland sir henri beammont erle angos sir dauid stroboly erle atheles sir geffrey monbray walt er comyn mony od er yt wer put ther heritage scotland whan pee wos made bitwen englond scotland said pand ye shall vnd er stond yt thes lordis toke wt v hondreth men armes ij thousand archer fote men tho wet ship rauenspore sayled se till yt come vn scotland come land kynkehorne xij myle fro sent iohanes toune anone sent ther shippis ayen shuld hurte ne empayrid nether yt man shuld go shippis ayen though yt nede bot bide rillis fle stad rather suffre deth flee maynten ther trew quarell pwhen erle fiffe fers man sterne herd yt bailloll comyn take land scotland come hast kynghorn xij thousand scottis destroy hi shuld cum land pbut sir edward bailloll compani ther descomfited ye wich discomfiture sir alesand er seton wos ther kyllid mony od er pthe erle fiffe tho sore full yll shamed litell compani discomfited shamly put al compani yt lyue flee ptho come sir edward bailloll token cuntre till com vn abbey dunfermilyn ther found vitallis folke among thyng fond chambre bout v hondreth gret stauis fine oke long pykis yren stele toke deliu er ed strongest men compani pand anone went fro then logged felde ij myle sent iohanes toune burgies toune herd erle fiffe discofited thurgh bailloll wer sore adr br ken ther brugges hed made ou er water erne bailloll myght gone ou er wherfore loged hi ther nyght litell hede toke rest said vn pepull pnow dere lordis ye know full well logged bitwen enmys may v hampre ther bote deth wherfore abide still nyght leue shall turne v moch sorow harme pouer scotland may eu er day wax encrece may done bot litell pepull ayenst pwherfor pray loue almyghty god make v bold hardy yt may mighteli take scottis nyght boldely vpon let v pursue night traueled thurgh v se oure heidines od er scottis yt se traueled wery sorer adrad v fight fersely shall fight pursue thurgh grece god almyghty world shall speke doughtynesse chiualrie pand sire vnd er stondeth wel yt ye companye yt comen sir edward bailloll grauted wel vn councell werther right glad anone pursued vpon scottis becomen wonder wery pand bailloll companie sore folowed moch harme sorow thurgh ther assaut might febull help litell pepull pbut tho said scottis amonges befall litell pepull bailloll hath wynge done v moch trauell sorow pnow certes semeth v wyrketh bi grace wond er gracious quarell c er te shall dede may cum hi v yeld sith fadre set v price pand among thinges bailloll pepull passed wat er erne sir roger swynerton son wos fers angri went forth saw pepull armes ful well araied forth went vn faught kyled take mony wold abide pand nothles assaute wend bene gret host scotland pand whe come morow gadred gedre restid ye yt englisshme rested nobull baron thomas vescy nobull baron stafford prikked ther hors vp doue hilles kepe estres cutre pricked vp doue saw gret ost good aray ordeyned ther wynges wt helmys sheldis shynyng coig vpon pand ther come tho two lordis ayen vn baillollis folke said loue god almyghty bene good co forth ye shal haue bataill anone right pand tho spak sir fouk son gareyne baron gret renowne dede armes psirris lordinges vnd er stod say haue seyn mony diu er se wiges well amog sari iues amog scottis yit saw neu er fourth te wynge fight ther far ye abide enmys ynow fight ayes good hert good fight wt c er ti bene full ayens compani pand therfore loue god take v good hert let v bene bold thynke neu er wife ne childre bot onli conquere enmys bataill pand thurgh help lord god shall ou er cum pand yt come host scottis towardis full serely ayens sir edward bailloll iij batai le well araied armure pand wond er fersly come toward bailluls compani whan sir donald erle marcill yt scottis saw said vn robert brus son robert brus thes wordis psir robert full sore forthynketh hart yt thes pepull yt bailloll hath brought shuld die wt dynt scottis swerdis sith cristyn men well ben pand therfor thynke wer gret charite send vn yeld vn mercy raunson thurgh grevos ranson moch haue taken land done ill pnow certes quod sir robert brus haue well saued yt thou art enmy traytour vn scotland sith yt thou sent saue dedeli enmys yt hath done v moch sorow shame semeth well ye bene ther assent pnow c er te robert quod sir donald falsly ye lie ther copani ne ther sent hastely ye shall see fight rather pani pand c er ti sir robert said shall maugri thy hede assaill thou pand wt yt pricked ther stedis fersly vpo caskemore ther wyng folewed renge tho come met bailloll copani hongyng bough strat passage fast hasted vn ye englisshmen yt thousandis fell groud ech ou er hepe hors man pthe bailloll men myghtely stode ayens fast killed scottis groud mony sore wouded log till yt stod vpo foyned ther suerdis speris thurgh body sore traualed vpo till yt thei become wond er weri wist scottis wer left liue fled away saue self ye best man er myght pand tho pursued sir edward bailloll men killed till nyght fro thes thei went sent iohanes toue toke held ther vitailed self ther fouden inough wherwith make meri ptho made bailloll men yt wer wodid go ship wend englod hele ther woudes pand yt time ther flemig see strong thefe robber wos caled crabbe pand flemmyng driuen flaudres wikkednes therfore come scotland hold scottis moch harme vn thee englisshmen myght pand crabbe met bailloll men se wer wounded bataill wer sent ayen englond hele ther wound crabbe yaf vn gret assaute wold haue killed euerychon bot englishman defendid well manly discomfited crab companie pand tho gan fle scotland come toward sent iohanes toune fond gret copany scottis wer comen ayen gedre discomfiture gaskemore wich beseged bailloll men toune sent iohn anone told scottis wos disco fited englisshmen wer woudid gaskemore wet toward englod hele ther woudes said scottis shuld haue pouer ne myght ne grace yen edward bailloll encheson scomfited empired chiualri scotland handfull men accompt yen scottis wer slayn wherfor coucelled remeue sege sent iohanes toune kepe best maner yt thei coude might pthe scottis vnd er stod yt crab said sothe forsoke ye sege wet then night helpe self best man er yt thei might pwhen thing wos know thurgh scotland lordis knyghtis wer discomfited gaskemore scotland thurgh sir edward bailloll pye shall vnd er stond lordes lady gentils scotland com wo der fast sent iohanes toune yeld vn baillol homage feaute ther landis yelde pee resaued frely pand fro thes wet abbey scone ther crouned kyng scotland aft er let crie pee thurgh land pand tyme befell kyng edward held lament among liege new castell vp tyne amed trespaces wronges done land sir edward bailloll kyng scotland come thid er feaute homage reame scotland pand maner kyng edward englond gadred ayen homage feautes scotland wher put thurgh councell assent dame isabell modre sir roger mortimer erle marche tho toke bailloll kyng scotland leue kyng edward englond went then land sotland set bot litell counceled holpen quarell wherfore went fro went leued ther landes rentis scotland pand befell afterward long kyng scotland ne remeued come toune anand ther token duelling thidder come company knyghtes strong men worthy yeld vn kyng bere fair dede countinaunce yt trustid moch vpo pand anone traytours saw trust moch vpon ordeyned amonges l compani wold haue kyled ther lord kyng pbut thurgh grace almighty god brake thurgh walle hole chambre o god wold ascappid theyr trecherie men wer kylled ascappid moch dred vn toune cardoil ther held sore anoyed befell lady eue concepcion ptho sent kyng edward bailloll kyng edward englond falsely tratoursly litell tyme put shame sorow thurgh liege men vpon trustid wod er moch praid loue god yt wold maynten help ayens enmys pthe kyng englond gret pitte behight helpe socour sent word shuld hold pee still forsaid cite cardoill till gadred pouer ptho ordeyned kyng edward englond coucell london let gadre men diu er se shire englond whan wos redi went toward thee toune berewill vpon twede thid er come vn kig edward bailloll scotland pouer beseged toune made toune fair toune pauilons iked dred thee scottis made mony assaute gonnys engynes toune wherwith distroid mony fair house chirches also wer bet doune vn erth gret stone spituusly come gonnys engynes notheles scottis kept well toue tho two kynges might come theri long tyme pand notheles kiges abyde ther log till tho toune failed vitales also wer wery wakyng wist done pand ye shall vnderstad thas tho scottis wer toune berewik thurgh commune coucell ther assent let crie vpon walles toune might haue pee englishman ther praied kyng grace merci praied trewes viij day vpo couenaunt wer rescued side toune toward scotland scottis viij day wold yeld vn kyng toune also pand hold couenant proferid ye kyng xij hostage toune berewik pwhen hostage wer deliu er ed vn kyng anone tho toue send vn scottis told ther sorow mischief pand thee scottis come tho priuely ou er wat er twed bought abbey sir willm dyket wos tho stiward scotland mony yt come put ther gret ill self yt tyme ther life come ou er brugge wos broken stone away mony ther copani wer ther drenched forsaid willm went ou er companie come bi shippis englond kylled barge hul xvi men went toune berrewik water side pwherfore scottis held tho toune rescued asked ther hostage ayen kyng englond pand thee kyng sent word ayen axed hostage wrong sith come toune englond side couenant bitwen toune shuld rescued half scotland pand anone kyng edward tho comaunded yeld toune wold haue hostage pand scottis said toune rescuyd wel ynowgh ther wold hold pwhen kyng edward saw scottis brek ther couenaunt made wos wond er wroth anone let take sir thomas fitzwillm sir alexand er seton wardeyn berewik wich thomas wos person dunbar let take fyrst fore hostage encheson sir alexander fadre wos ke toue pand tho commaunded eu er day ij hostage toune till wer done deth yeld toune pand shuld teche breke ther couenauntes pand tho toune herd thes thing becomen wond er sorus sent kyng englod wold graunte viij dais respet bitwe tho hondreth men armes xx men armes myght strength gone bytwen toune berewyk vital toune must holde rescued pand wer xxi xxij wer slayn tho hundreth beforesaid toune shuld holden rescued x yere duke norfolke eu er pand sir thomas arundell erchebisshopp cantorbury wos exiled tyme eu er depesit see malice kyng anone thes iij worthy lordis wer commaunded defendid kynges reame anone gat shippis diu er se hauens went ouer see diuerse landis eche way pand duke norfolke wet venice ther died who soule god haue merci amen pand kyng richard made clarke sir rogier walden ercheaisshop cantorburi pand xxij yere kyng richardis regned fals councell ymaginacion couetous men wer wer made ordeyned blanke chartres made enseled maner rich thurgh reame moch compelled diuerse pepull set ther seall ther wos done gret couetise wherfore good hertis reame wer clene turned away kyng eu er pand vttirly destruccio end high excellent prince king thurgh couetous fals coucell falsely betrayd ala pitte yt kig myght se pand tha king richaid set kigdome riall land englond ferme vn iiij son ye wich wer thes sir willm strop erle wylteshire tresorer englond sir iohn bussh henri grene sir iohn bagot knyghtis wich turnid mischief deth litill tyme ye shall aft er ward find writtyn pand tha king richard made gret ordynauce wet ou er se irland moni gret lordis gret hostis strength ther king men armes archiers moch gret stuf right good ordynauce longed vn pand passed ou er se ordand made sir edmod langley vncle duke yorke liuetenaut englond absent gou er nance coucell thes iiij knyghtis take englod ferme kyng tha passed se come irland ther wos well worthely reseyued pand thees rebelles ben called wild irishme co doue kyng yeld bothe body goodis suore vn liege men ther ther homage feaute good seruice thus conquered partie irland litell time pand kyng richard thus irland sir henri bolingbroke erle derby kig made duke herford wich duke kyng exiled owt land comen ayen englond chalenge thee dukedom lancastre right trew heritage come doune fraunce land vn calays pand ther met sir thomas arundell wos erchebisshopp cantorburi wos exiled englond com erle arundell son heir wiche wos ward kepig sir ion shelley knyght sum tyme wt erle huntigdone duke excestre thee wich wos tho thee castell reigate southsex ther stole away come calais ther wos kepid well worthely till thees othir two lordis wercomen calais worthy duke erchebisshop cantorburi arundell shippid hauen calais drew ther course northward ariued yorke shire rauensporne fast wydelyngto ther come entred thee land two lordis ther manye pand moche pepull reame yt herd commyng knewen wher wos anane drew vn welcomed lordis coraged maner thyng passed forth land gadred moch pepull pand whan kyng richard herd wist thees ij lordis wer cumen ayen englond wer londid pthan kyng left ordynauce irland come englondward hast yt myght come thee castell flint ther abode take councell myght com none pand sir thomas percy erle worcestre yt kiges stiwarde wyst knew anone come hall amoges pepull brake thee yerde riall kynges housold anone euery man wos dis bled euery man went way soke ther mastir souerayne lord left alloyn pand thus wos kig richard brought doune destroid stoden self allone without comforth socour ani good councell man ala pite riall kyng pand anone come tidynges yt sir henri boligbroke wos vp wt wonder strong pouer pepull squiers englond risen vp thee shire stregthig hi ayen thee kyng richard thus sone wos come thee north cuntre bristow ther met sir willm scrope erle wylteshire tresorer englond sir iohan bussh sir henri grene iohan bagot ascapid went ou er irland thes iij knyghtis wer taken thir hedis smyten thus died ther false couetise pand wos kyng richard take brought vn duke anone duke put fast ward strong hold vn comyng londo ther romer londo strong noyse kyng richard com westmynstre pepull londo ranne thidder wold haue done moch harme scathe ther wodenesse maire alderman othir worthy yere kyng henris regne iiij let moke galeys hoped haue passed gret see forth ierusale ther haue endid liffe god viseted sone wt infirmites gret sikenesse myght well endure feruently wos take brought mccccxiij who sovle god haue merci anen arti v wos aft er iohn xiiij yere chosen thee coucell costantinopli othir wos deposit yt streffe come pe chirch wich long tyme afore wos desyrid necessari thee defence faith myghtiest eu er wos rich gret iugge edefied tounys wallis stretis distroyd herises moch good thurgh nobull prince sygmunde gadred moch monay holy land geten ayen bot deth come oppon lettid made coucell afore deth mater ther decessed ugeni wos aft er martin xvij yere eugeny wos chosen pesablie deth martin man dowtid bot wos bot shortly wos expulsit rome wos fled nakid also wos cited councell basiliens deposit bothe chargid ayen began thee striffe wich stode deth tho fauoured said worthy moch louyng co trari said tho yt wer ayens bot sum eu er wos hee takyn dignite vpo hi fore wos gret abstenes good fame yt aft er leue thee iugemet god circa annum domini miiijcxiij kyng henri thee fifth wos kyng henris sone nd deth kyng henri iiij regned kyng henri sone borne monmouth wale worthy kyng gracious man gret conquerour thee frist yere regne gret loue goodnesse sent freris langely ther fad er berie kyng richard secud let take body erth yen bring westmynster riall chare pand margeri iurdmain wos brent smythfeld palso yere wos gret fray london flete strete nyghtis tyme bytwen men court men london diu er se men slayn sum hurt herbotell chief causer misgou er naunce aft er erle salisberi comyng london wos encountred blureheth lord awdeley moch othir pepull ordeyned distroy hauyng knawlech shuld met wos accomponied two sonny sir thomas sir iohn neuill gret feliship good men pand faught gedres wher therle salisberi whan feld lord awdeley wos slayn moy gentilmen chesshire moch pepull hurt therles two sonny wer hurt goyng homward afterward wer taken chestre quemes menye pafter calixt pius wos pope chosin yere mcccc lviij wos called fore eneas eloquent man poete laureate embassatour emprours fore tyme wrote coucell basilie nobull traittie auctorite palso canonised sent katherine senys pope ordined gret indulgens pardon wold go ayenst turke wrote epistle gret turke exorting becum cristyn end ordined passage ayenst thee turke ankone wich moch pepull drew tie cristyndo wich pepull sent mony home ayen thei suffised anone aft er died said place ankone yere lord mcccclxiiij xiiij day august phow andrew trollop soudiours calais forsoke ye duke yorke ther mastir therle warwik west cuntre duke yorke erles warwike salisbiri saw gou er naunce reame stode quene hir councell gret prince ye land wer callid councell set te onli bot wos said thurgh reame tho said lordis shuld destroyed vtterli openli shewed bloreheth wold haue slayn erle salisberi pthan thei sauacion ther lyues also ye comyn well reame thoght remedie thes thyng assembled gedre moch pepull toke feld thee west cuntre wich erle warwike come calais wt mony thold soudgers andrew trowlop othir who wisedom moch trusted pand whan thus assembled made ther feld king sent comissions priue seal vn lordis reame cum await ther best defensable aray eu er man come wise kyng wos stronger moch pepull duke yorke erles warwik salisberi noted eu er lord englond time durst disobey quene rewled peasibly done kyng wich wos good simple innocent man pand kyng wos comen place wher wer duke yorke feliship made ther felde strongest wise purposid verely haue byden haue foughten nyght andrew trollop old soudiours calais gret feliship sodenly deted ye dukis host went streght vn kynges feld ther wer ressaued ioyously knew thentent othir lordis also man er ther feldis pand duke york othir lordis seyng dissaued toke coucell shortely nyght detid fro thee feld leuyng behynd parti ther pepull kepe feld till thee morn pthen duke yorke secund son detid thurgh wale toward irland leuyng eldest son erle march erles warwik salusberi wich rode ged er wt iij iiij son streght deuenshire ther bi help ayde denham squier wich gate ship wich cost ccxx noble thee ship sailed then garnesey ther refresshid then sailed calais wher wer resaued castell postren toune wist duke yorke toke shippyng walis sailed ouer irland wher wos well resayued phow therles march warwik salisberi entrid calais therle warwik went irland kyng henri beyng host feld knowyng soden deting morne fonde none ye felde said lordis sent owt hast men folowe pursue aft er take met god wold kyng went ludlowe dispoiled castell toune sent duches yorke hir child lady bokyngham hir sustre wher wos kepid long tyme pand forthwith kyng ordeyned duke somersete capitayn calais thes othir lordis deted afore said wer clamid rebellis gret traytours pthen thee duke somerset oke soudiours deted fro feld made redy ye hast go calais take pocession office whan come fond therle warwike therin capitain therles march salisberi also landid scale went guisnes ther wos resaued fortoned sum tho shippis come ou er come calais hauen ther fre shipmen ought fauour therle warwike duke somerset wich shippis wer takin diu er se ienyn finkhill iohn felow kailles purser wich wer behedid sone aft er calais pand aft er come men daly ou er see thies lordis calais began wax stronger stronger borowed moch good staple pand othir side duke somersete beyng guysnes gat pepull wich come scarmusshed calais calais wiche endurid mony dayes thus scarmusshyng moch pepull dayly come ouer vn thes lordis pthan tyme avise counsell lordis calais sent ou er mast er denham gret feliship sandwich wich toke toune theri lord riu er lord scalis son toke moi shippis haue brought calais wich shippis mony marinere ther fre come calais ser ue erle warwike pand aft er erle werwike thauys lordis toke shippis mannyd well sailed self irland speke duke yorke take avise shuld entre englod ayen pand ther done erandis returned ayen toward calais brought modre countesse salisberi pand comyng west cuntre vpon se duke excestre amirell englond beyng grace due accompanied mony shippis met therle warwik flete faught substance pepull beyng duke excestre ought bettir fauour erle warwike tha deted come calais saufte blissid god pthen kyng councell seyng thes lordis ad getin tho shippis fro sandwich takyn lord riuers son ordined garnyson sandwich abide kepe toune made moutford capitayn toue man ne vitaill ne marchand shuld go flaudres shuld go calais pthen calais seyng made master denha mony othir go sandwych assailed toue water lond gat brought moutford ther capitayn ou er se rysebanke ther smoti hys hede yit dayly men com ou er tie englond phow erles march warwike salisberi ent er id englond feld northamton wher diu er se lordis wer slayn aft er fore said erles march warwik salisberi come ouer dou er moch pepull landid cuntre drew come londo armed pand let lordis kynges councell know treuth also ther entent assembled told yt entendit harme vn kyng parson sauf thei wold put son wer deted fro londo gret puissaunce toward northamton wher kyng accompanied mony lordis made strong feld wyth toune ther party met wos foughten grete bataill wich bataill wer slayn duke bokyngham erle shrowesberi viscounte beamond lord egremond mony knyghtis squiers othir also kig self wos taken feld aft er ward brought london pand anone wos parlament westmynstre wich parlament duke yorke come irland erle rutland ridyng gret feliship palais westmynstre toke kynges palais come parlament chambre ther toke kynges place clamed crouned propre enheritaunce right cast forth writig titell also wos rightfull heir wherfore moch conclusion appointed cludid kyng henri shold regne kyng naturall life moch kyng long wos possessid hys deth duke yorke shuld kyng heiris kyng aft er forthwith shuld clamed heire apparaunt shuld also protectour regent englond kynges life wt mony othir thyngis ordeyned parlament yf kyng henri life went oppoynttement ony article concludid said parlament shuld deposid duke shuld take croune kyng wich thyng wer enacted auctorite said parlament att wich parlament comunes reame beyng assembled comune hous comonyng treating vpo titell said duke yorke sodenli fell doun croune wich honge middes said hous wich frayter abbey westmynstre wich taken dige token regne kyng henri endid also croune wich stode hyghest toure stepull ye castell dou er fell doue yere phow noble duke yorke wos slayn feld wakefeld secund iourney sent albons quene prince moch o quene wt ye prince hir son northcuntre absent hir kyng wold obeye thynges wos concludid parlament ordeyned duke yorke protectour shuld go northward bring quene subdue suche wold obeye wyth wet erle salisberi sir thomas neuill sone moche pepull wakefeld cristemasse weke wer ou er throwen slayn lordis quenis partie wit duke yorke wos slayn erle rutland sir thomas neuill mony mo therle salisburi wos takyn othir iohn harow london captayn rewlar foot men hanson hull wich wer brought pou fret ther aft er behedid ther hedis senten yorke set vpon yatis pand thus wos nobull prince slayn duke yorke who soule cristyn soules god haue mercy tyme therle marche beig shrowsberi hering deth fad er desired assistence ayde toue avege fad er deth pand then went wale wher candilmase aft er bataill mortimer crosse ayenst therles penbroke wylshire wher therle march victorie quene wyth tho lordis north aft er distress slayn thee duke yo ke feliship com southward gret multitude puissaunce pepull cum kig defete conclusion ben taken parlament ayens who commyng duke norfolke erle warwik wyth moch papull ordinaunce went sent albons sad kyng henri wyth ther encountred gedre wyse faught duke norffolke erle warwyke wyth mony othir ther partie fled lost iourney wher kyng henri taken quene wyth prince edward son wych two geten feld pthen quene hir pertie beyng ther aboue sent anone london wych wos askiswedineday first day lente vitaill wych mayre ordined thauys alderman certayn cartis laden vitaill shuld sent seint albons vn pand tho cartis come crepylgate comunes cite keped gate token vitaillis cartis wold suffre passe pthen wer th certayn alderman comuners appoyntid go vn barnet speke wyth quenes counsell entreyt northerin men shuld sent home cuntre ayen cite london dred sore robbed despoyled yf comen pand thus trayte tydynges comen erle warwike met wyth thee erle marche cottyswold comyng walis wyth gret menye walsshmen wer commyng vn londonward panone thes tidyng wer knowe th tray te broken ye kyng quene prince thee othir lordis departid seint albons northward wyth pepull yit departid then hedid lord bonuyle sir thomas kiriell wich wer taken iourney done shroftewisday pthen duchis yorke beyng london hering losse feld nt albonis sent ou er se hir two yong sonny george richard wich went vtrecht pand ph lip malpas rich marchant lodo thomas vaghan squier mastir willm hatteclif mony othir fering comyng quene londo toke ship andwarp haue gone zeland coost wer taken colompne franshma ship toke prison er brought fraunce wher paied gret good ransum ther wos moch good rich ship pof deposiocion kyng henri sext kyng edward fourth toke possession bataill palmeson ay wos crouned whan erle march erle warwike mette gedres cotiswold continente conclud go vn london sent word anone vn maire cite shuld cum anane cite glad comyng hopyng thauys lordis spirituall temperall beyng londo erle march edward thee grace god oldest sun richard duke yorke rightfull heire next enheritour fad er ye iiij day march ye yer lord mcccclix toke possessio reame englod westmi ster gret hall aft er chirch abbey offerd king wt septre royall lordis spirituall teall homage obeyssauce ther soferayn liege lord kyng forthwith wos clamid thurgh cite kyng edward fourth name anone aft er kyng rood rii astate northward wt lordis subdue subiectis yt tyme beyng north avenge fadres deth pand palme sonday aft er gret bataill northcuntre place called towton fer yorke wher help god gat thee feld victorie wher wer slayn adu er saries xxx thousand men mo wos said wer ther pin wich bataill wos slayn erle northumberland lord clifford sir iohn neuill erle westmerlandis brother andrew trollop mony knyghtis squiers pthen kyng henri bene kyng beyng quene prince yorke hering losse feld moch peple slam ou er throwen anone forthwith detid thre wt ye duke sumerset lord roos othir toward scotland pand thee next day kyng edward armye entrid yorke wos ther proclamed kig obeyed ought mair ald er men comuns sworen lege men taried north northcuntre turned returned southward leuyng behynd therle warwike tho tie kepe gou er ne yt cuntre pand mydsomer aft er thee yere lord mcccclx thee frist yere regne wos crouned westmynstre anoynted kyng englod hauyng possession thee reame calixtus thee thrid wos pope nicholas iij yere v monethis calixt hold man whe chosen pope wos continually seke ne myght fulfill desire wich entendit ayens misbeleuyng turki deth come vpon wos chosin yere lord mcccclv died sext day ye wich made fyguracion also canonised seint vincent frere precher pand ther wos gret reformacion many monesteries diu er se party world theis reformacios wer made mony time almost none abode returned ayen wer fore succession tyme aft er deth thee worshipfull fadris pthe fest transfiguracion wos ordined calixt ye yeft grace meruel victorie done ayens turke hugarie sent sextis day mcccclvij ther meruelus victorie yeuen cristyn men hungri ayenst gret turke ther lost mony man fled shamfully drede enmys man folowid bot alone hande god ferid turke host sent calixtis day sent iohan de capestrano ther seyn present uokid thee pepull wer ferd folow tho misbeleuyng turki ther grot vengeauns turki saied ther wos gret nombre knyghtis foloed vn nethis durst loke bacward therfore flede leften ther tresour hynd wer holy angellis caused fle nota printerys bokis wer tyme mightely multeplied maguncie thurgh world thei began frist ther held craftis time mony men began sotell craftis suyfter euer wer fore pius secund wos pope aft er calixt vi yere pi wos chosin yer lord miiij hondrith lviij called eneas eloquent man gret oretor laurittit poet fore wos emprour embassatour cou sell basilien wrot nobull tretis thee auctorite thee man desirid haue passage thee turke mony man er tres com rome yaf blissig sent hom ayen thay wer sufficent turki host anone aft er decessid paulus venicion wos pope pius vij yere paule wos chosin yere lord ihu crist iiij hondreth lxiiij anone aloyed fest presentaciau lady pius man wos tought man rightwisenesse saied wos better make thynges kepe stedfastli tha make mony sone reuoke made gret palais sent markes decessed endid yere lord ihesu crist miiijclxxi pleodiu ye land luke wos appressid wt mony tribulacions yere lord ihesu crist thousand iiij hondreth lxviij vtterly wos destroyed bi caro lum duke burgoyn ye wich weddid dame margaret sustre kyng edward myghti fourth englond palso duke karolus entred land geldyr conquerid holy pthe yere grace also wos changed bi pope paule fauour mannys soule xxv yere vn xxv cursednesse haboundid sore grace haboundid also sore sixtus iiij ianuens frere minore wos pope paule yit makyng boke man wos generall order thee frere minoris wos cardinale wos chosin yere lord god miiij hondreth lxxi wos called afore frauncisc de sanona good fame vertues wos chosin cardinall without knaulech till wos made yere wos chosen pope turke taken cristen men ij empiris iiij kyngdoms xx uyncis tow hondreth cite destroyed men woman nombre yt meued pope yt shuld
